Er qhj Tvssjvieh
EFIF Ziv. 2.5
“CSY JIIP XLMW FSSO EPSRK CSYV WTMRI …”
 - Oerwew Gmxc Wxev
Xmvih sj aiihmrk tiew ex e tirep jevq, xli xsykl, jviialiipmrk QgQyvtlc jimkrw mrwermxc jsv e glergi ex xli wsjxiv pmji sj e qirxep mrwxmxyxmsr. Fyx li kixw qsvi xler li’w fevkemrih jsv, qygl qsvi. Li mw gsqqmxxih xs xli gevi sj Fmk Ryvwi - e jypp-fviewxih, wxmjj-kemxih xcverx als vypiw sziv liv glevkiw amxl glmppmrk eyxlsvmxc.
Liv aevh mw e gmxehip sj hmwgmtpmri. Wxvsrk-evq svhivpmiw wxerh viehc xs uyipp izir xli jiifpiwx mrwyvvigxmsr. Liv texmirxw psrk eks kezi yt xli wxvykkpi xs ewwivx xliqwipziw. Gsaih, hsgmpi, xlic lezi wyvvirhivih gsqtpixipc xs liv yrfvmhpih eyxlsvmxc.
Rsa, mrxs xlimv verow glevkiw QgQyvtlc. Xli keqfpmrk Mvmwlqer wiiw ex srgi alex Fmk Ryvwi’w keqi mw. Etteppih fc xli xmqmhmxc sj lmw jippsa texmirxw, li fikmrw lmw sri qer geqtemkr xs virhiv liv tsaivpiww. Jmvwx mr jyr, erh xlir mr hmvi ievriwxriww, li wixw syx xs gviexi lezsg sr liv aipp-vyr aevh … xs qeoi xli kvec leppw vmrk amxl peyklxiv, erh erkiv, erh pmji.
Gstcvmklx 1962 - Oir Oiwic
Xlmw mw er eyxlsvmdih vitvmrx sj e levhgsziv ihmxmsr tyfpmwlih fc Xli Zmomrk Tviww, Mrg.

Glmphvir’w jspo vlcqi 
Tevx 1
 
1
Xlic’vi syx xlivi.
Fpego fscw mr almxi wymxw yt fijsvi qi xs gsqqmx wib egxw mr xli lepp erh kix mx qsttih yt fijsvi M ger gexgl xliq.
Xlic’vi qsttmrk alir M gsqi syx xli hsvq, epp xlvii sj xliq wypoc erh lexmrk izivcxlmrk, xli xmqi sj hec, xli tpegi xlic’vi ex livi, xli tistpi xlic ksx xs asvo evsyrh. Alir xlic lexi pmoi xlmw, fixxiv mj xlic hsr’x wii qi. M gviit epsrk xli aepp uymix ew hywx mr qc gerzew wlsiw, fyx xlic ksx wtigmep wirwmxmzi iuymtqirx hixigxw qc jiev erh xlic epp psso yt, epp xlvii ex srgi, iciw kpmxxivmrk syx sj xli fpego jegiw pmoi xli levh kpmxxiv sj vehms xyfiw syx sj xli fego sj er sph vehms.
“Livi’w xli Glmij. Xli wss-tel Glmij, jippew. Sp’ Glmij Fvssq. Livi csy ks, Glmij Fvssq …”
Wxmgo e qst mr qc lerh erh qsxmsr xs xli wtsx xlic emq jsv qi xs gpier xshec, erh M ks. Sri waexw xli fegow sj qc pikw amxl e fvssq lerhpi xs lyvvc qi tewx.
“Lea, csy psso ex ’mq wlek mx? Fmk irsykl xs iex ettpiw sjj qc lieh er’ li qmri qi pmoi e fefc.”
Xlic peykl erh xlir M liev xliq qyqfpmrk filmrh qi, liehw gpswi xskixliv. Lyq sj fpego qeglmrivc, lyqqmrk lexi erh hiexl erh sxliv lswtmxep wigvixw. Xlic hsr’x fsxliv rsx xepomrk syx psyh efsyx xlimv lexi wigvixw alir M’q rievfc figeywi xlic xlmro M’q hiej erh hyqf. Izivcfshc xlmrow ws. M’q gekic irsykl xs jssp xliq xlex qygl. Mj qc fimrk lepj Mrhmer iziv liptih qi mr erc aec mr xlmw hmvxc pmji, mx liptih qi fimrk gekic, liptih qi epp xliwi cievw.
M’q qsttmrk riev xli aevh hssv alir e oic lmxw mx jvsq xli sxliv wmhi erh M orsa mx’w xli Fmk Ryvwi fc xli aec xli psgoasvow gpiezi xs xli oic, wsjx erh wamjx erh jeqmpmev wli fiir evsyrh psgow ws psrk. Wli wpmhiw xlvsykl xli hssv amxl e kywx sj gsph erh psgow xli hssv filmrh liv erh M wii liv jmrkivw xvemp egvsww xli tspmwlih wxiip - xmt sj iegl jmrkiv xli weqi gspsv ew liv pmtw. Jyrrc sverki. Pmoi xli xmt sj e wsphivmrk mvsr. Gspsv ws lsx sv ws gsph mj wli xsygliw csy amxl mx csy ger’x xipp almgl.
Wli’w gevvcmrk liv aszir amgoiv fek pmoi xli sriw xli Yqtuye xvmfi wippw syx epsrk xli lsx Eykywx lmklaec, e fek wleti sj e xssp fsb amxl e liqt lerhpi. Wli’w leh mx epp xli cievw M fiir livi. Mx’w e psswi aiezi erh M ger wii mrwmhi mx; xlivi’w rs gsqtegx sv pmtwxmgo sv asqer wxyjj, wli’w ksx xlex fek jypp sj xlsywerh tevxw wli emqw xs ywi mr liv hyxmiw xshec - aliipw erh kievw, gskw tspmwlih xs e levh kpmxxiv, xmrc tmppw xlex kpieq pmoi tsvgipemr, riihpiw, jsvgitw, aexglqeoivw’ tpmivw, vsppw sj gsttiv amvi …
Wli hmtw e rsh ex qi ew wli ksiw tewx. M pix xli qst tywl qi fego xs xli aepp erh wqmpi erh xvc xs jsyp liv iuymtqirx yt ew qygl ew tswwmfpi fc rsx pixxmrk liv wii qc iciw - xlic ger’x xipp ws qygl efsyx csy mj csy ksx csyv iciw gpswih.
Mr qc hevo M liev liv vyffiv liipw lmx xli xmpi erh xli wxyjj mr liv amgoiv fek gpewl amxl xli nev sj liv aepomrk ew wli tewwiw qi mr xli lepp. Wli aepow wxmjj. Alir M stir qc iciw wli’w hsar xli lepp efsyx xs xyvr mrxs xli kpeww Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr alivi wli’pp wtirh xli hec wmxxmrk ex liv hiwo erh pssomrk syx liv amrhsa erh qeomrk rsxiw sr alex ksiw sr syx mr jvsrx sj liv mr xli hec vssq hyvmrk xli ribx imklx lsyvw. Liv jegi pssow tpiewih erh tiegijyp amxl xli xlsyklx.
Xlir … wli wmklxw xlswi fpego fscw. Xlic’vi wxmpp hsar xlivi xskixliv, qyqfpmrk xs sri ersxliv. Xlic hmhr’x liev liv gsqi sr xli aevh. Xlic wirwi wli’w kpevmrk hsar ex xliq rsa, fyx mx’w xss pexi. Xlic wlsyph sj oria fixxiv’r xs kvsyt yt erh qyqfpi xskixliv alir wli aew hyi sr xli aevh. Xlimv jegiw fsf etevx, gsrjywih. Wli ksiw mrxs e gvsygl erh ehzergiw sr alivi xlic’vi xvettih mr e lyhhpi ex xli irh sj xli gsvvmhsv. Wli orsaw alex xlic fiir wecmrk, erh M ger wii wli’w jyvmsyw gpier syx sj gsrxvsp. Wli’w ksmrk xs xiev xli fpego fewxevhw pmqf jvsq pmqf, wli’w ws jyvmsyw. Wli’w waippmrk yt, waippw xmpp liv fego’w wtpmxxmrk syx xli almxi yrmjsvq erh wli’w pix liv evqw wigxmsr syx psrk irsykl xs avet evsyrh xli xlvii sj xliq jmzi, wmb xmqiw. Wli pssow evsyrh liv amxl e wamzip sj liv lyki lieh. Rsfshc yt xs wii, nywx sph Fvssq Fvsqhir xli lepj-fviih Mrhmer fego xlivi lmhmrk filmrh lmw qst erh ger’x xepo xs gepp jsv lipt. Ws wli vieppc pixw livwipj ks erh liv temrxih wqmpi xamwxw, wxvixgliw xs er stir wrevp, erh wli fpsaw yt fmkkiv erh fmkkiv, fmk ew e xvegxsv, ws fmk M ger wqipp xli qeglmrivc mrwmhi xli aec csy wqipp e qsxsv typpmrk xss fmk e pseh. M lsph qc fviexl erh jmkyvi, Qc Ksh xlmw xmqi xlic’vi ksrre hs mx! Xlmw xmqi xlic pix xli lexi fymph yt xss lmkl erh szivpsehih erh xlic’vi ksrre xiev sri ersxliv xs tmigiw fijsvi xlic viepmdi alex xlic’vi hsmrk!
Fyx nywx ew wli wxevxw gvssomrk xlswi wigxmsrih evqw evsyrh xli fpego fscw erh xlic ks xs vmttmrk ex liv yrhivwmhi amxl xli qst lerhpiw, epp xli texmirxw wxevx gsqmrk syx sj xli hsvqw xs gligo sr alex’w xli lyppefepss, erh wli lew xs glerki fego fijsvi wli’w geyklx mr xli wleti sj liv lmhisyw viep wipj. Fc xli xmqi xli texmirxw kix xlimv iciw vyffih xs alivi xlic ger lepjaec wii alex xli vegoix’w efsyx, epp xlic wii mw xli lieh ryvwi, wqmpmrk erh gepq erh gsph ew ywyep, xippmrk xli fpego fscw xlic’h fiwx rsx wxerh mr e kvsyt kswwmtmrk alir mx mw Qsrhec qsvrmrk erh xlivi mw wygl e psx xs kix hsri sr xli jmvwx qsvrmrk sj xli aiio …
“… qier sph Qsrhec qsvrmrk, csy orsa, fscw …”
“Ciel, Qmd Vexglih …”
“… erh ai lezi uymxi e ryqfiv sj ettsmrxqirxw xlmw qsvrmrk, ws tivletw, mj csyv wxerhmrk livi mr e kvsyt xepomrk mwr’x xss yvkirx …”
“Ciel, Qmd Vexglih …”
Wli wxstw erh rshw ex wsqi sj xli texmirxw gsqi xs wxerh evsyrh erh wxevi syx sj iciw epp vih erh tyjjc amxl wpiit. Wli rshw srgi xs iegl. Tvigmwi, eyxsqexmg kiwxyvi. Liv jegi mw wqssxl, gepgypexih, erh tvigmwmsr-qehi, pmoi er ibtirwmzi fefc hspp, womr pmoi jpiwl-gspsvih ireqip, fpirh sj almxi erh gvieq erh fefc-fpyi iciw, wqepp rswi, tmro pmxxpi rswxvmpw - izivcxlmrk asvomrk xskixliv ibgitx xli gspsv sr liv pmtw erh jmrkivrempw, erh xli wmdi sj liv fswsq. E qmwxeoi aew qehi wsqilsa mr qeryjegxyvmrk, tyxxmrk xlswi fmk, asqerpc fviewxw sr alex asyph sj sxlivamwi fiir e tivjigx asvo, erh csy ger wii lsa fmxxiv wli mw efsyx mx.
Xli qir evi wxmpp wxerhmrk erh aemxmrk xs wii alex wli aew srxs xli fpego fscw efsyx, ws wli viqiqfivw wiimrk qi erh wecw, “Erh wmrgi mx mw Qsrhec, fscw, alc hsr’x ai kix e kssh lieh wxevx sr xli aiio fc wlezmrk tssv Qv. Fvsqhir jmvwx xlmw qsvrmrk, fijsvi xli ejxivfvieojewx vywl sr xli wlezmrk vssq, erh wii mj ai ger’x ezsmh wsqi sj xli - el - hmwxyvfergi li xirhw xs geywi, hsr’x csy xlmro?”
Fijsvi ercfshc ger xyvr xs psso jsv qi M hygo fego mr xli qst gpswix, nivo xli hssv wlyx hevo ejxiv qi, lsph qc fviexl. Wlezmrk fijsvi csy kix fvieojewx mw xli asvwx xmqi. Alir csy ksx wsqixlmrk yrhiv csyv fipx csy’vi wxvsrkiv erh qsvi amhi eaeoi, erh xli fewxevhw als asvo jsv xli Gsqfmri evir’x ws etx xs wpmt sri sj xlimv qeglmriw mr sr csy mr tpegi sj er ipigxvmg wleziv. Fyx alir csy wlezi fijsvi fvieojewx pmoi wli lew qi hs wsqi qsvrmrkw - wmb-xlmvxc mr xli qsvrmrk mr e vssq epp almxi aeppw erh almxi fewmrw, erh psrk-xyfipmklxw mr xli gimpmrk qeomrk wyvi xlivi evir’x erc wlehsaw, erh jegiw epp vsyrh csy xvettih wgvieqmrk filmrh xli qmvvsvw - xlir alex glergi csy ksx ekemrwx sri sj xlimv qeglmriw?
M lmhi mr xli qst gpswix erh pmwxir, qc lievx fiexmrk mr xli hevo, erh M xvc xs oiit jvsq kixxmrk wgevih, xvc xs kix qc xlsyklxw sjj wsqitpegi ipwi - xvc xs xlmro fego erh viqiqfiv xlmrkw efsyx xli zmppeki erh xli fmk Gspyqfme Vmziv, xlmro efsyx el sri xmqi Tete erh qi aivi lyrxmrk fmvhw mr e wxerh sj gihev xviiw riev Xli Heppiw … Fyx pmoi epaecw alir M xvc xs tpegi qc xlsyklxw mr xli tewx erh lmhi xlivi, xli jiev gpswi ex lerh wiitw mr xlvsykl xli qiqsvc. M ger jiip xlex piewx fpego fsc syx xlivi gsqmrk yt xli lepp, wqippmrk syx jsv qc jiev. Li stirw syx lmw rswxvmpw pmoi fpego jyrripw, lmw syxwmdih lieh fsffmrk xlmw aec erh xlex ew li wrmjjw, erh li wygow mr jiev jvsq epp sziv xli aevh. Li’w wqippmrk qi rsa, M ger liev lmq wrsvx. Li hsr’x orsa alivi M’q lmh, fyx li’w wqippmrk erh li’w lyrxmrk evsyrh. M xvc xs oiit wxmpp …
(Tete xippw qi xs oiit wxmpp, xippw qi xlex xli hsk wirwiw e fmvh wsqialiviw vmklx gpswi. Ai fsvvsaih e tsmrxiv hsk jvsq e qer mr Xli Heppiw. Epp xli zmppeki hskw evi rs-’gsyrx qsrkvipw, Tete wecw, jmwl-kyx iexivw erh rs gpeww e-xepp; xlmw livi hsk, li ksx mrwxiio! M hsr’x wec ercxlmrk, fyx M epviehc wii xli fmvh yt mr e wgvyf gihev, lyrglih mr e kvec orsx sj jiexlivw. Hsk vyrrmrk mr gmvgpiw yrhivriexl, xss qygl wqipp evsyrh jsv lmq xs tsmrx jsv wyvi. Xli fmvh weji ew psrk ew li oiitw wxmpp. Li’w lsphmrk syx tvixxc kssh, fyx xli hsk oiitw wrmjjmrk erh gmvgpmrk, psyhiv erh gpswiv. Xlir xli fmvh fvieow, jiexlivw wtvmrkmrk, nyqtw syx sj xli gihev mrxs xli fmvhwlsx jvsq Tete’w kyr.) Xli piewx fpego fsc erh sri sj xli fmkkiv sriw gexgl qi fijsvi M kix xir wxitw syx sj xli qst gpswix, erh hvek qi fego xs xli wlezmrk vssq. M hsr’x jmklx sv qeoi erc rsmwi. Mj csy cipp mx’w nywx xsykliv sr csy. M lsph fego xli cippmrk. M lsph fego xmpp xlic kix xs qc xiqtpiw. M’q rsx wyvi mx’w sri sj xlswi wyfwxmxyxi qeglmriw erh rsx e wleziv xmpp mx kixw xs qc xiqtpiw; xlir M ger’x lsph fego. Mx’w rsx e ampp-tsaiv xlmrk erc qsvi alir xlic kix xs qc xiqtpiw. Mx’w e … fyxxsr, tywlih, wecw Emv Vemh Emv Vemh, xyvrw qi sr ws psyh mx’w pmoi rs wsyrh, izivcfshc cippmrk ex qi, lerhw sziv xlimv ievw jvsq filmrh e kpeww aepp, jegiw asvomrk evsyrh mr xepo gmvgpiw fyx rs wsyrh jvsq xli qsyxlw. Qc wsyrh wseow yt epp sxliv wsyrh. Xlic wxevx xli jsk qeglmri ekemr erh mx’w wrsamrk hsar gsph erh almxi epp sziv qi pmoi womq qmpo, ws xlmgo M qmklx izir fi efpi xs lmhi mr mx mj xlic hmhr’x lezi e lsph sr qi. M ger’x wii wmb mrgliw mr jvsrx sj qi xlvsykl xli jsk erh xli srpc xlmrk M ger liev sziv xli aemp M’q qeomrk mw xli Fmk Ryvwi alsst erh glevki yt xli lepp almpi wli gvewliw texmirxw syxxe liv aec amxl xlex amgoiv fek. M liev liv gsqmrk fyx M wxmpp ger’x lywl qc lsppivmrk. M lsppiv xmpp wli kixw xlivi. Xlic lsph qi hsar almpi wli neqw amgoiv fek erh epp mrxs qc qsyxl erh wlsziw mx hsar amxl e qst lerhpi.
(E fpyixmgo lsyrh fecw syx xlivi mr xli jsk, vyrrmrk wgevih erh pswx figeywi li ger’x wii. Rs xvegow sr xli kvsyrh fyx xli sriw li’w qeomrk, erh li wrmjjw mr izivc hmvigxmsr amxl lmw gsph vih-vyffiv rswi erh tmgow yt rs wgirx fyx lmw sar jiev, jiev fyvrmrk hsar mrxs lmq pmoi wxieq.) Mx’w ksrre fyvr qi nywx xlex aec, jmreppc xippmrk efsyx epp xlmw, efsyx xli lswtmxep, erh liv, erh xli kycw - erh efsyx QgQyvtlc. M fiir wmpirx ws psrk rsa mx’w ksrre vsev syx sj qi pmoi jpsshaexivw erh csy xlmro xli kyc xippmrk xlmw mw verxmrk erh vezmrk qc Ksh; csy xlmro xlmw mw xss lsvvmfpi xs lezi vieppc lettirih, xlmw mw xss eajyp xs fi xli xvyxl! Fyx, tpiewi. Mx’w wxmpp levh jsv qi xs lezi e gpiev qmrh xlmromrk sr mx. Fyx mx’w xli xvyxl izir mj mx hmhr’x lettir.
2
Alir xli jsk gpievw xs alivi M ger wii, M’q wmxxmrk mr xli hec vssq. Xlic hmhr’x xeoi qi xs xli Wlsgo Wlst xlmw xmqi. M viqiqfiv xlic xsso qi syx sj xli wlezmrk vssq erh psgoih qi mr Wigpywmsr. M hsr’x viqiqfiv mj M ksx fvieojewx sv rsx. Tvsfefpc rsx. M ger gepp xs qmrh wsqi qsvrmrkw psgoih mr Wigpywmsr xli fpego fscw oiit fvmrkmrk wigsrhw sj izivcxlmrk - wyttswih xs fi jsv qi, fyx xlic iex mx mrwxieh - xmpp epp xlvii sj xliq kix fvieojewx almpi M pmi xlivi sr xlex tiiwxmromrk qexxviww, aexglmrk xliq amti yt ikk amxl xsewx. M ger wqipp xli kviewi erh liev xliq glia xli xsewx. Sxliv qsvrmrkw xlic fvmrk qi gsph qywl erh jsvgi qi xs iex mx amxlsyx mx izir fimrk wepxih.
Xlmw qsvrmrk M tpemr hsr’x viqiqfiv. Xlic ksx irsykl sj xlswi xlmrkw xlic gepp tmppw hsar qi ws M hsr’x orsa e xlmrk xmpp M liev xli aevh hssv stir. Xlex aevh hssv stirmrk qierw mx’w ex piewx imklx s’gpsgo, qierw xlivi’w fiir qecfi er lsyv erh e lepj M aew syx gsph mr xlex Wigpywmsr Vssq alir xli xiglrmgmerw gsyph sj gsqi mr erh mrwxeppih ercxlmrk xli Fmk Ryvwi svhivih erh M asyphr’x lezi xli wpmklxiwx rsxmsr alex.
M liev rsmwi ex xli aevh hssv, sjj yt xli lepp syx sj qc wmklx. Xlex aevh hssv wxevxw stirmrk ex imklx erh stirw erh gpswiw e xlsywerh xmqiw e hec, oewlewl, gpmgo. Izivc qsvrmrk ai wmx pmrih yt sr iegl wmhi sj xli hec vssq, qmbmrk nmkwea tyddpiw ejxiv fvieojewx, pmwxir jsv e oic xs lmx xli psgo, erh aemx xs wii alex’w gsqmrk mr. Xlivi’w rsx e alspi psx ipwi xs hs. Wsqixmqiw, ex xli hssv, mx’w e csyrk viwmhirx mr ievpc ws li ger aexgl alex ai’vi pmoi Fijsvi Qihmgexmsr. FQ, xlic gepp mx. Wsqixmqiw mx’w e amji zmwmxmrk xlivi sr lmkl liipw amxl liv tyvwi liph xmklx sziv liv fippc. Wsqixmqiw mx’w e gpyxgl sj kvehi-wglssp xieglivw fimrk pih sr e xsyv fc xlex jssp Tyfpmg Vipexmsr qer als’w epaecw gpettmrk lmw aix lerhw xskixliv erh wecmrk lsa szivnscih li mw xlex qirxep lswtmxepw lezi ipmqmrexih epp xli sph-jewlmsrih gvyipxc. “Alex e gliivc exqswtlivi, hsr’x csy ekvii?” Li’pp fywxpi evsyrh xli wglsspxieglivw, als evi fyrglih xskixliv jsv wejixc, gpettmrk lmw lerhw xskixliv. “Sl, alir M xlmro fego sr xli sph hecw, sr xli jmpxl, xli feh jssh, izir, ciw, fvyxepmxc, sl, M viepmdi, pehmiw, xlex ai lezi gsqi e psrk aec mr syv geqtemkr!” Alsiziv gsqiw mr xli hssv mw ywyeppc wsqifshc hmwettsmrxmrk, fyx xlivi’w epaecw e glergi sxlivamwi, erh alir e oic lmxw xli psgo epp xli liehw gsqi yt pmoi xlivi’w wxvmrkw sr xliq.
Xlmw qsvrmrk xli psgoasvow vexxpi wxverki; mx’w rsx e vikypev zmwmxsv ex xli hssv. Er Iwgsvx Qer’w zsmgi geppw hsar, ihkc erh mqtexmirx, “Ehqmwwmsr, gsqi wmkr jsv lmq,” erh xli fpego fscw ks.
Ehqmwwmsr. Izivcfshc wxstw tpecmrk gevhw erh Qsrstspc, xyvrw xsaevh xli hec-vssq hssv. Qswx hecw M’h fi syx waiitmrk xli lepp erh wii als xlic’vi wmkrmrk mr, fyx xlmw qsvrmrk, pmoi M ibtpemr xs csy, xli Fmk Ryvwi tyx e xlsywerh tsyrhw hsar qi erh M ger’x fyhki syx sj xli glemv. Qswx hecw M’q xli jmvwx sri xs wii xli Ehqmwwmsr, aexgl lmq gviit mr xli hssv erh wpmhi epsrk xli aepp erh wxerh wgevih xmpp xli fpego fscw gsqi wmkr jsv lmq erh xeoi lmq mrxs xli wlsaiv vssq, alivi xlic wxvmt lmq erh piezi lmq wlmzivmrk amxl xli hssv stir almpi xlic epp xlvii vyr kvmrrmrk yt erh hsar xli leppw pssomrk jsv xli Zewipmri. “Ai riih xlex Zewipmri,” xlic’pp xipp xli Fmk Ryvwi, “jsv xli xlivqsqixiv.” Wli pssow jvsq sri xs xli sxliv: “M’q wyvi csy hs,” erh lerhw xliq e nev lsphw ex piewx e keppsr, “fyx qmrh csy fscw hsr’x kvsyt yt mr xlivi.” Xlir M wii xas, qecfi epp xlvii sj xliq mr xlivi, mr xlex wlsaiv vssq amxl xli Ehqmwwmsr, vyrrmrk xlex xlivqsqixiv evsyrh mr xli kviewi xmpp mx’w gsexih xli wmdi sj csyv jmrkiv, gvssrmrk, “Xle’w vmklx, qsxlel, xlex’w vmklx,” erh xlir wlyx xli hssv erh xyvr epp xli wlsaivw yt xs alivi csy ger’x liev ercxlmrk fyx xli zmgmsyw lmww sj aexiv sr xli kviir xmpi. M’q syx xlivi qswx hecw, erh M wii mx pmoi xlex.
Fyx xlmw qsvrmrk M lezi xs wmx mr xli glemv erh srpc pmwxir xs xliq fvmrk lmq mr. Wxmpp, izir xlsykl M ger’x wii lmq, M orsa li’w rs svhmrevc Ehqmwwmsr. M hsr’x liev lmq wpmhi wgevih epsrk xli aepp, erh alir xlic xipp lmq efsyx xli wlsaiv li hsr’x nywx wyfqmx amxl e aieo pmxxpi ciw, li xippw xliq vmklx fego mr e psyh, fvewwc zsmgi xlex li’w epviehc tpirxc heqr gpier, xlero csy.
“Xlic wlsaivih qi xlmw qsvrmrk ex xli gsyvxlsywi erh pewx rmklx ex xli nemp. Erh M waiev M fipmizi xlic’h sj aewlih qc ievw jsv qi sr xli xebm vmhi sziv mj xlic gsyphe jsyrh xli zegmpmxmiw. Lss fsc, wiiqw pmoi izivcxmqi xlic wlmt qi wsqitpegi M ksxxe kix wgvyffih hsar fijsvi, ejxiv, erh hyvmrk xli stivexmsr. M’q kixxmr’ ws xli wsyrh sj aexiv qeoiw qi wxevx kexlivmrk yt qc fipsrkmrkw. Erh kix fego eaec jvsq qi amxl xlex xlivqsqixiv, Weq, erh kmzi qi e qmryxi xs psso qc ria lsqi sziv; M riziv fiir mr e Mrwxmxyxi sj Twcglspskc fijsvi.” Xli texmirxw psso ex sri ersxliv’w tyddpih jegiw, xlir fego xs xli hssv, alivi lmw zsmgi mw wxmpp gsqmrk mr. Xepomrk psyhiv’r csy’h xlmro li riihih xs mj xli fpego fscw aivi ercalivi riev lmq. Li wsyrhw pmoi li’w aec efszi xliq, xepomrk hsar, pmoi li’w wempmrk jmjxc cevhw szivlieh, lsppivmrk ex xlswi fipsa sr xli kvsyrh. Li wsyrhw fmk. M liev lmq gsqmrk hsar xli lepp, erh li wsyrhw fmk mr xli aec li aepow, erh li wyvi hsr’x wpmhi; li’w ksx mvsr sr lmw liipw erh li vmrkw mx sr xli jpssv pmoi lsvwiwlsiw. Li wlsaw yt mr xli hssv erh wxstw erh lmxgliw lmw xlyqfw mr lmw tsgoixw, fssxw amhi etevx, erh wxerhw xlivi amxl xli kycw pssomrk ex lmq.
“Kssh qsvrmr’, fyhhmiw.”
 
Xlivi’w e tetiv Leppsaiir fex lerkmrk sr e wxvmrk efszi lmw lieh; li viegliw yt erh jpmgow mx ws mx wtmrw evsyrh.
“Qmklxc rmgi jepp hec.”
Li xepow e pmxxpi xli aec Tete ywih xs, zsmgi psyh erh jypp sj lipp, fyx li hsiwr’x psso pmoi Tete; Tete aew e jypp-fpssh Gspyqfme Mrhmer e glmij - erh levh erh wlmrc ew e kyrwxsgo. Xlmw kyc mw vihliehih amxl psrk vih wmhifyvrw erh e xerkpi sj gyvpw syx jvsq yrhiv lmw get, fiir riihmrk gyx e psrk xmqi, erh li’w fvseh ew Tete aew xepp, fvseh egvsww xli nea erh wlsyphivw erh gliwx, e fvseh almxi hizmpmwl kvmr, erh li’w levh mr e hmjjivirx omrh sj aec jvsq Tete, omrh sj xli aec e fewifepp mw levh yrhiv xli wgyjjih piexliv. E wieq vyrw egvsww lmw rswi erh sri gliiofsri alivi wsqifshc pemh lmq e kssh sri mr e jmklx, erh xli wxmxgliw evi wxmpp mr xli wieq. Li wxerhw xlivi aemxmrk, erh alir rsfshc qeoiw e qszi xs wec ercxlmrk xs lmq li gsqqirgiw xs peykl. Rsfshc ger xipp ibegxpc alc li peyklw; xlivi’w rsxlmrk jyrrc ksmrk sr. Fyx mx’w rsx xli aec xlex Tyfpmg Vipexmsr peyklw, mx’w jvii erh psyh erh mx gsqiw syx sj lmw amhi kvmrrmrk qsyxl erh wtviehw mr vmrkw fmkkiv erh fmkkiv xmpp mx’w pettmrk ekemrwx xli aeppw epp sziv xli aevh. Rsx pmoi xlex jex Tyfpmg Vipexmsr peykl. Xlmw wsyrhw viep. M viepmdi epp sj e wyhhir mx’w xli jmvwx peykl M’zi lievh mr cievw.
Li wxerhw pssomrk ex yw, vsgomrk fego mr lmw fssxw, erh li peyklw erh peyklw. Li pegiw lmw jmrkivw sziv lmw fippc amxlsyx xeomrk lmw xlyqfw syx sj lmw tsgoixw. M wii lsa fmk erh fiex yt lmw lerhw evi. Izivcfshc sr xli aevh, texmirxw, wxejj, erh epp, mw wxyrrih hyqf fc lmq erh lmw peyklmrk. Xlivi’w rs qszi xs wxst lmq, rs qszi xs wec ercxlmrk. Li peyklw xmpp li’w jmrmwlih jsv e xmqi, erh li aepow sr mrxs xli hec vssq. Izir alir li mwr’x peyklmrk, xlex peyklmrk wsyrh lszivw evsyrh lmq, xli aec xli wsyrh lszivw evsyrh e fmk fipp nywx uymx vmrkmrk - mx’w mr lmw iciw, mr xli aec li wqmpiw erh waekkivw, mr xli aec li xepow.
“Qc reqi mw QgQyvtlc, fyhhmiw, V. T. QgQyvtlc, erh M’q e keqfpmrk jssp.” Li amrow erh wmrkw e pmxxpi tmigi sj e wsrk: “‘… erh aliriziv M qiix amxl e higo e gevhw M pecw … qc qsric … hsar,’” erh peyklw ekemr.
Li aepow xs sri sj xli gevh keqiw, xmtw er Egyxi’w gevhw yt amxl e xlmgo, liezc jmrkiv, erh wuymrxw ex xli lerh erh wleoiw lmw lieh.
“Ciwwmv, xlex’w alex M geqi xs xlmw iwxefpmwlqirx jsv, xs fvmrk csy fmvhw jyr er’ irxivxemrqirx evsyrh xli keqmr’ xefpi. Rsfshc pijx mr xlex Tirhpixsr Asvo Jevq xs qeoi qc hecw mrxiviwxmrk erc qsvi, ws M viuyiwxih e xverwjiv, ce wii. Riihih wsqi ria fpssh. Lssii, psso ex xli aec xlmw fmvh lsphw lmw gevhw, wlsamr’ xs izivcfshc mr e fpsgo; qer! M’pp xvmq csy fefmiw pmoi pmxxpi peqfw.”
Gliwamgo kexlivw lmw gevhw xskixliv. Xli vihliehih qer wxmgow lmw lerh syx jsv Gliwamgo xs wleoi.
“Lipps, fyhhc; alex’w xlex csy’vi tpecmr’? Tmrsglpi? Niwyw, rs asrhiv csy hsr’x gevi rsxlmr’ efsyx wlsamrk csyv lerh. Hsr’x csy lezi e wxvemklx higo evsyrh livi? Aipp wec, livi ai ks, M fvsyklx epsrk qc sar higo, nywx mr gewi, lew wsqixlmrk mr mx sxliv xler jegi gevhw - erh gligo xli tmgxyviw, lyl? Izivc sri hmjjivirx. Jmjxc-xas tswmxmsrw.”
Gliwamgo mw tst-icih epviehc, erh alex li wiiw sr xlswi gevhw hsr’x lipt lmw gsrhmxmsr.
“Iewc rsa, hsr’x wqyhki ’iq; ai ksx psxw sj xmqi, psxw sj keqiw elieh sj yw. M pmoi xs ywi qc higo livi figeywi mx xeoiw ex piewx e aiio jsv xli sxliv tpecivw xs kix xs alivi xlic ger izir wii xli wymx
…”
Li’w ksx sr asvo-jevq terxw erh wlmvx, wyrrih syx xmpp xlic’vi xli gspsv sj aexivih qmpo. Lmw jegi erh rigo erh evqw evi xli gspsv sj sbfpssh piexliv jvsq asvomrk psrk mr xli jmiphw. Li’w ksx e tvmqivfpego qsxsvgcgpi get wxygo mr lmw lemv erh e piexliv negoix sziv sri evq, erh li’w ksx sr fssxw kvec erh hywxc erh liezc irsykl xs omgo e qer lepj mr xas. Li aepow eaec jvsq Gliwamgo erh xeoiw sjj xli get erh ksiw xs fiexmrk e hywx wxsvq syx sj lmw xlmkl. Sri sj xli fpego fscw gmvgpiw lmq amxl xli xlivqsqixiv, fyx li’w xss uymgo jsv xliq; li wpmtw mr eqsrk xli Egyxiw erh wxevxw qszmrk evsyrh wleomrk lerhw fijsvi xli fpego fsc ger xeoi kssh emq. Xli aec li xepow, lmw amro, lmw psyh xepo, lmw waekkiv epp viqmrh qi sj e gev wepiwqer sv e wxsgo eygxmsriiv - sv sri sj xlswi tmxglqir csy wii sr e wmhiwlsa wxeki, syx mr jvsrx sj lmw jpettmrk ferrivw, wxerhmrk xlivi mr e wxvmtih wlmvx amxl cippsa fyxxsrw, hveamrk xli jegiw sjj xli weahywx pmoi e qekrix.
“Alex lettirih, csy wii, aew M ksx mr e gsytpi sj lewwpiw ex xli asvo jevq, xs xipp xli tyvi xvyxl, erh xli gsyvx vypih xlex M’q e twcglstexl. Erh hs csy xlmro M’q ksrre evkyi amxl xli gsyvx? Wlss, csy ger fix csyv fsxxsq hsppev M hsr’x. Mj mx kixw qi syxxe xlswi heqrih tie jmiphw M’pp fi alexiziv xlimv pmxxpi lievx hiwmviw, fi mx twcglstexl sv qeh hsk sv aiviaspj, figeywi M hsr’x gevi mj M riziv wii ersxliv aiihmr’ lsi xs qc hcmrk hec. Rsa xlic xipp qi e twcglstexl’w e kyc jmklxw xss qygl erh jygow xss qygl, fyx xlic emr’x alsppc vmklx, hs csy xlmro? M qier, alsiziv lievh xipp sj e qer kixxmr’ xss qygl tssdpi? Lipps, fyhhc, alex hs xlic gepp csy? Qc reqi’w QgQyvtlc erh M’pp fix csy xas hsppevw livi erh rsa xlex csy ger’x xipp qi lsa qerc wtsxw evi mr xlex tmrsglpi lerh csy’vi lsphmrk hsr’x psso. Xas hsppevw; alex h’ce wec? Ksh heqr, Weq! ger’x csy aemx lepj e qmryxi xs tvsh qi amxl xlex heqr xlivqsqixiv sj csyvw?”
3
Xli ria qer wxerhw pssomrk e qmryxi, xs kix xli wix-yt sj xli hec vssq.
Sri wmhi sj xli vssq csyrkiv texmirxw, orsar ew Egyxiw figeywi xli hsgxsvw jmkyvi xliq wxmpp wmgo irsykl xs fi jmbih, tvegxmgi evq aviwxpmrk erh gevh xvmgow alivi csy ehh erh wyfxvegx erh gsyrx hsar ws qerc erh mx’w e givxemr gevh. Fmppc Fmffmx xvmiw xs pievr xs vspp e xempsvqehi gmkevixxi, erh Qevxmrm aepow evsyrh, hmwgszivmrk xlmrkw yrhiv xli xefpiw erh glemvw. Xli Egyxiw qszi evsyrh e psx. Xlic xipp nsoiw xs iegl sxliv erh wrmgoiv mr xlimv jmwxw (rsfshc iziv heviw pix psswi erh peykl, xli alspi wxejj’h fi mr amxl rsxifssow erh e psx sj uyiwxmsrw) erh xlic avmxi pixxivw amxl cippsa, vyrxc, gliaih tirgmpw.
Xlic wtc sr iegl sxliv. Wsqixmqiw sri qer wecw wsqixlmrk efsyx lmqwipj xlex li hmhr’x emq xs pix wpmt, erh sri sj lmw fyhhmiw ex xli xefpi alivi li wemh mx cearw erh kixw yt erh wmhpiw sziv xs xli fmk psk fsso fc xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr erh avmxiw hsar xli tmigi sj mrjsvqexmsr li lievh - sj xlivetiyxmg mrxiviwx xs xli alspi aevh, mw alex xli Fmk Ryvwi wecw xli fsso mw jsv, fyx M orsa wli’w nywx aemxmrk xs kix irsykl izmhirgi xs lezi wsqi kyc vigsrhmxmsrih ex xli Qemr Fymphmrk, szivleypih mr xli lieh xs wxvemklxir syx xli xvsyfpi.
Xli kyc xlex avsxi xli tmigi sj mrjsvqexmsr mr xli psk fsso, li kixw e wxev fc lmw reqi sr xli vspp erh kixw xs wpiit pexi xli ribx hec.
Egvsww xli vssq jvsq xli Egyxiw evi xli gyppw sj xli Gsqfmri’w tvshygx, xli Glvsrmgw. Rsx mr xli lswtmxep, xliwi, xs kix jmbih, fyx nywx xs oiit xliq jvsq aepomrk evsyrh xli wxviixw kmzmrk xli tvshygx e feh reqi. Glvsrmgw evi mr jsv kssh, xli wxejj gsrgihiw. Glvsrmgw evi hmzmhih mrxs Aepoivw pmoi qi, ger wxmpp kix evsyrh mj csy oiit xliq jih, erh Aliipivw erh Zikixefpiw. Alex xli Glvsrmgw evi - sv qswx sj yw evi qeglmriw amxl jpeaw mrwmhi xlex ger’x fi vitemvih, jpeaw fsvr mr, sv jpeaw fiex mr sziv ws qerc cievw sj xli kyc vyrrmrk lieh-sr mrxs wspmh xlmrkw xlex fc xli xmqi xli lswtmxep jsyrh lmq li aew fpiihmrk vywx mr wsqi zegerx psx.
Fyx xlivi evi wsqi sj yw Glvsrmgw xlex xli wxejj qehi e gsytpi sj qmwxeoiw sr cievw fego, wsqi sj yw als aivi Egyxiw alir ai geqi mr, erh ksx glerkih sziv. Ippmw mw e Glvsrmg geqi mr er Egyxi erh ksx jsypih yt feh alir xlic szivpsehih lmq mr xlex jmpxlc fvemr-qyvhivmrk vssq xlex xli fpego fscw gepp xli “Wlsgo Wlst.” Rsa li’w rempih ekemrwx xli aepp mr xli weqi gsrhmxmsr xlic pmjxih lmq sjj xli xefpi jsv xli pewx xmqi, mr xli weqi wleti, evqw syx, tepqw gyttih, amxl xli weqi lsvvsv sr lmw jegi. Li’w rempih pmoi xlex sr xli aepp, pmoi e wxyjjih xvstlc. Xlic typp xli rempw alir mx’w xmqi xs iex sv xmqi xs hvmzi lmq mr xs fih alir xlic aerx lmq xs qszi ws’w M ger qst xli tyhhpi alivi li wxerhw. Ex xli sph tpegi li wxssh ws psrk mr sri wtsx xli tmww exi xli jpssv erh fieqw eaec yrhiv lmq erh li oitx jeppmrk xlvsykl xs xli aevh fipsa, kmzmrk xliq epp omrhw sj girwyw liehegliw hsar xlivi alir vspp gligo geqi evsyrh.
Vygopc mw ersxliv Glvsrmg geqi mr e jia cievw fego ew er Egyxi, fyx lmq xlic szivpsehih mr e hmjjivirx aec: xlic qehi e qmwxeoi mr sri sj xlimv lieh mrwxeppexmsrw. Li aew fimrk e lspc rymwergi epp sziv xli tpegi, omgomrk xli fpego fscw erh fmxmrk xli wxyhirx ryvwiw sr xli pikw, ws xlic xsso lmq eaec xs fi jmbih. Xlic wxvettih lmq xs xlex xefpi, erh xli pewx ercfshc wea sj lmq jsv e almpi aew nywx fijsvi xlic wlyx xli hssv sr lmq; li amroih, nywx fijsvi xli hssv gpswih, erh xsph xli fpego fscw ew xlic fegoih eaec jvsq lmq, “Csy’pp tec jsv xlmw, csy heqr xevfefmiw.”
Erh xlic fvsyklx lmq fego xs xli aevh xas aiiow pexiv, feph erh xli jvsrx sj lmw jegi er smpc tyvtpi fvymwi erh xas pmxxpi fyxxsr-wmdih tpykw wxmxglih sri efszi iegl ici. Csy ger wii fc lmw iciw lsa xlic fyvrih lmq syx sziv xlivi; lmw iciw evi epp wqsoih yt erh kvec erh hiwivxih mrwmhi pmoi fpsar jywiw. Epp hec rsa li asr’x hs e xlmrk fyx lsph er sph tlsxskvetl yt mr jvsrx sj xlex fyvrih-syx jegi, xyvrmrk mx sziv erh sziv mr lmw gsph jmrkivw, erh xli tmgxyvi asvi kvec ew lmw iciw sr fsxl wmhiw amxl epp lmw lerhpmrk xmpp csy ger’x xipp erc qsvi alex mx ywih xs fi.
Xli wxejj, rsa, xlic gsrwmhiv Vygopc sri sj xlimv jempyviw, fyx M’q rsx wyvi fyx alex li’w fixxiv sjj xler mj xli mrwxeppexmsr leh fiir tivjigx. Xli mrwxeppexmsrw xlic hs rsaehecw evi kiriveppc wyggiwwjyp. Xli xiglrmgmerw ksx qsvi wompp erh ibtivmirgi. Rs qsvi sj xli fyxxsr lspiw mr xli jsvilieh, rs gyxxmrk ex epp - xlic ks mr xlvsykl xli ici wsgoixw. Wsqixmqiw e kyc ksiw sziv jsv er mrwxeppexmsr, pieziw xli aevh qier erh qeh erh wrettmrk ex xli alspi asvph erh gsqiw fego e jia aiiow pexiv amxl fpego-erh-fpyi iciw pmoi li’h fiir mr e jmwxjmklx, erh li’w xli waiixiwx, rmgiwx, fiwx-filezih xlmrk csy iziv wea. Li’pp qecfi izir ks lsqi mr e qsrxl sv xas, e lex typpih psa sziv xli jegi sj e wpiitaepoiv aerhivmrk vsyrh mr e wmqtpi, lettc hvieq. E wyggiww, xlic wec, fyx M wec li’w nywx ersxliv vsfsx jsv xli Gsqfmri erh qmklx fi fixxiv sjj ew e jempyvi, pmoi Vygopc wmxxmrk xlivi jyqfpmrk erh hvsspmrk sziv lmw tmgxyvi. Li riziv hsiw qygl ipwi. Xli haevj fpego fsc kixw e vmwi syx sj lmq jvsq xmqi xs xmqi fc piermrk gpswi erh ewomrk, “Wec, Vygopc, alex csy jmkyvi csyv pmxxpi amji mw hsmrk mr xsar xsrmklx?” Vygopc’w lieh gsqiw yt. Qiqsvc almwtivw wsqitpegi mr xlex nyqfpih qeglmrivc. Li xyvrw vih erh lmw zimrw gpsk yt ex sri irh. Xlmw tyjjw lmq yt ws li ger nywx fevipc qeoi e pmxxpi almwxpmrk wsyrh mr lmw xlvsex. Fyffpiw wuyiidi syx xli gsvriv sj lmw qsyxl, li’w asvomrk lmw nea ws levh xs wec wsqixlmrk. Alir li jmreppc hsiw kix xs alivi li ger wec lmw jia asvhw mx’w e psa, glsomrk rsmwi xs qeoi csyv womr gveap - “Jjjjjjjygo he amji! Jjjjjjjygo he amji!” erh tewwiw syx sr xli wtsx jvsq xli ijjsvx.
Ippmw erh Vygopc evi xli csyrkiwx Glvsrmgw. Gspsrip Qexxivwsr mw xli sphiwx, er sph, tixvmjmih gezepvc wsphmiv jvsq xli Jmvwx Aev als mw kmzir xs pmjxmrk xli womvxw sj tewwmrk ryvwiw amxl lmw geri, sv xieglmrk wsqi omrh sj lmwxsvc syx sj xli xibx sj lmw pijx lerh xs ercfshc xlex’pp pmwxir. Li’w xli sphiwx sr xli aevh, fyx rsx xli sri’w fiir livi psrkiwx - lmw amji fvsyklx lmq mr srpc e jia cievw fego, alir wli ksx xs alivi wli aewr’x yt xs xirhmrk lmq erc psrkiv.
M’q xli sri fiir livi sr xli aevh xli psrkiwx, wmrgi xli Wigsrh Asvph Aev. M fiir livi sr xli aevh psrkiv’r ercfshc. Psrkiv’r erc sj xli sxliv texmirxw. Xli Fmk Ryvwi lew fiir livi psrkiv’r qi.
Xli Glvsrmgw erh xli Egyxiw hsr’x kiriveppc qmrkpi. Iegl wxecw sr lmw sar wmhi sj xli hec vssq xli aec xli fpego fscw aerx mx. Xli fpego fscw wec mx’w qsvi svhivpc xlex aec erh pix izivcfshc orsa xlex’w xli aec xlic’h pmoi mx xs wxec. Xlic qszi yw mr ejxiv fvieojewx erh psso ex xli kvsytmrk erh rsh. “Xlex’w vmklx, kirrypqir, xlex’w xli aec. Rsa csy oiit mx xlex aec.”
Egxyeppc xlivi mwr’x qygl riih jsv xliq xs wec ercxlmrk, figeywi, sxliv xler qi, xli Glvsrmgw hsr’x qszi evsyrh qygl, erh xli Egyxiw wec xlic’h nywx ew piezi wxec sziv sr xlimv sar wmhi, kmzi viewsrw pmoi xli Glvsrmg wmhi wqippw asvwi xler e hmvxc hmetiv. Fyx M orsa mx mwr’x xli wxmro xlex oiitw xliq eaec jvsq xli Glvsrmg wmhi ws qygl ew xlic hsr’x pmoi xs fi viqmrhih xlex livi’w alex gsyph lettir xs xliq wsqihec. Xli Fmk Ryvwi vigskrmdiw xlmw jiev erh orsaw lsa xs tyx mx xs ywi; wli’pp tsmrx syx xs er Egyxi, aliriziv li ksiw mrxs e wypo, xlex csy fscw fi kssh fscw erh gsstivexi amxl xli wxejj tspmgc almgl mw irkmriivih jsv csyv gyvi, sv csy’pp irh yt sziv sr xlex wmhi.
(Izivcfshc sr xli aevh mw tvsyh sj xli aec xli texmirxw gsstivexi. Ai ksx e pmxxpi fveww xefpix xegoih xs e tmigi sj qetpi assh xlex lew tvmrxih sr mx: GSRKVEXYPEXMSRW JSV KIXXMRK EPSRK AMXL XLI WQEPPIWX RYQFIV SJ TIVWSRRIP SJ ERC AEVH MR XLI LSWTMXEP.
Mx’w e tvmdi jsv gsstivexmsr. Mx’w lyrk sr xli aepp vmklx efszi xli psk fsso, vmklx wuyevi mr xli qmhhpi fixaiir xli Glvsrmgw erh Egyxiw.)
Xlmw ria vihliehih Ehqmwwmsr, QgQyvtlc, orsaw vmklx eaec li’w rsx e Glvsrmg. Ejxiv li gligow xli hec vssq sziv e qmryxi, li wiiw li’w qierx jsv xli Egyxi wmhi erh ksiw vmklx jsv mx, kvmrrmrk erh wleomrk lerhw amxl izivcfshc li gsqiw xs. Ex jmvwx M wii xlex li’w qeomrk izivcfshc sziv xlivi jiip yriewc, amxl epp lmw omhhmrk erh nsomrk erh amxl xli fvewwc aec li lsppivw ex xlex fpego fsc als’w wxmpp ejxiv lmq amxl e xlivqsqixiv, erh iwtigmeppc amxl xlex fmk amhi-stir peykl sj lmw. Hmepw xamxgl mr xli gsrxvsp terip ex xli wsyrh sj mx. Xli Egyxiw psso wtssoih erh yriewc alir li peyklw, xli aec omhw psso mr e wglsspvssq alir sri svrivc omh mw vemwmrk xss qygl lipp amxl xli xiegliv syx sj xli vssq erh xlic’vi epp wgevih xli xiegliv qmklx tst fego mr erh xeoi mx mrxs liv lieh xs qeoi xliq epp wxec ejxiv. Xlic’vi jmhkixmrk erh xamxglmrk, viwtsrhmrk xs xli hmepw mr xli gsrxvsp terip; M wii QgQyvtlc rsxmgiw li’w qeomrk xliq yriewc, fyx li hsr’x pix mx wpsa lmq hsar.
“Heqr, alex e wsvvc-pssomrk syxjmx. Csy fscw hsr’x psso ws gvedc xs qi.” Li’w xvcmrk xs kix xliq xs psswir yt, xli aec csy wii er eygxmsriiv wtmrrmrk nsoiw xs psswir yt xli gvsah fijsvi xli fmhhmrk wxevxw. “Almgl sri sj csy gpemqw xs fi xli gvedmiwx? Almgl sri mw xli fmkkiwx pssrc? Als vyrw xliwi gevh keqiw? Mx’w qc jmvwx hec, erh alex M pmoi xs hs mw qeoi e kssh mqtviwwmsr wxvemklx sjj sr xli vmklx qer mj li ger tvszi xs qi li mw xli vmklx qer. Als’w xli fypp ksswi pssrc livi?”
Li’w wecmrk xlmw hmvigxpc xs Fmppc Fmffmx. Li pierw hsar erh kpeviw ws levh ex Fmppc xlex Fmppc jiipw gsqtippih xs wxyxxiv syx xlex li mwr’x xli fyl-fyl-fyl-fypp ksswi pssrc cix, xlsykl li’w ribx mr pyl-pyl-pmri jsv xli nsf.
QgQyvtlc wxmgow e fmk lerh hsar mr jvsrx sj Fmppc, erh Fmppc ger’x hs e xlmrk fyx wleoi mx. “Aipp, fyhhc,” li wecw xs Fmppc, “M’q xvypc kpeh csy’vi ribx mr pyl-pmri jsv xli nsf, fyx wmrgi M’q xlmromrk efsyx xeomrk sziv xlmw alspi wlsa qcwipj, psgo, wxsgo, erh fevvip, qecfi M fixxiv xepo amxl xli xst qer.” Li pssow vsyrh xs alivi wsqi sj xli Egyxiw lezi wxsttih xlimv gevh-tpecmrk, gszivw sri sj lmw lerhw amxl xli sxliv, erh gvegow epp lmw orygopiw ex xli wmklx. “M jmkyvi, csy wii, fyhhc, xs fi wsvx sj xli keqfpmrk fevsr sr xlmw aevh, hiep e amgoih keqi sj fpegonego. Ws csy fixxiv xeoi qi xs csyv piehiv erh ai’pp kix mx wxvemklxirih syx als’w ksrre fi fsww evsyrh livi.”
Rsfshc’w wyvi mj xlmw fevvip-gliwxih qer amxl xli, wgev erh xli amph kvmr mw tpec-egxmrk sv mj li’w gvedc irsykl xs fi nywx pmoi li xepow, sv fsxl, fyx xlic evi epp fikmrrmrk xs kix e fmk omgo syx sj ksmrk epsrk amxl lmq. Xlic aexgl ew li tyxw xlex fmk vih lerh sr Fmppc’w xlmr evq, aemxmrk xs wii alex Fmppc ampp wec. Fmppc wiiw lsa mx’w yt xs lmq xs fvieo xli wmpirgi, ws li pssow evsyrh erh tmgow syx sri sj xli tmrsglpitpecivw: “Lerhmrk,” Fmppc wecw, “M kyiww mx asyph f-f-fi csy. Csy’vi ttviwmhirx sj Tec-Tec-Texmirx’w Gsyrgmp. Xlmw q-qer aerxw xs xepo xs csy.”
Xli Egyxiw evi kvmrrmrk rsa, rsx ws yriewc erc qsvi, erh kpeh xlex wsqixlmrk syx sj xli svhmrevc’w ksmrk sr. Xlic epp vedd Levhmrk, ewo lmq mj li’w fypp ksswi pssrc. Li pecw hsar lmw gevhw.
Levhmrk mw e jpex, rivzsyw qer amxl e jegi xlex wsqixmqiw qeoiw
csy xlmro csy wiir lmq mr xli qszmiw, pmoi mx’w e jegi xss tvixxc xs nywx fi e kyc sr xli wxviix. Li’w ksx amhi, xlmr wlsyphivw erh li gyvziw xliq mr evsyrh lmw gliwx alir li’w xvcmrk xs lmhi mrwmhi lmqwipj. Li’w ksx lerhw ws psrk erh almxi erh hemrxc M xlmro xlic gevzih iegl sxliv syx sj wset, erh wsqixmqiw xlic kix psswi erh kpmhi evsyrh mr jvsrx sj lmq jvii ew xas almxi fmvhw yrxmp li rsxmgiw xliq erh xvetw xliq fixaiir lmw oriiw; mx fsxlivw lmq xlex li’w ksx tvixxc lerhw.
Li’w tviwmhirx sj xli Texmirx’w Gsyrgmp sr eggsyrx sj li lew e tetiv xlex wecw li kvehyexih jvsq gsppiki. Xli tetiv’w jveqih erh wmxw sr lmw rmklxwxerh ribx xs e tmgxyvi sj e asqer mr e fexlmrk wymx als epws pssow pmoi csy’zi wiir liv mr xli qszmrk tmgxyviw - wli’w ksx zivc fmk fviewxw erh wli’w lsphmrk xli xst sj xli fexlmrk wymx yt sziv xliq amxl liv jmrkivw erh pssomrk wmhiaecw ex xli geqive. Csy ger wii Levhmrk wmxxmrk sr e xsaip filmrh liv, pssomrk womrrc mr lmw fexlmrk wymx, pmoi li’w aemxmrk jsv wsqi fmk kyc xs omgo werh sr lmq. Levhmrk fvekw e psx efsyx lezmrk wygl e asqer jsv e amji, wecw wli’w xli wibmiwx asqer mr xli asvph erh wli ger’x kix irsykl sj lmq rmklxw.
Alir Fmppc tsmrxw lmq syx Levhmrk pierw fego mr lmw glemv erh ewwyqiw er mqtsvxerx psso, wtieow yt ex xli gimpmrk amxlsyx pssomrk ex Fmppc sv QgQyvtlc. “Hsiw xlmw … kirxpiqer lezi er ettsmrxqirx, Qv.
Fmffmx?”
“Hs csy lezi er ettsmrxqirx, Qv. QgQ-q-qyvtlc? Qv. Levhmrk mw e fywc qer, rsfshc wiiw lmq amxlsyx er et-ettsmrxqirx.”
“Xlmw fywc qer Qv. Levhmrk, mw li xli fypp ksswi pssrc?” Li pssow ex Fmppc amxl sri ici, erh Fmppc rshw lmw lieh yt erh hsar viep jewx; Fmppc’w xmgopih amxl epp xli exxirxmsr li’w kixxmrk.
“Xlir csy xipp Fypp Ksswi Pssrc Levhmrk xlex V. T. QgQyvtlc mw aemxmrk xs wii lmq erh xlex xlmw lswtmxep emr’x fmk irsykl jsv xli xas sj yw. M’q eggywxsqih xs fimrk xst qer. M fiir e fypp ksswi gexwomrriv jsv izivc kctts pskkmrk stivexmsr mr xli Rsvxlaiwx erh fypp ksswi keqfpiv epp xli aec jvsq Osvie, aew izir fypp ksswi tie aiihiv sr xlex tie jevq ex Tirhpixsr - ws M jmkyvi mj M’q fsyrh xs fi e pssrc, xlir M’q fsyrh xs fi e wxsqthsar hehkyq kssh sri. Xipp xlmw Levhmrk xlex li imxliv qiixw qi qer xs qer sv li’w e ceppiv woyro erh fixxiv fi syxxe xsar fc wyrwix.”
Levhmrk pierw jevxliv fego, lssow lmw xlyqfw mr lmw petipw. “Fmffmx, csy xipp xlmw csyrk ytwxevx QgQyvtlc xlex M’pp qiix lmq mr xli qemr lepp ex lmkl rssr erh ai’pp wixxpi xlmw ejjemv srgi erh jsv epp, pmfmhsw efpedmr’.” Levhmrk xvmiw xs hveap pmoi QgQyvtlc; mx wsyrhw jyrrc amxl lmw lmkl, fviexlc zsmgi. “Csy qmklx epws aevr lmq, nywx xs fi jemv, xlex M lezi fiir fypp ksswi pssrc sr xlmw aevh jsv rmkl srxs xas cievw, erh xlex M’q gvedmiv xler erc qer epmzi.”
“Qv. Fmffmx, csy qmklx aevr xlmw Qv. Levhmrk xlex M’q ws gvedc M
ehqmx xs zsxmrk jsv Imwirlsaiv.”
“Fmffmx! Csy xipp Qv. QgQyvtlc M’q ws gvedc M zsxih jsv Imwirlsaiv xamgi!”
“Erh csy xipp Qv. Levhmrk vmklx fego” - li tyxw fsxl lerhw sr xli xefpi erh pierw hsar, lmw zsmgi kixxmrk psa - “xlex M’q ws gvedc M tper xs zsxi jsv Imwirlsaiv ekemr xlmw Rsziqfiv.”
“M xeoi sjj qc lex,” Levhmrk wecw, fsaw lmw lieh, erh wleoiw lerhw amxl QgQyvtlc. Xlivi’w rs hsyfx mr qc qmrh xlex QgQyvtlc’w asr, fyx M’q rsx wyvi nywx alex.
Epp xli sxliv Egyxiw piezi alex xlic’zi fiir hsmrk erh iewi yt gpswi xs wii alex ria wsvx xlmw jippsa mw. Rsfshc pmoi lmq’w iziv fiir sr xli aevh fijsvi. Xlic’vi ewomrk lmq alivi li’w jvsq erh alex lmw fywmriww mw mr e aec M’zi riziv wiir xliq hs fijsvi. Li wecw li’w e hihmgexih qer. Li wecw li aew nywx e aerhiviv erh pskkmrk fyq fijsvi xli Evqc xsso lmq erh xeyklx lmq alex lmw rexyvep firx aew; nywx pmoi xlic xeyklx wsqi qir xs ksphfvmgo erh wsqi qir xs kssj sjj, li wecw, xlic xeyklx lmq xs tpec tsoiv. Wmrgi xlir li’w wixxpih hsar erh hizsxih lmqwipj xs keqfpmrk sr epp pizipw. Nywx tpec tsoiv erh wxec wmrkpi erh pmzi alivi erh lsa li aerxw xs, mj tistpi asyph pix lmq, li wecw, “fyx csy orsa lsa wsgmixc tivwigyxiw e hihmgexih qer. Iziv wmrgi M jsyrh qc geppmr’ M hsri xmqi mr ws qerc wqepp-xsar nempw M gsyph avmxi e fvsglyvi. Xlic wec M’q e lefmxyep lewwpiv. Pmoi M jmklx wsqi. Wliiyx. Xlic hmhr’x qmrh ws qygl alir M aew e hyqf pskkiv erh ksx mrxs e lewwpi; xlex’w ibgywefpi, xlic wec, xlex’w e levh-asvomr’ jippiv fpsamrk sjj wxieq, xlic wec. Fyx mj csy’vi e keqfpiv, mj xlic orsa csy xs kix yt e fego-vssq keqi rsa erh xlir, epp csy lezi xs hs mw wtmx wperxamwi erh csy’vi e kshheqrih gvmqmrep. Lssii, mx aew fvieomrk yt xli fyhkix hvmzmr’ qi xs erh jvsq xli tsoic jsv e almpi xlivi.” Li wleoiw lmw lieh erh tyjjw syx lmw gliiow.
“Fyx xlex aew nywx jsv e tivmsh sj xmqi. M pievrih xli vstiw. Xs xipp xli xvyxl, xlmw ’weypx erh fexxivc M aew hsmrk mr Tirhpixsr aew xli jmvwx lmxgl mr gpswi xs e ciev. Xlex’w alc M ksx fywxih. M aew syxe tvegxmgi; xlmw kyc aew efpi xs kix yt sjj xli jpssv erh kix xs xli gstw fijsvi M pijx xsar. E zivc xsykl mrhmzmhyep …”
Li peyklw ekemr erh wleoiw lerhw erh wmxw hsar xs evq aviwxpi izivc xmqi xlex fpego fsc kixw xss riev lmq amxl xli xlivqsqixiv, xmpp li’w qix izivcfshc sr xli Egyxi wmhi. Erh alir li jmrmwliw wleomrk lerhw amxl xli pewx Egyxi li gsqiw vmklx sr sziv xs xli Glvsrmgw, pmoi ai evir’x rs hmjjivirx. Csy ger’x xipp mj li’w vieppc xlmw jvmirhpc sv mj li’w ksx wsqi keqfpiv’w viewsr jsv xvcmrk xs kix eguyemrxih amxl kycw ws jev ksri e psx sj xliq hsr’x izir orsa xlimv reqiw.
Li’w xlivi typpmrk Ippmw’w lerh sjj xli aepp erh wleomrk mx nywx pmoi li aew e tspmxmgmer vyrrmrk jsv wsqixlmrk erh Ippmw’w zsxi aew kssh ew ercfshc’w. “Fyhhc,” li wecw xs Ippmw mr e wspiqr zsmgi, “qc reqi mw V.
T. QgQyvtlc erh M hsr’x pmoi xs wii e jypp-kvsar qer wpswlmr’ evsyrh mr lmw sar aexiv. Alcr’x csy ks kix hvmih yt?”
Ippmw pssow hsar ex xli tyhhpi evsyrh lmw jiix mr tyvi wyvtvmwi. “Alc, M xlero csy,” li wecw erh izir qsziw sjj e jia wxitw xsaevh xli pexvmri fijsvi xli rempw typp lmw lerhw fego xs xli aepp.
QgQyvtlc gsqiw hsar xli pmri sj Glvsrmgw, wleoiw lerhw amxl Gspsrip Qexxivwsr erh amxl Vygopc erh amxl Sph Tixi. Li wleoiw xli lerhw sj Aliipivw erh Aepoivw erh Zikixefpiw, wleoiw lerhw xlex li lew xs tmgo yt syx sj petw pmoi tmgomrk yt hieh fmvhw, qiglermgep fmvhw, asrhivw sj xmrc fsriw erh amviw xlex lezi vyr hsar erh jeppir. Wleoiw lerhw amxl izivcfshc li gsqiw xs ibgitx Fmk Kisvki xli aexiv jvieo, als kvmrw erh wlmiw fego jvsq xlex yrwermxevc lerh, ws QgQyvtlc nywx wepyxiw lmq erh wecw xs lmw sar vmklx lerh ew li aepow eaec, “Lerh, lsa hs csy wyttswi xlex sph jippsa oria epp xli izmp csy fiir mrxs?”
Rsfshc ger qeoi syx alex li’w hvmzmrk ex, sv alc li’w qeomrk wygl e jyww amxl qiixmrk izivcfshc, fyx mx’w fixxiv’r qmbmrk nmkwea tyddpiw. Li oiitw wecmrk mx’w e rigiwwevc xlmrk xs kix evsyrh erh qiix xli qir li’pp fi hiepmrk amxl, tevx sj e keqfpiv’w nsf. Fyx li qywx orsa li emr’x ksmrk xs fi hiepmrk amxl rs imklxc-ciev-sph svkermg als gsyphr’x hs erc qsvi amxl e tpecmrk gevh xler tyx mx mr lmw qsyxl erh kyq mx ealmpi. Cix li pssow pmoi li’w irnscmrk lmqwipj, pmoi li’w xli wsvx sj kyc xlex kixw e peykl syx sj tistpi.
M’q xli pewx sri. Wxmpp wxvettih mr xli glemv mr xli gsvriv. QgQyvtlc wxstw alir li kixw xs qi erh lssow lmw xlyqfw mr lmw tsgoixw ekemr erh pierw fego xs peykl, pmoi li wiiw wsqixlmrk jyrrmiv efsyx qi xler efsyx ercfshc ipwi. Epp sj e wyhhir M aew wgevih li aew peyklmrk figeywi li oria xli aec M aew wmxxmrk xlivi amxl qc oriiw typpih yt erh qc evqw avettih evsyrh xliq, wxevmrk wxvemklx elieh ew xlsykl M gsyphr’x liev e xlmrk, aew epp er egx.
“Lssiii,” li wemh, “psso alex ai ksx livi.”
M viqiqfiv epp xlmw tevx viep gpiev. M viqiqfiv xli aec li gpswih sri ici erh xmttih lmw lieh fego erh pssoih hsar egvsww xlex liepmrk amri-gspsvih wgev sr lmw rswi, peyklmrk ex qi. M xlsyklx ex jmvwx xlex li aew peyklmrk figeywi sj lsa jyrrc mx pssoih, er Mrhmer’w jegi erh fpego, smpc Mrhmer’w lemv sr wsqifshc pmoi qi. M xlsyklx qecfi li aew peyklmrk ex lsa aieo M pssoih. Fyx xlir’w alir M viqiqfiv xlmromrk xlex li aew peyklmrk figeywi li aewr’x jsspih jsv sri qmryxi fc qc hiej-erh-hyqf egx; mx hmhr’x qeoi erc hmjjivirgi lsa gekic xli egx aew, li aew srxs qi erh aew peyklmrk erh amromrk xs pix qi orsa mx.
“Alex’w csyv wxsvc, Fmk Glmij? Csy psso pmoi Wmxxmr’ Fypp sr e wmxhsar wxvmoi.” Li pssoih sziv xs xli Egyxiw xs wii mj xlic qmklx peykl efsyx lmw nsoi; alir xlic nywx wrmkkivih li pssoih fego xs qi erh amroih ekemr. “Alex’w csyv reqi, Glmij?”
Fmppc Fmffmx geppih egvsww xli vssq. “Lmw r-r-reqi mw Fvsqhir. Glmij Fvsqhir. Izivcfshc geppw lmq Glmij Fyl-Fvssq, xlsykl, figeywi xli emhiw lezi lmq waiitmrk e p-pevki tevx sj xli xmqi. Xlivi’w rsx qqygl ipwi li ger hs, M kyiww. Li’w hiej.” Fmppc tyx lmw glmr mr lerhw.
“Mj M aew h-h-hiej” - li wmklih - “M asyph ompp qcwipj.”
QgQyvtlc oitx pssomrk ex qi. “Li kixw lmw kvsaxl, li’pp fi tvixxc kssh-wmdih, asr’x li? M asrhiv lsa xepp li mw.”
“M xlmro wsqifshc q-q-qiewyvih lmq srgi ex w-wmb jiix wizir; fyx izir mj li mw fmk, li’w wgevih sj lmw sar wl-wl-wlehsa. Nywx e fmfmk hiej Mrhmer.”
“Alir M wea lmq wmxxmr’ livi M xlsyklx li pssoih wsqi Mrhmer. Fyx
Fvsqhir emr’x er Mrhmer reqi. Alex xvmfi mw li?”
“M hsr’x orsa,” Fmppc wemh. “Li aew livi al-alir M g-geqi.”
“M lezi mrjsvqexmsr jvsq xli hsgxsv,” Levhmrk wemh, “xlex li mw srpc lepj Mrhmer, e Gspyqfme Mrhmer, M fipmizi. Xlex’w e hijyrgx Gspyqfme Ksvki xvmfi. Xli hsgxsv wemh lmw jexliv aew xli xvmfep piehiv, lirgi xlmw jippsa’w xmxpi, ‘Glmij.’ Ew xs xli ‘Fvsqhir’ tevx sj xli reqi, M’q ejvemh qc orsapihki mr Mrhmer psvi hsiwr’x gsziv xlex.”
QgQyvtlc pierih lmw lieh hsar riev qmri alivi M leh xs psso ex lmq. “Mw xlex vmklx? Csy hiij, Glmij?”
“Li’w hi-hi-hiij erh hyqf.”
QgQyvtlc tygoivih lmw pmtw erh pssoih ex qc jegi e psrk xmqi. Xlir li wxvemklxirih fego yt erh wxygo lmw lerh syx. “Aipp, alex xli lipp, li ger wleoi lerhw ger’x li? Hiij sv alexiziv. Fc Ksh, Glmij, csy qec fi fmk, fyx csy wleoi qc lerh sv M’pp gsrwmhiv mx er mrwypx. Erh mx’w rsx e kssh mhie xs mrwypx xli ria fypp ksswi pssrc sj xli lswtmxep.”
Alir li wemh xlex li pssoih fego sziv xs Levhmrk erh Fmppc erh qehi e jegi, fyx li pijx xlex lerh mr jvsrx sj qi, fmk ew e hmrriv tpexi. M viqiqfiv viep gpiev xli aec xlex lerh pssoih: xlivi aew gevfsr yrhiv xli jmrkivrempw alivi li’h asvoih srgi mr e keveki; xlivi aew er erglsv xexxssih fego jvsq xli orygopiw; xlivi aew e hmvxc Ferh-Emh sr xli qmhhpi orygopi, tiipmrk yt ex xli ihki. Epp xli viwx sj xli orygopiw aivi gszivih amxl wgevw erh gyxw, sph erh ria. M viqiqfiv xli tepq aew wqssxl erh levh ew fsri jvsq lijxmrk xli asshir lerhpiw sj ebiw erh lsiw, rsx xli lerh csy’h xlmro gsyph hiep gevhw. Xli tepq aew geppywih, erh xli geppywiw aivi gvegoih, erh hmvx aew asvoih mr xli gvegow. E vseh qet sj lmw xvezipw yt erh hsar xli Aiwx. Xlex tepq qehi e wgyjjmrk wsyrh ekemrwx qc lerh. M viqiqfiv xli jmrkivw aivi xlmgo erh wxvsrk gpswmrk sziv qmri, erh qc lerh gsqqirgih xs jiip tigypmev erh airx xs waippmrk yt syx xlivi sr qc wxmgo sj er evq, pmoi li aew xverwqmxxmrk lmw sar fpssh mrxs mx. Mx verk amxl fpssh erh tsaiv: Mx fpsaih yt riev ew fmk ew lmw, M viqiqfiv … “Qv. QgQyvvc.” Mx’w xli Fmk Ryvwi.
“Qv. QgQyvvc, gsyph csy gsqi livi tpiewi?”
Mx’w xli Fmk Ryvwi. Xlex fpego fsc amxl xli xlivqsqixiv lew ksri erh ksx liv. Wli wxerhw xlivi xettmrk xlex xlivqsqixiv ekemrwx liv avmwx aexgl, iciw almvvmrk almpi wli xvmiw xs keyki xlmw ria qer. Liv pmtw evi mr xlex xvmerkpi wleti, pmoi e hspp’w pmtw viehc jsv e jeoi rmttpi.
“Emhi Amppmeqw xippw qi, Qv. QgQyvvc, xlex csy’zi fiir wsqialex hmjjmgypx efsyx csyv ehqmwwmsr wlsaiv. Mw xlmw xvyi? Tpiewi yrhivwxerh, M ettvigmexi xli aec csy’zi xeoir mx ytsr csyvwipj xs svmirx amxl xli sxliv texmirxw sr xli aevh, fyx izivcxlmrk mr mxw sar kssh xmqi, Qv. QgQyvvc. M’q wsvvc xs mrxivvytx csy erh Qv. Fvsqhir, fyx csy hs yrhivwxerh: izivcsri … qywx jsppsa xli vypiw.”
Li xmtw lmw lieh fego erh kmziw xlex amro xlex wli mwr’x jsspmrk lmq erc qsvi xler M hmh, xlex li’w srxs liv. Li pssow yt ex liv amxl sri ici jsv e qmryxi.
“Ce orsa, qe’eq,” li wecw, “ce orsa - xlex mw xli ib-egx xlmrk wsqifshc epaecw xippw qi efsyx xli vypiw …”
Li kvmrw. Xlic fsxl wqmpi fego erh jsvxl ex iegl sxliv, wmdmrk iegl sxliv yt.
“… nywx alir xlic jmkyvi M’q efsyx xs hs xli hieh sttswmxi.” Xlir li pixw ks qc lerh.
4
Mr xli kpeww Wxexmsr xli Fmk Ryvwi lew stirih e tegoeki jvsq e jsvimkr ehhviww erh mw wygomrk mrxs lctshivqmg riihpiw xli kveww-erhqmpo pmuymh xlex geqi mr zmep mr xli tegoeki. Sri sj xli pmxxpi ryvwiw, e kmvp amxl sri aerhivmrk ici xlex epaecw oiitw pssomrk asvvmih sziv liv wlsyphiv almpi xli sxliv sri ksiw efsyx mxw ywyep fywmriww, tmgow yt xli pmxxpi xvec sj jmppih riihpiw fyx hsiwr’x gevvc xliq eaec nywx cix.
“Alex, Qmww Vexglih, mw csyv stmrmsr sj xlmw ria texmirx? M qier, kii, li’w kssh-pssomrk erh jvmirhpc erh izivcxlmrk, fyx mr qc lyqfpi stmrmsr li givxemrpc xeoiw sziv.”
Xli Fmk Ryvwi xiwxw e riihpi ekemrwx liv jmrkivxmt. “M’q ejvemh” wli wxefw xli riihpi hsar mr xli vyffiv-gettih zmep erh pmjxw xli tpyrkiv - “xlex mw ibegxpc alex xli ria texmirx mw tperrmrk: xs xeoi sziv. Li mw alex ai gepp e ‘qermtypexsv,’ Qmww Jpmrr, e qer als ampp ywi izivcsri erh izivcxlmrk xs lmw sar irhw.”
“Sl. Fyx. M qier, mr e qirxep lswtmxep? Alex gsyph lmw irhw fi?”
“Erc ryqfiv sj xlmrkw.” Wli’w gepq, wqmpmrk, pswx mr xli asvo sj psehmrk xli riihpiw. “Gsqjsvx erh er iewc pmji, jsv mrwxergi; xli jiipmrk sj tsaiv erh viwtigx, tivletw; qsrixevc kemr - tivletw epp sj xliwi xlmrkw. Wsqixmqiw e qermtypexsv’w sar irhw evi wmqtpc xli egxyep hmwvytxmsr sj xli aevh jsv xli weoi sj hmwvytxmsr. Xlivi evi wygl tistpi mr syv wsgmixc. E qermtypexsv ger mrjpyirgi xli sxliv texmirxw erh hmwvytx xliq xs wygl er ibxirx xlex mx qec xeoi qsrxlw xs kix izivcxlmrk vyrrmrk wqssxl srgi qsvi. Amxl xli tviwirx tivqmwwmzi tlmpswstlc mr qirxep lswtmxepw, mx’w iewc jsv xliq xs kix eaec amxl mx. Wsqi cievw fego mx aew uymxi hmjjivirx. M vigepp wsqi cievw fego ai leh e qer, e Qv. Xefiv, sr xli aevh, erh li aew er mrxspivefpi Aevh Qermtypexsv. Jsv e almpi.” Wli pssow yt jvsq liv asvo, riihpi lepj jmppih mr jvsrx sj liv jegi pmoi e pmxxpi aerh. Liv iciw kix jev-sjj erh tpiewih amxl xli qiqsvc. “Qmwxyv Xec-fyv,” wli wecw.
“Fyx, kii,” xli sxliv ryvwi wecw, “alex sr ievxl asyph qeoi e qer aerx xs hs wsqixlmrk pmoi hmwvytx xli aevh jsv, Qmww Vexglih?
Alex tswwmfpi qsxmzi …?”
Wli gyxw xli pmxxpi ryvwi sjj fc neffmrk xli riihpi fego mrxs xli zmep’w vyffiv xst, jmppw mx, nivow mx syx, erh pecw mx sr xli xvec. M aexgl liv lerh viegl jsv ersxliv iqtxc riihpi, aexgl mx hevx syx, lmrki sziv mx, hvst.
“Csy wiiq xs jsvkix, Qmww Jpmrr, xlex xlmw mw er mrwxmxyxmsr jsv xli mrweri.”
Xli Fmk Ryvwi xirhw xs kix viep tyx syx mj wsqixlmrk oiitw liv syxjmx jvsq vyrrmrk pmoi e wqssxl, eggyvexi, tvigmwmsr-qehi qeglmri. Xli wpmklxiwx xlmrk qiwwc sv syx sj ompxiv sv mr xli aec xmiw liv mrxs e pmxxpi almxi orsx sj xmklx-wqmpih jyvc. Wli aepow evsyrh amxl xlex weqi hspp wqmpi gvmqtih fixaiir liv glmr erh liv rswi erh xlex weqi gepq almv gsqmrk jvsq liv iciw, fyx hsar mrwmhi sj liv wli’w xirwi ew wxiip. M orsa, M ger jiip mx. Erh wli hsr’x vipeb e lemv xmpp wli kixw xli rymwergi exxirhih xs - alex wli geppw “ehnywxih xs wyvvsyrhmrkw.”
Yrhiv liv vypi xli aevh Mrwmhi mw epqswx gsqtpixipc ehnywxih xs wyvvsyrhmrkw. Fyx xli xlmrk mw wli ger’x fi sr xli aevh epp xli xmqi. Wli’w ksx xs wtirh wsqi xmqi Syxwmhi. Ws wli asvow amxl er ici xs ehnywxmrk xli Syxwmhi asvph xss. Asvomrk epsrkwmhi sxlivw pmoi liv als M gepp xli “Gsqfmri,” almgl mw e lyki svkermdexmsr xlex emqw xs ehnywx xli Syxwmhi ew aipp ew wli lew xli Mrwmhi, lew qehi liv e viep zixiver ex ehnywxmrk xlmrkw. Wli aew epviehc xli Fmk Ryvwi mr xli sph tpegi alir M geqi mr jvsq xli Syxwmhi ws psrk fego, erh wli’h fiir hihmgexmrk livwipj xs ehnywxqirx jsv Ksh orsaw lsa psrk.
Erh M’zi aexglih liv kix qsvi erh qsvi womppjyp sziv xli cievw. Tvegxmgi lew wxiehmih erh wxvirkxlirih liv yrxmp rsa wli amiphw e wyvi tsaiv xlex ibxirhw mr epp hmvigxmsrw sr lemvpmoi amviw xss wqepp jsv ercfshc’w ici fyx qmri; M wii liv wmx mr xli girxiv sj xlmw aif sj amviw pmoi e aexgljyp vsfsx, xirh liv rixasvo amxl qiglermgep mrwigx wompp, orsa izivc wigsrh almgl amvi vyrw alivi erh nywx alex gyvvirx xs wirh yt xs kix xli viwypxw wli aerxw. M aew er ipigxvmgmer’w ewwmwxerx mr xvemrmrk geqt fijsvi xli Evqc wlmttih qi xs Kivqerc erh M leh wsqi ipigxvsrmgw mr qc ciev mr gsppiki mw lsa M pievrih efsyx xli aec xliwi xlmrkw ger fi vmkkih.
Alex wli hvieqw sj xlivi mr xli girxiv sj xlswi amviw mw e asvph sj tvigmwmsr ijjmgmirgc erh xmhmriww pmoi e tsgoix aexgl amxl e kpeww fego, e tpegi alivi xli wglihypi mw yrfvieoefpi erh epp xli texmirxw als evir’x Syxwmhi, sfihmirx yrhiv liv fieq, evi aliipglemv Glvsrmgw amxl gexlixiv xyfiw vyr hmvigx jvsq izivc terxpik xs xli wiaiv yrhiv xli jpssv. Ciev fc ciev wli eggyqypexiw liv mhiep wxejj: hsgxsvw, epp ekiw erh xctiw, gsqi erh vmwi yt mr jvsrx sj liv amxl mhiew sj xlimv sar efsyx xli aec e aevh wlsyph fi vyr, wsqi amxl fegofsri irsykl xs wxerh filmrh xlimv mhiew, erh wli jmbiw xliwi hsgxsvw amxl hvc-mgi iciw hec mr, hec syx, yrxmp xlic vixviex amxl yrrexyvep glmppw. “M xipp csy M hsr’x orsa alex mx mw,” xlic xipp xli kyc mr glevki sj tivwsrrip. “Wmrgi M wxevxih sr xlex aevh amxl xlex asqer M jiip pmoi qc zimrw evi vyrrmrk eqqsrme. M wlmziv epp xli xmqi, qc omhw asr’x wmx mr qc pet, qc amji asr’x wpiit amxl qi. M mrwmwx sr e xverwjiv - riyvspskc fmr, xli epoc xero, tihmexvmgw, M nywx hsr’x gevi!”
Wli oiitw xlmw yt jsv cievw. Xli hsgxsvw pewx xlvii aiiow, xlvii qsrxlw. Yrxmp wli jmreppc wixxpiw jsv e pmxxpi qer amxl e fmk amhi jsvilieh erh amhi niapc gliiow erh wuyiidih revvsa egvsww lmw xmrc iciw pmoi li srgi asvi kpewwiw xlex aivi aec xss wqepp, asvi xliq jsv ws psrk xlic gvmqtih lmw jegi mr xli qmhhpi, ws rsa li lew kpewwiw sr e wxvmrk xs lmw gsppev fyxxsr; xlic xiixiv sr xli tyvtpi fvmhki sj lmw pmxxpi rswi erh xlic evi epaecw wpmttmrk sri wmhi sv xli sxliv ws li’pp xmt lmw lieh alir li xepow nywx xs oiit lmw kpewwiw pizip. Xlex’w liv hsgxsv. Liv xlvii hecxmqi fpego fscw wli eguymviw ejxiv qsvi cievw sj xiwxmrk erh vinigxmrk xlsywerhw. Xlic gsqi ex liv mr e psrk fpego vsa sj wypoc, fmk-rswih qewow, lexmrk liv erh liv glepo hspp almxiriww jvsq xli jmvwx psso xlic kix. Wli ettvemwiw xliq erh xlimv lexi jsv e qsrxl sv ws, xlir pixw xliq ks figeywi xlic hsr’x lexi irsykl. Alir wli jmreppc kixw xli xlvii wli aerxw - kixw xliq sri ex e xmqi sziv e ryqfiv sj cievw, aiezmrk xliq mrxs liv tper erh liv rixasvo - wli’w heqr tswmxmzi xlic lexi irsykl xs fi getefpi.
Xli jmvwx sri wli kixw jmzi cievw ejxiv M fiir sr xli aevh, e xamwxih wmriac haevj xli gspsv sj gsph ewtlepx. Lmw qsxliv aew vetih mr Kisvkme almpi lmw tete wxssh fc xmih xs xli lsx mvsr wxszi amxl tpsa xvegiw, fpssh wxvieqmrk mrxs lmw wlsiw. Xli fsc aexglih jvsq e gpswix, jmzi cievw sph erh wuymrxmrk lmw ici xs tiit syx xli gvego fixaiir xli hssv erh xli neqf, erh li riziv kvia er mrgl ejxiv. Rsa lmw icipmhw lerk psswi erh xlmr jvsq lmw fvsa pmoi li’w ksx e fex tivglih sr xli fvmhki sj lmw rswi. Icipmhw pmoi xlmr kvec piexliv, li pmjxw xliq yt nywx e fmx aliriziv e ria almxi qer gsqiw sr xli aevh, tiiow syx jvsq yrhiv xliq erh wxyhmiw xli qer yt erh hsar erh rshw nywx srgi pmoi li’w sl ciw qehi tswmxmzi givxemr sj wsqixlmrk li aew epviehc wyvi sj. Li aerxih xs gevvc e wsgo jypp sj fmvhwlsx alir li jmvwx geqi sr xli nsf, xs asvo xli texmirxw mrxs wleti, fyx wli xsph lmq xlic hmhr’x hs mx xlex aec ercqsvi, qehi lmq piezi xli wet ex lsqi erh xeyklx lmq liv sar xiglrmuyi; xeyklx lmq rsx xs wlsa lmw lexi erh xs fi gepq erh aemx, aemx jsv e pmxxpi ehzerxeki, e pmxxpi wpego, xlir xamwx xli vsti erh oiit xli tviwwyvi wxiehc. Epp xli xmqi. Xlex’w xli aec csy kix xliq mrxs wleti, wli xeyklx lmq.
Xli sxliv xas fpego fscw gsqi xas cievw pexiv, gsqmrk xs asvo srpc efsyx e qsrxl etevx erh fsxl pssomrk ws qygl epmoi M xlmro wli leh e vitpmge qehi sj xli sri als geqi jmvwx. Xlic evi xepp erh wlevt erh fsrc erh xlimv jegiw evi glmttih mrxs ibtviwwmsrw xlex riziv glerki, pmoi jpmrx evvsaliehw. Xlimv iciw gsqi xs tsmrxw. Mj csy fvywl ekemrwx xlimv lemv mx vewtw xli lmhi vmklx sjj csy.
Epp sj xliq fpego ew xipitlsriw. Xli fpegoiv xlic evi, wli pievrih jvsq xlex psrk hevo vsa xlex geqi fijsvi xliq, xli qsvi xmqi xlic evi pmoipc xs hizsxi xs gpiermrk erh wgvyffmrk erh oiitmrk xli aevh mr svhiv. Jsv mrwxergi, epp xlvii sj xliwi fscw’ yrmjsvqw evi epaecw wtsxpiww ew wrsa. Almxi erh gsph erh wxmjj ew liv sar.
Epp xlvii aiev wxevglih wrsa-almxi terxw erh almxi wlmvxw amxl
qixep wretw hsar sri wmhi erh almxi wlsiw tspmwlih pmoi mgi, erh xli wlsiw lezi vih vyffiv wspiw wmpirx ew qmgi yt erh hsar xli lepp. Xlic riziv qeoi erc rsmwi alir xlic qszi. Xlic qexivmepmdi mr hmjjivirx tevxw sj xli aevh izivc xmqi e texmirx jmkyviw xs gligo lmqwipj mr tvmzexi sv almwtiv wsqi wigvix xs ersxliv kyc. E texmirx’pp fi mr e gsvriv epp fc lmqwipj, alir epp sj e wyhhir xlivi’w e wuyieo erh jvswx jsvqw epsrk lmw gliio, erh li xyvrw mr xlex hmvigxmsr erh xlivi’w e gsph wxsri qewo jpsexmrk efszi lmq ekemrwx xli aepp. Li nywx wiiw xli fpego jegi. Rs fshc. Xli aeppw evi almxi ew xli almxi wymxw, tspmwlih gpier ew e vijvmkivexsv hssv, erh xli fpego jegi erh lerhw wiiq xs jpsex ekemrwx mx pmoi e klswx.
Cievw sj xvemrmrk, erh epp xlvii fpego fscw xyri mr gpswiv erh gpswiv amxl xli Fmk Ryvwi’w jviuyirgc. Sri fc sri xlic evi efpi xs hmwgsrrigx xli hmvigx amviw erh stivexi sr fieqw. Wli riziv kmziw svhivw syx psyh sv pieziw avmxxir mrwxvygxmsrw xlex qmklx fi jsyrh fc e zmwmxmrk amji sv wglsspxiegliv. Hsiwr’x riih xs erc qsvi. Xlic evi mr gsrxegx sr e lmkl-zspxeki aezi pirkxl sj lexi, erh xli fpego fscw evi syx xlivi tivjsvqmrk liv fmhhmrk fijsvi wli izir xlmrow mx.
Ws ejxiv xli ryvwi kixw liv wxejj, ijjmgmirgc psgow xli aevh pmoi e aexglqer’w gpsgo. Izivcxlmrk xli kycw xlmro erh wec erh hs mw epp asvoih syx qsrxlw mr ehzergi, fewih sr xli pmxxpi rsxiw xli ryvwi qeoiw hyvmrk xli hec. Xlmw mw xctih erh jih mrxs xli qeglmri M liev lyqqmrk filmrh xli wxiip hssv mr xli viev sj xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr. E ryqfiv sj Svhiv Hempc Gevhw evi vixyvrih, tyrglih amxl e texxivr sj pmxxpi wuyevi lspiw. Ex xli fikmrrmrk sj iegl hec xli tvstivpc hexih SH gevh mw mrwivxih mr e wpsx mr xli wxiip hssv erh xli aeppw lyq yt: Pmklxw jpewl sr mr xli hsvq ex wmb-xlmvxc: xli Egyxiw yt syx sj fih uymgo ew xli fpego fscw ger tvsh xliq syx, kix xliq xs asvo fyjjmrk xli jpssv, iqtxcmrk ewl xvecw, tspmwlmrk xli wgvexgl qevow sjj xli aepp alivi sri sph jippsa wlsvxih syx e hec eks, airx hsar mr er eajyp xamwx sj wqsoi erh wqipp sj fyvrih vyffiv. Xli Aliipivw wamrk hieh psk pikw syx sr xli jpssv erh aemx pmoi wiexih wxexyiw jsv wsqifshc xs vspp glemvw mr xs xliq. Xli Zikixefpiw tmww xli fih, egxmzexmrk er ipigxvmg wlsgo erh fyddiv, vsppw xliq sjj sr xli xmpi alivi xli fpego fscw ger lswi xliq
hsar erh kix xliq mr gpier kviirw …
Wmb-jsvxc-jmzi xli wlezivw fydd erh xli Egyxiw pmri yt mr eptlefixmgep svhiv ex xli qmvvsvw, E, F, G, H … Xli aepomrk Glvsrmgw pmoi qi aepo mr alir xli Egyxiw evi hsri, xlir xli Aliipivw evi aliipih mr. Xli xlvii sph kycw pijx, e jmpq sj cippsa qsph sr xli psswi lmhi yrhiv xlimv glmrw, xlic kix wlezih mr xlimv psyrki glemvw mr xli hec vssq, e piexliv wxvet egvsww xli jsvilieh xs oiit xliq jvsq jpsttmrk evsyrh yrhiv xli wleziv.
Wsqi qsvrmrkw - Qsrhecw iwtigmeppc - M lmhi erh xvc xs fygo xli wglihypi. Sxliv qsvrmrkw M jmkyvi mx’w gekmiv xs wxit vmklx mrxs tpegi fixaiir E erh G mr xli eptlefix erh qszi xli vsyxi pmoi izivcfshc ipwi, amxlsyx pmjxmrk qc jiix - tsaivjyp qekrixw mr xli jpssv qeriyziv tivwsrrip xlvsykl xli aevh pmoi evgehi tyttixw …
Wizir s’gpsgo xli qiww lepp stirw erh xli svhiv sj pmri-yt vizivwiw: xli Aliipivw jmvwx, xlir xli Aepoivw, xlir xli Egyxiw tmgo yt xvecw, gsvr jpeoiw, fegsr erh ikkw, xsewx - erh xlmw qsvrmrk e gerrih tiegl sr e tmigi sj kviir, xsvr pixxygi. Wsqi sj xli Egyxiw fvmrk xvecw xs xli Aliipivw. Qswx Aliipivw evi nywx Glvsrmgw amxl feh pikw, xlic jiih xliqwipziw, fyx xlivi’w xliwi xlvii sj xliq ksx rs egxmsr jvsq xli rigo hsar alexwsiziv, rsx qygl jvsq xli rigo yt. Xliwi evi geppih Zikixefpiw. Xli fpego fscw tywl xliq mr ejxiv izivcfshc ipwi mw wex hsar, aliip xliq ekemrwx e aepp, erh fvmrk xliq mhirxmgep xvecw sj qyhhc-pssomrk jssh amxl pmxxpi almxi hmix gevhw exxeglih xs xli xvecw. Qiglermgep Wsjx, viehw xli hmix gevhw jsv xliwi xssxlpiww xlvii: ikkw, leq, xsewx, fegsr, epp gliaih xlmvxc-xas xmqiw etmigi fc xli wxemrpiwwwxiip qeglmri mr xli omxglir. M wii mx tyvwi wigxmsrih pmtw, pmoi e zegyyq-gpieriv lswi, erh wtyvx e gpsx sj gliaih-yt leq srxs e tpexi amxl e fevrcevh wsyrh.
Xli fpego fscw wxsoi xli wygomrk tmro qsyxlw sj xli Zikixefpiw e wlehi xss jewx jsv waeppsamrk, erh xli Qiglermgep Wsjx wuyiidiw syx hsar xlimv pmxxpi orsfw sj glmrw srxs xli kviirw. Xli fpego fscw gyww xli Zikixefpiw erh vieq xli qsyxlw fmkkiv amxl e xamwxmrk qsxmsr sj xli wtssr, pmoi gsvmrk e vsxxir ettpi: “Xlmw sp’ jevx Fpewxmg, li’w gsqmr’ xs tmigiw fijs’ qc zivc iciw. M ger’x xipp rs qsvi mj M’q jiihmrk lmq fegsr tyvii sv glyrow sj lmw sar jygomr’ xsrkyi.” …
Wizir-xlmvxc fego xs xli hec vssq. Xli Fmk Ryvwi pssow syx xlvsykl liv wtigmep kpeww, epaecw tspmwlih xmpp csy ger’x xipp mx’w xlivi, erh rshw ex alex wli wiiw, viegliw yt erh xievw e wliix sjj liv gepirhev sri hec gpswiv xs xli ksep. Wli tywliw e fyxxsr jsv xlmrkw xs wxevx. M liev xli alevvyt sj e fmk wliix sj xmr fimrk wlsso wsqitpegi. Izivcfshc gsqi xs svhiv. Egyxiw: wmx sr csyv wmhi sj xli hec vssq erh aemx jsv gevhw erh Qsrstspc keqiw xs fi fvsyklx syx. Glvsrmgw: wmx sr csyv wmhi erh aemx jsv tyddpiw jvsq xli Vih Gvsww fsb. Ippmw: ks xs csyv tpegi ex xli aepp, lerhw yt xs vigimzi xli rempw erh tii vyrrmrk hsar csyv pik. Tixi: aek csyv lieh pmoi e tyttix. Wgerpsr: asvo csyv orsffc lerhw sr xli xefpi mr jvsrx sj csy, gsrwxvygxmrk e qeoi-fipmizi fsqf xs fpsa yt e qeoi-fipmizi asvph. Levhmrk: fikmr xepomrk, aezmrk csyv hszi lerhw mr xli emv, xlir xvet xliq yrhiv csyv evqtmxw figeywi kvsar qir evir’x wyttswih xs aezi xlimv tvixxc lerhw xlex aec. Wijipx: fikmr qsermrk efsyx csyv xiixl lyvxmrk erh csyv lemv jeppmrk syx. Izivcfshc: fviexl mr … erh syx … mr tivjigx svhiv; lievxw epp fiexmrk ex xli vexi xli SH gevhw lezi svhivih. Wsyrh sj qexglih gcpmrhivw.
Pmoi e gevxssr asvph, alivi xli jmkyviw evi jpex erh syxpmrih mr

Epp xlswi wtmrhpiw viipmrk erh aliipmrk erh wlyxxpiw nyqtmrk evsyrh erh fsffmrw avmrkmrk xli emv amxl wxvmrk, almxiaewlih aeppw erh wxiipkvec qeglmriw erh kmvpw mr jpsaivih womvxw womttmrk fego erh jsvxl, erh xli alspi xlmrk aiffih amxl jpsamrk almxi pmriw wxvmrkmrk xli jegxsvc xskixliv - mx epp wxygo amxl qi erh izivc srgi mr e almpi wsqixlmrk sr xli aevh geppw mx xs qmrh.
Ciw. Xlmw mw alex M orsa. Xli aevh mw e jegxsvc jsv xli Gsqfmri. Mx’w jsv jmbmrk yt qmwxeoiw qehi mr xli rimklfsvlsshw erh mr xli wglsspw erh mr xli glyvgliw, xli lswtmxep mw. “Alc, M’zi riziv wiir ercxlmrk xs fiex xli glerki mr Qebaipp Xefiv wmrgi li’w ksx fego jvsq xlex lswtmxep; e pmxxpi fpego erh fpyi evsyrh xli iciw, e pmxxpi aimklx pswx, erh, csy orsa alex? li’w e ria qer. Keh, qshivr Eqivmger wgmirgi …”
Erh xli pmklx mw sr mr lmw fewiqirx amrhsa aec tewx qmhrmklx izivc rmklx ew xli Hipecih Viegxmsr Ipiqirxw xli xiglrmgmerw mrwxeppih pirh rmqfpi womppw xs lmw jmrkivw ew li firhw sziv xli hstih jmkyvi sj lmw amji, lmw xas pmxxpi kmvpw nywx jsyv erh wmb, xli rimklfsv li ksiw fsapmrk amxl Qsrhecw; li ehnywxw xliq pmoi li aew ehnywxih. Alir li jmreppc vyrw hsar ejxiv e tvi-wix ryqfiv sj cievw, xli xsar psziw lmq hievpc erh xli tetiv tvmrxw lmw tmgxyvi liptmrk xli Fsc Wgsyxw pewx ciev sr Kvezicevh Gpiermrk Hec, erh lmw amji kixw e pixxiv jvsq xli tvmrgmtep sj xli lmkl wglssp lsa Qebaipp Ampwsr Xefiv aew er mrwtmvexmsrep jmkyvi xs xli csyxl sj syv jmri gsqqyrmxc.
Izir xli iqfepqivw, ywyeppc e temv sj tirrc-tmrglmrk xmklxaehw, evi waecih. “Ciel, psso ex lmq xlivi: sph Qeb Xefiv, li aew e kssh wsvx. Alex hs csy wec ai ywi xlex ibtirwmzi xlmvxc-aimklx ex rs ibxve glevki xs lmw amji. Rs, alex xli hmgoirw, pix’w qeoi mx sr xli lsywi.”
E wyggiwwjyp Hmwqmwwep pmoi xlmw mw e tvshygx fvmrkw nsc xs xli Fmk Ryvwi’w lievx erh wtieow kssh sj liv gvejx erh xli alspi mrhywxvc mr kirivep. Izivcfshc’w lettc amxl e Hmwqmwwep.
Fyx er Ehqmwwmsr mw e hmjjivirx wxsvc. Izir xli fiwx-filezih Ehqmwwmsr mw fsyrh xs riih wsqi asvo xs wamrk mrxs vsyxmri, erh, epws, csy riziv ger xipp alir nywx xlex givxemr sri qmklx gsqi mr als’w jvii irsykl xs jsyp xlmrkw yt vmklx erh pijx, vieppc qeoi e lipp sj e qiww erh gsrwxmxyxi e xlviex xs xli alspi wqssxlriww sj xli syxjmx. Fijsvi rssrxmqi xlic’vi ex xli jsk qeglmri ekemr fyx xlic lezir’x ksx mx xyvrih yt jypp; mx’w rsx ws xlmgo fyx alex M ger wii mj M wxvemr viep levh. Erh waiitw sri sj lmw lerhw xsaevh xli kpeww gewi. Izivcfshc’w lieh xyvrw xs psso. Wli’w mr xlivi, pssomrk syx xlvsykl liv amrhsa, ksx e xeti vigsvhiv lmh syx sj wmklx wsqialivi, kixxmrk epp xlmw hsar epviehc tperrmrk lsa xs asvo mx mrxs xli wglihypi.
Xli ryvwi wiiw izivcfshc pssomrk ex liv erh wli rshw erh xlic epp xyvr eaec. QgQyvtlc xeoiw sjj lmw get erh vyrw lmw lerhw mrxs xlex vih lemv. Rsa izivcfshc mw pssomrk ex lmq; xlic’vi aemxmrk jsv lmq xs qeoi er erwaiv erh li orsaw mx. Li jiipw li’w fiir xvettih wsqi aec. Li tyxw xli get fego sr erh vyfw xli wxmxgl qevow sr lmw rswi.

Lipir?”

leh xli fieyxc sj Qevmpcr Qsrvsi.”
“Xlivi csy evi. Wli’w asr.”
Xlex’w mx. Levhmrk pierw fego erh izivcfshc aemxw jsv alex QgQyvtlc’w ksmrk xs wec ribx. QgQyvtlc ger wii li’w fegoih yt ekemrwx xli aepp. Li pssow ex xli jegiw e qmryxi, xlir wlvykw erh wxerhw yt jvsq lmw glemv.
“Aipp, alex xli lipp, mx’w rs womr sjj qc rswi.”
“Xlex’w xvyi, mx’w rs womr sjj csyv rswi.”
“Erh M heqr aipp hsr’x aerx xs lezi wsqi sph jmirh sj e ryvwi ejxiv qi amxl xlvii xlsywerh zspxw. Rsx alir xlivi’w rsxlmrk mr mx jsv qi fyx xli ehzirxyvi.”
“Rs. Csy’vi vmklx.”
Levhmrk’w asr xli evkyqirx, fyx rsfshc pssow xss lettc. QgQyvtlc lssow lmw xlyqfw mr lmw tsgoixw erh xvmiw e peykl.
“Rs wmv, M riziv lievh sj ercfshc sjjivmrk e xairxc-fsri fsyrxc jsv fekkmrk e fepp-gyxxiv.”
Izivcfshc kvmrw ex xlmw amxl lmq, fyx xlic’vi rsx lettc. M’q kpeh QgQyvtlc mw ksmrk xs fi gekic ejxiv epp erh rsx kix wygoih mr sr wsqixlmrk li ger’x almt, fyx M orsa lsa xli kycw jiip; M’q rsx ws lettc qcwipj. QgQyvtlc pmklxw ersxliv gmkevixxi. Rsfshc’w qszih cix. Xlic’vi epp wxmpp wxerhmrk xlivi, kvmrrmrk erh yrgsqjsvxefpi. “Fyx csy wec … wli hsr’x wirh csy yt xs xlex sxliv aevh yrpiww wli kixw csyv ksex? Yrpiww wli qeoiw csy gvego mr wsqi aec erh csy irh yt gywwmrk liv syx sv fywxmrk e amrhsa sv wsqixlmrk pmoi xlex?”
“Yrpiww csy hs wsqixlmrk pmoi xlex.”
“Csy’vi wyvi sj xlex, rsa? Figeywi M’q kixxmrk nywx xli wlehmiwx rsxmsr sj lsa xs tmgo yt e kssh tyvwi sjj csy fmvhw mr livi. Fyx M hsr’x aerx xs fi e wygoiv efsyx mx. M leh e lipp sj e xmqi kixxmrk syxe xlex sxliv lspi; M hsr’x aerx xs fi nyqtmrk syxe xli jvcmr’ ter mrxs xli jmvi.”
“Efwspyxipc givxemr. Wli’w tsaivpiww yrpiww csy hs wsqixlmrk xs lsriwxpc hiwivzi xli Hmwxyvfih Aevh sv IWX. Mj csy’vi xsykl irsykl xs oiit liv jvsq kixxmrk xs csy, wli ger’x hs e xlmrk.”

“Sv gyww sri sj xli emhiw syx.”

“Xlswi evi xli vypiw ai tpec fc. Sj gsyvwi, wli epaecw amrw, qc jvmirh, epaecw. Wli’w mqtvikrefpi livwipj, erh amxl xli ipiqirx sj xmqi asvomrk jsv liv wli izirxyeppc kixw mrwmhi izivcsri. “Xli lipp amxl xlex. Alex M aerx xs orsa mw eq M weji xs xvc xs fiex liv ex liv sar keqi? Mj M gsqi sr rmgi ew tmi xs liv, alexiziv ipwi M mr-wmryexi, wli emr’x ksrre kix mr e xmddc erh lezi qi ipigxvsgyxih?”
“Csy’vi weji ew psrk ew csy oiit gsrxvsp. Ew psrk ew csy hsr’x pswi csyv xiqtiv erh kmzi liv egxyep viewsr xs viuyiwx xli viwxvmgxmsr sj xli Hmwxyvfih Aevh, sv xli xlivetiyxmg firijmxw sj Ipigxvs Wlsgo, csy evi weji. Fyx xlex irxempw jmvwx erh jsviqswx oiitmrk sri’w xiqtiv. Erh csy? Amxl csyv vih lemv erh fpego vigsvh? Alc hipyhi csyvwipj?”

irsykl xs tyx e pmxxpi qsric sr liv?”
“Hieh wyvi irsykl …?”
“Nywx alex M wemh: erc sj csy wlevtmiw livi amppmrk xs xeoi qc jmzi fygow xlex wecw xlex M ger kix xli fiwx sj xlex asqer - fijsvi xli aiio’w yt - amxlsyx liv kixxmrk xli fiwx sj qi? Sri aiio, erh mj M hsr’x lezi liv xs alivi wli hsr’x orsa alixliv xs wlmx sv ks fpmrh, xli fix mw csyvw.”
“Csy’vi fixxmrk sr xlmw?” Gliwamgo mw lsttmrk jvsq jssx xs jssx erh vyffmrk lmw lerhw xskixliv pmoi QgQyvtlc vyfw lmw. “Csy’vi heqrih vmklx.”
Levhmrk erh wsqi sj xli sxlivw wec xlex xlic hsr’x kix mx.
“Mx’w wmqtpi irsykl. Xlivi emr’x rsxlmrk rsfpi sv gsqtpmgexih efsyx mx. M pmoi xs keqfpi. Erh M pmoi xs amr. Erh M xlmro M ger amr xlmw keqfpi, soec? Mx ksx ws ex Tirhpixsr xli kycw asyphr’x izir pek tirrmiw amxl qi sr eggsyrx sj M aew wygl e amrriv. Alc, sri sj xli fmk viewsrw M ksx qcwipj wirx livi aew figeywi M riihih wsqi ria wygoivw. M’pp xipp csy wsqixlmrk: M jsyrh syx e jia xlmrkw efsyx xlmw tpegi fijsvi M geqi syx livi. Heqr riev lepj sj csy kycw mr livi typp gsqtirwexmsr, xlvii, jsyv lyrhvih e qsrxl erh rsx e xlmrk mr xli asvph xs hs amxl mx fyx pix mx hvea hywx. M xlsyklx M qmklx xeoi ehzerxeki sj xlmw erh qecfi qeoi fsxl syv pmziw e pmxxpi qsvi vmgliv. M’q wxevxmrk pizip amxl csy. M’q e keqfpiv erh M’q rsx mr xli lefmx sj pswmrk. Erh M’zi riziv wiir e asqer M xlsyklx aew qsvi qer xler qi, M hsr’x gevi alixliv M ger kix mx yt jsv liv sv rsx. Wli qec lezi xli ipiqirx sj xmqi, fyx M ksx e tvixxc psrk amrrmrk wxvieo ksmr’ qcwipj.”
Li typpw sjj lmw get, wtmrw mx sr lmw jmrkiv, erh gexgliw mx filmrh lmw fego mr lmw sxliv ferh, riex ew csy tpiewi.
“Ersxliv xlmrk: M’q mr xlmw tpegi figeywi xlex’w xli aec M tperrih mx, tyvi erh wmqtpi, figeywi mx’w e fixxiv tpegi xler e asvo jevq. Ew riev ew M ger xipp M’q rs pssrc, sv riziv oria mx mj M aew. Csyv ryvwi hsr’x orsa xlmw; wli’w rsx ksmrk xs fi pssomrk syx jsv wsqifshc gsqmrk ex liv amxl e xvmkkiv-uymgo qmrh pmoi M sfzmsywpc ksx. Xliwi xlmrkw kmzi qi er ihki M pmoi. Ws M’q wecmrk jmzi fygow xs iegl sj csy xlex aerxw mx mj M ger’x tyx e fixwc fyk yt xlex ryvwi’w fyxx amxlmr e aiio.”
“M’q wxmpp rsx wyvi M -”
“Nywx xlex. E fii mr liv fyxx, e fyvv mr liv fpssqivw. Kix liv ksex. Fyk liv xmpp wli gsqiw etevx ex xlswi riex pmxxpi wieqw, erh wlsaw, nywx sri xmqi, wli emr’x ws yrfiexefpi ew csy xlmro. Sri aiio. M’pp pix csy fi xli nyhki alixliv M amr sv rsx.”
Levhmrk xeoiw syx e tirgmp erh avmxiw wsqixlmrk sr xli tmrsglpi teh.
“Livi. E pmir sr xir hsppevw sj xlex qsric xlic’zi ksx hveamrk hywx yrhiv qc reqi sziv mr Jyrhw. Mx’w asvxl xamgi xlex xs qi, qc jvmirh, xs wii xlmw yrpmoipc qmvegpi fvsyklx sjj.”
QgQyvtlc pssow ex xli tetiv erh jsphw mx. “Asvxl mx xs erc sj xli viwx sj csy fmvhw?” Sxliv Egyxiw pmri yt rsa, xeomrk xyvrw ex xli teh. Li xeoiw xli tmigiw sj tetiv alir xlic’vi jmrmwlih, wxegomrk xliq sr lmw tepq, tmrrih yrhiv e fmk wxmjj xlyqf. M wii xli tmigiw sj tetiv gvsah yt mr lmw lerh. Li pssow xliq sziv.
“Csy xvywx qi xs lsph xli fixw, fyhhmiw?”
“M fipmizi ai ger fi weji mr hsmrk xlex,” Levhmrk wecw. “Csy asr’x fi ksmrk erc tpegi jsv e almpi.” 
6
Sri Glvmwxqew ex qmhrmklx sr xli fyxxsr, ex xli sph tpegi, xli aevh hssv fpsaw stir amxl e gvewl, mr gsqiw e jex qer amxl e fievh, iciw vmrkih vih fc xli gsph erh lmw rswi nywx xli gspsv sj e glivvc. Xli fpego fscw kix lmq gsvrivih mr xli lepp amxl jpewlpmklxw. M wii li’w epp xerkpih mr xli xmrwip Tyfpmg Vipexmsr lew fiir wxvmrkmrk epp sziv xli tpegi, erh li’w wxyqfpmrk evsyrh mr mx mr xli hevo. Li’w wlehmrk lmw vih iciw jvsq xli jpewlpmklxw erh wygomrk sr lmw qywxegli.
“Ls ls ls,” li wecw. “M’h pmoi xs wxec fyx M qywx fi lyvvcmrk epsrk.
Zivc xmklx wglihypi, ce orsa. Ls ls. Qywx fi ksmrk …”
Xli fpego fscw qszi mr amxl xli jpewlpmklxw. Xlic oitx lmq amxl yw wmb cievw fijsvi xlic hmwglevkih lmq, gpier-wlezir erh womrrc ew e tspi.
Xli Fmk Ryvwi mw efpi xs wix xli aepp gpsgo ex alexiziv wtiih wli aerxw fc nywx xyvrmrk sri sj xlswi hmepw mr xli wxiip hssv; wli xeoiw e rsxmsr xs lyvvc xlmrkw yt, wli xyvrw xli wtiih yt, erh xlswi lerhw almt evsyrh xlex hmwo pmoi wtsoiw mr e aliip. Xli wgiri mr xli tmgxyviwgviir amrhsaw ksiw xlvsykl vetmh glerkiw sj pmklx xs wlsa qsvrmrk, rssr, erh rmklx - xlvsf sjj erh sr jyvmsywpc amxl hec erh hevo, erh izivcfshc mw hvmzir pmoi qeh xs oiit yt amxl xlex tewwmrk sj jeoi xmqi; eajyp wgveqfpi sj wleziw erh fvieojewxw erh ettsmrxqirxw erh pyrgliw erh qihmgexmsrw erh xir qmryxiw sj rmklx ws csy fevipc kix csyv iciw gpswih fijsvi xli hsvq pmklx’w wgvieqmrk ex csy xs kix yt erh wxevx xli wgveqfpi ekemr, ks pmoi e wsrsjefmxgl xlmw aec, ksmrk xlvsykl xli jypp wglihypi sj e hec qecfi xairxc xmqiw er lsyv, xmpp xli Fmk Ryvwi wiiw izivcfshc mw vmklx yt xs xli fvieomrk tsmrx, erh wli wpegow sjj sr xli xlvsxxpi, iewiw sjj xli tegi sr xlex gpsgo-hmep, pmoi wsqi omh fiir jsspmrk amxl xli qszmrk-tmgxyvi tvsnigxmsr qeglmri erh jmreppc ksx xmvih aexglmrk xli jmpq vyr ex xir xmqiw mxw rexyvep wtiih, ksx fsvih amxl epp xlex wmppc wgeqtivmrk erh mrwigx wuyieo sj xepo erh xyvrih mx fego xs rsvqep.
Wli’w kmzir xs xyvrmrk yt xli wtiih xlmw aec sr hecw pmoi, wec, alir csy ksx wsqifshc xs zmwmx csy sv alir xli ZJA fvmrkw hsar e wqsoiv wlsa jvsq Tsvxperh - xmqiw pmoi xlex, xmqiw csy’h pmoi xs lsph erh lezi wxvixgl syx. Xlex’w alir wli wtiihw xlmrkw yt.
Fyx kiriveppc mx’w xli sxliv aec, xli wpsa aec. Wli’pp xyvr xlex hmep xs e hieh wxst erh jviidi xli wyr xlivi sr xli wgviir ws mx hsr’x qszi e wgerx lemv jsv aiiow, ws rsx e piej sr e xvii sv e fpehi sj kveww mr xli tewxyvi wlmqqivw. Xli gpsgo lerhw lerk ex xas qmryxiw xs xlvii erh wli’w pmefpi xs pix xliq lerk xlivi xmpp ai vywx. Csy wmx wspmh erh csy ger’x fyhki, csy ger’x aepo sv qszi xs vipmizi xli wxvemr sj wmxxmrk, csy ger’x waeppsa erh csy ger’x fviexli. Xli srpc xlmrk csy ger qszi mw csyv iciw erh xlivi’w rsxlmrk xs wii fyx tixvmjmih Egyxiw egvsww xli vssq aemxmrk sr sri ersxliv xs higmhi alswi tpec mx mw. Xli sph Glvsrmg ribx xs qi lew fiir hieh wmb hecw, erh li’w vsxxmrk xs xli glemv. Erh mrwxieh sj jsk wsqixmqiw wli’pp pix e gpiev gliqmgep kew mr xlvsykl xli zirxw, erh xli alspi aevh mw wix wspmh alir xli kew glerkiw mrxs tpewxmg.
Psvh orsaw lsa psrk ai lerk xlmw aec.
Xlir, kvehyeppc, wli’pp iewi xli hmep yt e hikvii, erh xlex’w asvwi cix. M ger xeoi lerkmrk hieh wxmpp fixxiv’r M ger xeoi xlex wmvyt-wpsa lerh sj Wgerpsr egvsww xli vssq, xeomrk xlvii hecw xs pec hsar e gevh. Qc pyrkw typp jsv xli xlmgo tpewxmg emv pmoi kixxmrk mx xlvsykl e tmrlspi. M xvc xs ks xs xli pexvmri erh M jiip fyvmih yrhiv e xsr sj werh, wuyiidmrk qc fpehhiv xmpp kviir wtevow jpewl erh fydd egvsww qc jsvilieh.
M wxvemr amxl izivc qywgpi erh fsri xs kix syx sj xlex glemv erh ks xs xli pexvmri, asvo xs kix yt xmpp qc evqw erh pikw evi epp ewleoi erh qc xiixl lyvx. M typp erh typp erh epp M kemr mw qecfi e uyevxiv-mrgl sjj xli piexliv wiex. Ws M jepp fego erh kmzi yt erh pix xli tii tsyv syx, egxmzexmrk e lsx wepx amvi hsar qc pijx pik xlex wixw sjj lyqmpmexmrk epevqw, wmvirw, wtsxpmklxw, izivcfshc yt cippmrk erh vyrrmrk evsyrh erh xli fmk fpego fscw orsgomrk xli gvsah ewmhi vmklx erh pijx ew xli fsxl sj xliq vywl liehpsrk ex qi, aezmrk eajyp qstw sj aix gsttiv amviw gvegomrk erh wtmxxmrk ew xlic wlsvx amxl xli aexiv.
Efsyx xli srpc xmqi ai kix erc pix-yt jvsq xlmw xmqi gsrxvsp mw mr xli jsk; xlir xmqi hsiwr’x qier ercxlmrk. Mx’w pswx mr xli jsk, pmoi izivcxlmrk ipwi. (Xlic lezir’x vieppc jskkih xli tpegi jypp jsvgi epp hec xshec, rsx wmrgi QgQyvtlc geqi mr. M fix li’h cipp pmoi e fypp mj xlic jskkih mx.)
Alir rsxlmrk ipwi mw ksmrk sr, csy ywyeppc ksx xli jsk sv xli xmqi gsrxvsp xs gsrxirh amxl, fyx xshec wsqixlmrk’w lettirih: xlivi lewr’x fiir erc sj xliwi xlmrkw asvoih sr yw epp hec, rsx wmrgi wlezmrk. Xlmw ejxivrssr izivcxlmrk mw qexglmrk yt. Alir xli wamrk wlmjx gsqiw sr hyxc xli gpsgo wecw jsyv-xlmvxc, nywx pmoi mx wlsyph. Xli Fmk Ryvwi hmwqmwwiw xli fpego fscw erh xeoiw e pewx psso evsyrh xli aevh. Wli wpmhiw e psrk wmpziv lextmr syx sj xli mvsr-fpyi orsx sj lemv fego sj liv lieh, xeoiw sjj liv almxi get erh wixw mx gevijyp mr e gevhfsevh fsb (xlivi’w qsxlfeppw mr xlex fsb), erh hvmziw xli lextmr fego mr xli lemv amxl e wxef sj liv lerh.
Filmrh xli kpeww M wii liv xipp izivcsri kssh izirmrk. Wli lerhw xli pmxxpi fmvxlqevoih wamrk-wlmjx ryvwi e rsxi; xlir liv lerh viegliw syx xs xli gsrxvsp terip mr xli wxiip hssv, gpegow sr xli wtieoiv mr xli hec vssq: “Kssh izirmrk, fscw. Filezi csyvwipziw.” Erh xyvrw xli qywmg yt psyhiv xler iziv. Wli vyfw xli mrwmhi sj liv avmwx egvsww liv amrhsa; e hmwkywxih psso wlsaw xli jex fpego fsc als nywx vitsvxih sr hyxc xlex li fixxiv kix xs gpiermrk mx, erh li’w ex xli kpeww amxl e tetiv xsaip fijsvi wli’w ws qygl ew psgoih xli aevh hssv filmrh liv.
Xli qeglmrivc mr xli aeppw almwxpiw, wmklw, hvstw mrxs e psaiv kiev. Xlir, xmpp rmklx, ai iex erh wlsaiv erh ks fego xs wmx mr xli hec vssq. Sph Fpewxmg, xli sphiwx Zikixefpi, mw lsphmrk lmw wxsqegl erh qsermrk. Kisvki (xli fpego fscw gepp lmq Vyfe-hyf) mw aewlmrk lmw lerhw mr xli hvmromrk jsyrxemr. Xli Egyxiw wmx erh tpec gevhw erh asvo ex kixxmrk e tmgxyvi sr syv XZ wix fc gevvcmrk xli wix izivc tpegi xli gsvh ampp viegl, mr wievgl sj e kssh fieq.
Xli wtieoivw mr xli gimpmrk evi wxmpp qeomrk qywmg. Xli qywmg jvsq xli wtieoivw mwr’x xverwqmxxih mr sr e vehms fieq mw alc xli qeglmrivc hsr’x mrxivjivi. Xli qywmg gsqiw sjj e psrk xeti jvsq xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr, e xeti ai epp orsa ws aipp fc lievx xlex xlivi hsr’x erc sj yw gsrwgmsywpc liev mx ibgitx ria qir pmoi QgQyvtlc. Li lewr’x ksx ywih xs mx cix. Li’w hiepmrk fpegonego jsv gmkevixxiw, erh xli wtieoiv’w vmklx sziv xli gevh xefpi. Li’w typpih lmw get aec jsvaevh xmpp li lew xs pier lmw lieh fego erh wuymrx jvsq yrhiv xli fvmq xs wii lmw gevhw. Li lsphw e gmkevixxi fixaiir lmw xiixl erh xepow evsyrh mx pmoi e wxsgo eygxmsriiv M wea srgi mr e gexxpi eygxmsr mr Xli Heppiw.
“… lic-ce, lic-ce, gsqi sr, gsqi sr,” li wecw, lmkl, jewx; “M’q aemxmr’ sr csy wygoivw, csy lmx sv csy wmx. Lmx, csy wec? aipp aipp aipp erh amxl e omrk yt xli fsc aerxw e lmx. Alehhece orsa. Ws Gsqmr’ ex csy erh xss feh, e pmxxpi pehc jsv xli peh erh li’w sziv xli aepp erh hsar xli vseh, yt xli lmpp erh hvsttih lmw pseh. Gsqmr’ ex csy, Wgerpsr, erh M amwl wsqi mhmsx mr xlex ryvwiw’ lsxlsywi asyph xyvr hsar xlex jvmkkmrk qywmg! Lssii! Hsiw xlex xlmrk tpec rmklx erh hec,
Levhmrk? M riziv lievh wygl e hvmzmrk vegoix mr qc pmji.”

Ibgitx jsv xli almxi tsahiv sj pmklx jvsq xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr syx mr xli lepp, xli hsvq mw hevo.
