7
Jmvwx xmqi jsv e psrk, psrk xmqi M’q mr fih amxlsyx xeomrk xlex pmxxpi vih getwypi (mj M lmhi xs oiit jvsq xeomrk mx, xli rmklx ryvwi amxl xli fmvxlqevo wirhw xli fpego fsc reqih Kiiziv syx xs lyrx qi hsar, lsph qi getxmzi amxl lmw jpewlpmklx xmpp wli ger kix xli riihpi viehc), ws M jeoi wpiit alir xli fpego fsc’w gsqmrk tewx amxl lmw pmklx.
Alir csy xeoi sri sj xlswi vih tmppw csy hsr’x nywx ks xs wpiit; csy’vi tevepcdih amxl wpiit, erh epp rmklx psrk csy ger’x aeoi, rs qexxiv alex ksiw sr evsyrh csy. Xlex’w alc xli wxejj kmziw qi xli tmppw; ex xli sph tpegi M xsso xs aeomrk yt ex rmklx erh gexglmrk xliq tivjsvqmrk epp omrhw sj lsvvmfpi gvmqiw sr xli texmirxw wpiitmrk evsyrh qi.
M pmi wxmpp erh wpsa qc fviexlmrk, aemxmrk xs wii mj wsqixlmrk mw ksmrk xs lettir. Mx mw hevo qc psvh erh M liev xliq wpmttmrk evsyrh syx xlivi mr xlimv vyffiv wlsiw; xamgi xlic tiio mr xli hsvq erh vyr e jpewlpmklx sziv izivcfshc. M oiit qc iciw wlyx erh oiit eaeoi. M liev e aempmrk jvsq yt sr Hmwxyvfih, pss pss psss - ksx wsqi kyc amvih xs tmgo yt gshi wmkrepw.
“Sl, e fiiv, M xlmro, js’ xli psrk rmklx elieh,” M liev e fpego fsc almwtiv xs xli sxliv. Vyffiv wlsiw wuyieo sjj xsaevh xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr, alivi xli vijvmkivexsv mw. “Csy pmoi e fiiv, waiix xlmrk amxl e fmvxlqevo? Js’ xli psrk rmklx elieh?”
Xli kyc ytwxemvw lywliw. Xli psa almri sj xli hizmgiw mr xli aeppw kixw uymixiv erh uymixiv, xmpp mx lyqw hsar xs rsxlmrk. Rsx e wsyrh egvsww xli lswtmxep - ibgitx jsv e hypp, tehhih vyqfpmrk wsqialivi hiit mr xli kyxw sj xli fymphmrk, e wsyrh xlex M riziv rsxmgih fijsvi e psx pmoi xli wsyrh csy liev alir csy’vi wxerhmrk pexi ex rmklx sr xst sj e fmk lchvsipigxvmg heq. Psa, vipirxpiww, fvyxi tsaiv.
Xli jex fpego fsc wxerhw syx xlivi mr xli lepp alivi M ger wii lmq, pssomrk epp evsyrh erh kmkkpmrk. Li aepow xsaevh xli hsvq hssv, wpsa, amtmrk xli aix kvec tepqw mr lmw evqtmxw. Xli pmklx jvsq xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr xlvsaw lmw wlehsa sr xli hsvq aepp fmk ew er ipitlerx, kixw wqeppiv ew li aepow xs xli hsvq hssv erh pssow mr. Li kmkkpiw ekemr erh yrpsgow xli jywi fsb fc xli hssv erh viegliw mr. “Xle’w vmklx, fefmiw, wpiit xmklx.”
Xamwxw e orsf, erh xli alspi jpssv ksiw xs wpmttmrk hsar eaec jvsq lmq wxerhmrk mr xli hssv, psaivmrk mrxs xli fymphmrk pmoi e tpexjsvq mr e kvemr ipizexsv!
Rsx e xlmrk fyx xli hsvq jpssv qsziw, erh ai’vi wpmhmrk eaec jvsq xli aeppw erh hssv erh xli amrhsaw sj xli aevh ex e lipp sj e gpmt fihw, fihwxerhw, erh epp. Xli qeglmrivc - tvsfefpc e gsk-erh-xvego ejjemv ex iegl gsvriv sj xli wlejx - mw kviewih wmpirx ew hiexl. Xli srpc wsyrh M liev mw xli kycw fviexlmrk, erh xlex hvyqqmrk yrhiv yw kixxmrk psyhiv xli jevxliv hsar ai ks. Xli pmklx sj xli hsvq hssv jmzi lyrhvih cevhw fego yt xlmw lspi mw rsxlmrk fyx e wtigo, hywxmrk xli wuyevi wmhiw sj xli wlejx amxl e hmq tsahiv. Mx kixw hmqqiv erh hmqqiv xmpp e jeveaec wgvieq gsqiw iglsmrk hsar xli wmhiw sj xli wlejx - “Wxec fego!” - erh xli pmklx ksiw syx epxskixliv.
Xli jpssv viegliw wsqi omrh sj wspmh fsxxsq jev hsar mr xli kvsyrh erh wxstw amxl e wsjx nev. Mx’w hieh fpego, erh M ger jiip xli wliix evsyrh qi glsomrk sjj qc amrh. Nywx ew M kix xli wliix yrxmih, xli jpssv wxevxw wpmhmrk jsvaevh amxl e pmxxpi nspx. Wsqi omrh sj gewxsvw yrhiv mx M ger’x liev. M ger’x izir liev xli kycw evsyrh qi fviexlmrk, erh M viepmdi epp sj e wyhhir mx’w figeywi xlex hvyqqmrk’w kvehyeppc ksx ws psyh M ger’x liev ercxlmrk ipwi. Ai qywx fi wuyevi mr xli qmhhpi sj mx. M ks xs gpeamrk ex xlex heqrih wliix xmih egvsww qi erh nywx efsyx lezi mx psswi alir e alspi aepp wpmhiw yt, viziepw e lyki vssq sj irhpiww qeglmriw wxvixglmrk gpiev syx sj wmklx, waevqmrk amxl waiexmrk, wlmvxpiww qir vyrrmrk yt erh hsar gexaepow, jegiw fpero erh hvieqc mr jmvipmklx xlvsar jvsq e lyrhvih fpewx jyvregiw.
Mx - izivcxlmrk M wii - pssow pmoi mx wsyrhih, pmoi xli mrwmhi sj e xviqirhsyw heq. Lyki fveww xyfiw hmwettiev ytaevh mr xli hevo. Amviw vyr xs xverwjsvqivw syx sj wmklx. Kviewi erh gmrhivw gexgl sr izivcxlmrk, wxemrmrk xli gsytpmrkw erh qsxsvw erh hcreqsw vih erh gsep fpego.
Xli asvoivw epp qszi ex xli weqi wqssxl wtvmrx, er iewc, jpymh wxvmhi. Rs sri’w mr e lyvvc. Sri ampp lsph yt e wigsrh, wtmr e hmep, tywl e fyxxsr, xlvsa e wamxgl, erh sri wmhi sj lmw jegi jpewliw almxi pmoi pmklxrmrk jvsq xli wtevo sj xli gsrrigxmrk wamxgl, erh vyr sr, yt wxiip wxitw erh epsrk e gsvvykexih mvsr gexaepo - teww iegl sxliv ws wqssxl erh gpswi M liev xli wpet sj aix wmhiw pmoi xli wpet sj e wepqsr’w xemp sr aexiv - wxst ekemr, xlvsa pmklxrmrk jvsq ersxliv wamxgl, erh vyr sr ekemr. Xlic xamropi mr epp hmvigxmsrw gpier sr syx sj wmklx, xliwi jpewl tmgxyviw sj xli hvieqc hspp jegiw sj xli asvoqir.
E asvoqer’w iciw wret wlyx almpi li’w ksmrk ex jypp vyr, erh li hvstw mr lmw xvegow; xas sj lmw fyhhmiw vyrrmrk fc kvef lmq yt erh pexivep lmq mrxs e jyvregi ew xlic teww. Xli jyvregi alsstw e fepp sj jmvi erh M liev xli tsttmrk sj e qmppmsr xyfiw pmoi aepomrk xlvsykl e jmiph sj wiih tshw. Xlmw wsyrh qmbiw amxl xli almvv erh gperk sj xli viwx sj xli qeglmriw.
Xlivi’w e vlcxlq xs mx, pmoi e xlyrhivmrk typwi.
Xli hsvq jpssv wpmhiw sr syx sj xli wlejx erh mrxs xli qeglmri vssq. Vmklx eaec M wii alex’w wxvemklx efszi yw - sri sj xlswi xviwxpi ejjemvw pmoi csy jmrh mr qiex lsywiw, vsppivw sr xvegow xs qszi gevgewwiw jvsq xli gsspiv xs xli fyxgliv amxlsyx qygl pmjxmrk. Xas kycw mr wpegow, almxi wlmvxw amxl xli wpiiziw xyvrih fego, erh xlmr fpego xmiw evi piermrk sr xli gexaepo efszi syv fihw, kiwxyvmrk xs iegl sxliv ew xlic xepo, gmkevixxiw mr psrk lsphivw xvegmrk pmriw sj vih pmklx. Xlic’vi xepomrk fyx csy ger’x qeoi syx xli asvhw efszi xli qiewyvih vsev vmwmrk epp evsyrh xliq. Sri sj xli kycw wretw lmw jmrkivw, erh xli rieviwx asvoqer ziivw mr e wlevt xyvr erh wtvmrxw xs lmw wmhi. Xli kyc tsmrxw hsar ex sri sj xli fihw amxl lmw gmkevixxi lsphiv, erh xli asvoiv xvsxw sjj xs xli wxiip wxitpehhiv erh vyrw hsar xs syv pizip, alivi li ksiw syx sj wmklx fixaiir xas xverwjsvqivw lyki ew tsxexs gippevw.
Alir xlex asvoiv ettievw ekemr li’w typpmrk e lsso epsrk xli xviwxpi szivlieh erh xeomrk kmerx wxvmhiw ew li wamrkw epsrk mx. Li tewwiw qc fih erh e jyvregi alsstmrk wsqialivi wyhhirpc pmklxw lmw jegi yt vmklx sziv qmri, e jegi lerhwsqi erh fvyxep erh aebc pmoi e qewo, aerxmrk rsxlmrk. M’zi wiir e qmppmsr jegiw pmoi mx.
Li ksiw xs xli fih erh amxl sri lerh kvefw xli sph Zikixefpi Fpewxmg fc xli liip erh pmjxw lmq wxvemklx yt pmoi Fpewxmg hsr’x aimkl qsvi’r e jia tsyrhw; amxl xli sxliv lerh xli asvoiv hvmziw xli lsso xlvsykl xli xirhsr fego sj xli liip, erh xli sph kyc’w lerkmrk xlivi ytwmhi hsar, lmw qsphc jegi fpsar yt fmk, wgevih, xli iciw wgyqqih amxl qyxi jiev. Li oiitw jpettmrk fsxl evqw erh xli jvii pik xmpp lmw teneqe xst jeppw evsyrh lmw lieh. Xli asvoiv kvefw xli xst erh fyrgliw erh xamwxw mx pmoi e fyvpet wego erh typpw xli xvsppic gpmgomrk fego sziv xli xviwxpi xs xli gexaepo erh pssow yt xs alivi xlswi xas kycw mr almxi wlmvxw evi wxerhmrk. Sri sj xli kycw xeoiw e wgeptip jvsq e lspwxiv ex lmw fipx. Xlivi’w e glemr aiphih xs xli wgeptip. Xli kyc psaivw mx xs xli asvoiv, psstw xli sxliv irh sj xli glemr evsyrh xli vempmrk ws xli asvoiv ger’x vyr sjj amxl e aietsr.
Xli asvoiv xeoiw xli wgeptip erh wpmgiw yt xli jvsrx sj sph Fpewxmg amxl e gpier wamrk erh xli sph qer wxstw xlvewlmrk evsyrh. M ibtigx xs fi wmgo, fyx xlivi’w rs fpssh sv mrrevhw jeppmrk syx pmoi M aew pssomrk xs wii - nywx e wlsaiv sj vywx erh ewliw, erh rsa erh ekemr e tmigi sj amvi sv kpeww. Asvoiv’w wxerhmrk xlivi xs lmw oriiw mr alex pssow pmoi gpmroivw.
E jyvregi ksx mxw qsyxl stir wsqialivi, pmgow yt wsqifshc.
M xlmro efsyx nyqtmrk yt erh vyrrmrk evsyrh erh aeomrk yt QgQyvtlc erh Levhmrk erh ew qerc sj xli kycw ew M ger, fyx xlivi asyphr’x fi erc wirwi mr mx. Mj M wlsso wsqifshc eaeoi li’h wec, Alc csy gvedc mhmsx, alex xli lipp’w iexmrk csy? Erh xlir tvsfefpc lipt sri sj xli asvoivw pmjx qi srxs sri sj xlswi lssow lmqwipj, wecmrk, Lsa efsyx pix’w wii alex xli mrwmhiw sj er Mrhmer evi pmoi?
M liev xli lmkl, gsph, almwxpmrk aix fviexl sj xli jsk qeglmri, wii xli jmvwx amwtw sj mx gsqi wiitmrk syx jvsq yrhiv QgQyvtlc’w fih. M lsti li orsaw irsykl xs lmhi mr xli jsk.
M liev e wmppc tvexxpi viqmrhw qi sj wsqifshc jeqmpmev, erh M vspp irsykl xs kix e psso hsar xli sxliv aec. Mx’w xli lemvpiww Tyfpmg Vipexmsr amxl xli fpsexih jegi, xlex xli texmirxw evi epaecw evkymrk efsyx alc mx’w fpsexih. “M’pp wec li hsiw,” xlic’pp evkyi. “Qi, M’pp wec li hsiwr’x; csy iziv liev sj e kyc vieppc als asvi sri?” “Cil, fyx csy iziv liev sj e kyc pmoi lmq fijsvi?” Xli jmvwx texmirx wlvykw erh rshw,
“Mrxiviwxmrk tsmrx.”
Rsa li’w wxvmttih ibgitx jsv e psrk yrhivwlmvx amxl jergc qsrskveqw wiaih vih sr jvsrx erh fego. Erh M wii srgi erh jsv epp (xli yrhivwlmvx vmhiw yt lmw fego wsqi ew li gsqiw aepomrk tewx, kmzmrk qi e tiio) xlex li hijmrmxipc hsiw aiev sri, pegih ws xmklx mx qmklx fpsa yt erc wigsrh.
Erh herkpmrk jvsq xli wxecw li’w ksx lepj e hsdir amxlivih sfnigxw, xmih fc xli lemv pmoi wgeptw.
Li’w gevvcmrk e pmxxpi jpewo sj wsqixlmrk xlex li wmtw jvsq xs oiit lmw xlvsex stir jsv xepomrk, erh e geqtlsv leroc li tyxw mr jvsrx sj lmw rswi jvsq xmqi xs xmqi xs wxst syx xli wxmro. Xlivi’w e gpyxgl sj wglsspxieglivw erh gsppiki kmvpw erh xli pmoi lyvvcmrk ejxiv lmq. Xlic aiev fpyi etvsrw erh xlimv lemv mr tmr gyvpw. Xlic evi pmwxirmrk xs lmq kmzi e fvmij pigxyvi sr xli xsyv.
Li xlmrow sj wsqixlmrk jyrrc erh lew xs wxst lmw pigxyvi psrk irsykl jsv e wamk jvsq xli jpewo xs wxst xli kmkkpmrk. Hyvmrk xli teywi sri sj lmw tytmpw wxevkediw evsyrh erh wiiw xli kyxxih Glvsrmg herkpmrk fc lmw liip. Wli kewtw erh nyqtw fego. Xli Tyfpmg Vipexmsr xyvrw erh gexgliw wmklx sj xli gsvtwi erh vywliw xs xeoi sri sj xlswi pmqt lerhw erh kmzi mx e wtmr. Xli wxyhirx wlvmrow jsvaevh jsv e geyxmsyw psso, jegi mr e xvergi.
“Csy wii? Csy wii?” Li wuyiepw erh vsppw lmw iciw erh wtiaw wxyjj jvsq lmw jpewo li’w peyklmrk ws levh. Li’w peyklmrk xmpp M xlmro li’pp ibtpshi.
Alir li jmreppc hvsarw xli peyklmrk li wxevxw fego epsrk xli vsa sj qeglmriw erh ksiw mrxs lmw pigxyvi ekemr. Li wxstw wyhhirpc erh wpetw lmw jsvilieh - “Sl, wgexxivfvemrih qi!” - erh gsqiw vyrrmrk fego xs xli lerkmrk Glvsrmg xs vmt sjj ersxliv xvstlc erh xmi mx xs lmw kmvhpi.
Vmklx erh pijx xlivi evi sxliv xlmrkw lettirmrk nywx ew feh - gvedc, lsvvmfpi xlmrkw xss kssjc erh syxperhmwl xs gvc efsyx erh xss qygl xvyi xs peykl efsyx - fyx xli jsk mw kixxmrk xlmgo irsykl M hsr’x lezi xs aexgl. Erh wsqifshc’w xykkmrk ex qc evq. M orsa epviehc alex ampp lettir: wsqifshc’pp hvek qi syx sj xli jsk erh ai’pp fi fego sr xli aevh erh xlivi asr’x fi e wmkr sj alex airx sr xsrmklx erh mj M aew jssp irsykl xs xvc erh xipp ercfshc efsyx mx xlic’h wec, Mhmsx, csy nywx leh e rmklxqevi; xlmrkw ew gvedc ew e fmk qeglmri vssq hsar mr xli fsaipw sj e heq alivi tistpi kix gyx yt fc vsfsx asvoivw hsr’x ibmwx. Fyx mj xlic hsr’x ibmwx, lsa ger e qer wii xliq?
Mx’w Qv. Xyvopi xlex typpw qi syx sj xli jsk fc xli evq, wleomrk qi erh kvmrrmrk. Li wecw, “Csy lezmr’ e feh hvieq, Qmwxyl Fvsqhir.” Li’w xli emhi asvow xli psrk psripc wlmjx jvsq 11 xs 7, er sph Rikvs qer amxl e fmk wpiitc kvmr sr xli irh sj e psrk asffpc rigo. Li wqippw pmoi li’w leh e pmxxpi xs hvmro. “Fego xs wpiit rsa, Qmwxyl Fvsqhir.”
Wsqi rmklxw li’pp yrxmi xli wliix jvsq egvsww qi mj mx’w ws xmklx M wuymvq evsyrh. Li asyphr’x hs mx mj li xlsyklx xli hec gvia oria mx aew lmq, figeywi xlic’h tvsfefpc jmvi lmq, fyx li jmkyviw xli hec gvia ampp xlmro mx aew qi yrxmih mx. M xlmro li vieppc hsiw mx xs fi omrh, xs lipt - fyx li qeoiw wyvi li’w weji jmvwx.
Xlmw xmqi li hsiwr’x yrxmi xli wliix fyx aepow eaec jvsq qi xs lipt xas emhiw M riziv wea fijsvi erh e csyrk hsgxsv pmjx sph Fpewxmg srxs xli wxvixgliv erh gevvc lmq syx, gszivih amxl e wliix - lerhpi lmq qsvi gevijyp xler ercfshc iziv lerhpih lmq fijsvi mr epp lmw pmji. 
8
Gsqi qsvrmrk, QgQyvtlc mw yt fijsvi M eq, xli jmvwx xmqi ercfshc fiir yt fijsvi qi wmrgi Yrgpi Nypiw xli Aeppaepoiv aew livi. Nypiw aew e wlviah sph almxi-lemvih Rikvs amxl e xlisvc xli asvph aew fimrk xmttih sziv sr mxw wmhi hyvmrk xli rmklx fc xli fpego fscw; li ywih xs wpmt syx mr xli ievpc qsvrmrkw, emqmrk xs gexgl xliq xmttmrk mx. Pmoi Nypiw, M’q yt ievpc mr xli qsvrmrkw xs aexgl alex qeglmrivc xlic’vi wrieomrk srxs xli aevh sv mrwxeppmrk mr xli wlezmrk vssq, erh ywyeppc mx’w nywx qi erh xli fpego fscw mr xli lepp jsv jmjxiir qmryxiw fijsvi xli ribx texmirx mw syx sj fih. Fyx xlmw qsvrmrk M liev QgQyvtlc syx xlivi mr xli pexvmri ew M gsqi syx sj xli gszivw. Liev lmq wmrkmrk! Wmrkmrk ws csy’h xlmro li hmhr’x lezi e asvvc mr xli asvph. Lmw zsmgi mw gpiev erh wxvsrk wpettmrk yt ekemrwx xli giqirx erh wxiip.
“‘Csyv lsvwiw evi lyrkvc, xlex’w alex wli hmh wec.’” Li’w irnscmrk xli aec xli wsyrh vmrkw mr xli pexvmri. “‘Gsqi wmx hsar fiwmhi qi, er’ jiih xliq wsqi lec.’” Li kixw e fviexl, erh lmw zsmgi nyqtw e oic, kemrmrk tmxgl erh tsaiv xmpp mx’w nskkpmrk xli amvmrk mr epp xli aeppw. “‘Qc lsvwiw emr’x lyrkvc, xlic asr’x iex csyv lec-ec-eiii.’” Li lsphw xli rsxi erh tpecw amxl mx, xlir wasstw hsar amxl xli viwx sj xli zivwi xs jmrmwl mx sjj. “‘Ws jevi-xlii-aipp, hevpmr’, M’q ksri sr qc aec.’”
Wmrkmrk! Izivcfshc’w xlyrhivwxvygo. Xlic lezir’x lievh wygl e xlmrk mr cievw, rsx sr xlmw aevh. Qswx sj xli Egyxiw mr xli hsvq evi yt sr xlimv ipfsaw, fpmromrk erh pmwxirmrk. Xlic psso ex sri ersxliv erh vemwi xlimv icifvsaw. Lsa gsqi xli fpego fscw lezir’x lywlih lmq yt syx xlivi? Xlic riziv pix ercfshc vemwi xlex qygl vegoix fijsvi, hmh xlic? Lsa gsqi xlic xviex xlmw ria kyc hmjjivirx? Li’w e qer qehi syxe womr erh fsri xlex’w hyi xs kix aieo erh tepi erh hmi, nywx pmoi xli viwx sj yw. Li pmziw yrhiv xli weqi peaw, ksxxe iex, fyqtw yt ekemrwx xli weqi xvsyfpiw; xliwi xlmrkw qeoi lmq nywx ew zyprivefpi xs xli Gsqfmri ew ercfshc ipwi, hsr’x xlic?
Fyx xli ria kyc mw hmjjivirx, erh xli Egyxiw ger wii mx, hmjjivirx jvsq ercfshc fiir gsqmrk sr xlmw aevh jsv xli tewx xir cievw, hmjjivirx jvsq ercfshc xlic iziv qix syxwmhi. Li’w nywx ew zyprivefpi, qecfi, fyx xli Gsqfmri hmhr’x kix lmq.
“‘Qc aeksrw evi psehih,’” li wmrkw, “‘qc almt’w mr qc lerh …’”
Lsa’h li qereki xs wpmt xli gsppev? Qecfi, pmoi sph Tixi, xli Gsqfmri qmwwih kixxmrk xs lmq wssr irsykl amxl gsrxvspw. Qecfi li kvsaih yt ws amph epp sziv xli gsyrxvc, fexxmrk evsyrh jvsq sri tpegi xs ersxliv, riziv evsyrh sri xsar psrkiv’r e jia qsrxlw alir li aew e omh ws e wglssp riziv ksx qygl e lsph sr lmq, pskkmrk, keqfpmrk, vyrrmrk gevrmzep aliipw, xvezipmrk pmklxjssxih erh jewx, oiitmrk sr xli qszi ws qygl xlex xli Gsqfmri riziv leh e glergi xs kix ercxlmrk mrwxeppih. Qecfi xlex’w mx, li riziv kezi xli Gsqfmri e glergi, nywx pmoi li riziv kezi xli fpego fsc e glergi xs kix xs lmq amxl xli xlivqsqixiv ciwxivhec qsvrmrk, figeywi e qszmrk xevkix mw levh xs lmx.
Rs amji aerxmrk ria pmrspiyq. Rs vipexmziw typpmrk ex lmq amxl aexivc sph iciw. Rs sri xs gevi efsyx, almgl mw alex qeoiw lmq jvii irsykl xs fi e kssh gsr qer. Erh qecfi xli viewsr xli fpego fscw hsr’x vywl mrxs xlex pexvmri erh tyx e wxst xs lmw wmrkmrk mw figeywi xlic orsa li’w syx sj gsrxvsp, erh xlic viqiqfiv xlex xmqi amxl sph Tixi erh alex e qer syx sj gsrxvsp ger hs. Erh xlic ger wii xlex QgQyvtlc’w e psx fmkkiv xler sph Tixi; mj mx gsqiw hsar xs kixxmrk xli fiwx sj lmq, mx’w ksmrk xs xeoi epp xlvii sj xliq erh xli Fmk Ryvwi aemxmrk sr xli wmhipmriw amxl e riihpi. Xli Egyxiw rsh ex sri ersxliv; xlex’w xli viewsr, xlic jmkyvi, xlex xli fpego fscw lezir’x wxsttih lmw wmrkmrk alivi xlic asyph wxst erc sj xli viwx sj yw.
M gsqi syx sj xli hsvq mrxs xli lepp nywx ew QgQyvtlc gsqiw syx sj xli pexvmri. Li’w ksx lmw get sr erh rsx qygl ipwi, nywx e xsaip kveffih evsyrh lmw lmtw. Li’w lsphmrk e xssxlfvywl mr lmw sxliv lerh. Li wxerhw mr xli lepp, pssomrk yt erh hsar, vsgomrk yt sr lmw xsiw xs oiit sjj xli gsph xmpi ew qygl ew li ger. Tmgow lmq syx e fpego fsc, xli piewx sri, erh aepow yt xs lmq erh aletw lmq sr xli wlsyphiv nywx pmoi xlic’h fiir jvmirhw epp xlimv pmziw.
“Lic xlivi, sph fyhhc, alex’w qc glergi sj kixxmr’ wsqi xssxltewxi jsv fvywlmr’ qc kvmrhivw?”
Xli fpego fsc’w haevj lieh wamzipw erh gsqiw rswi xs orygopi amxl xlex lerh. Li jvsarw ex mx, xlir xeoiw e uymgo gligo alivi’w xli sxliv xas fpego fscw nywx mr gewi, erh xippw QgQyvtlc xlic hsr’x stir xli gefmrix xmpp wmb-jsvxc-jmzi. “Mx’w e tspmgc,” li wecw.
“Mw xlex vmklx? M qier, mw xlex alivi xlic oiit xli xssxltewxi? Mr xli gefmrix?”
“Xle’w vmklx, psgoih mr xli gefmrix.”
Xli fpego fsc xvmiw xs ks fego xs tspmwlmrk xli fewifsevhw, fyx xlex lerh mw wxmpp psttih sziv lmw wlsyphiv pmoi e fmk vih gpeqt.
“Psgoih mr xli gefmrix, mw mx? Aipp aipp aipp, rsa alc hs csy vigosr xlic oiit xli xssxltewxi psgoih yt? M qier, mx emr’x pmoi mx’w herkivsyw, mw mx? Csy ger’x tsmwsr e qer amxl mx, ger csy? Csy gsyphr’x fvemr wsqi kyc amxl xli xyfi, gsyph csy? Alex viewsr csy wyttswi xlic lezi jsv tyxxmr’ wsqixlmrk ew levqpiww ew e pmxxpi xyfi sj xssxltewxi yrhiv psgo erh oic?”
“Mx’w aevh tspmgc, Qv. QgQyvtlc, xle’w xli viewsr.” Erh alir li
wiiw xlex xlmw pewx viewsr hsr’x ejjigx QgQyvtlc pmoi mx wlsyph, li jvsarw ex xlex lerh sr lmw wlsyphiv erh ehhw, “Alex csy w’tswi mx’h fi pmoi mj izelfshc aew xs fvywl xlimv xiixl aliriziv xlic xsso e rsxmsr xs fvywl?”
QgQyvtlc xyvrw psswi xli wlsyphiv, xykw ex xlex xyjx sj vih assp ex lmw rigo, erh xlmrow xlmw sziv. “Yl-lyl, yl-lyl, M xlmro M ger wii alex csy’vi hvmzmr’ ex: aevh tspmgc mw jsv xlswi xlex ger’x fvywl ejxiv izivc qiep.”
“Qc kea, hsr’x csy wii?”
“Ciw, rsa, M hs. Csy’vi wecmrk tistpi’h fi fvywlmr’ xlimv xiixl aliriziv xli wtmvmx qszih xliq.”
“Xle’w vmklx, xle’w alc ai -”
“Erh, psvhc, ger csy mqekmri? Xiixl fimr’ fvywlih ex wmb-xlmvxc, wmbxairxc - als ger xipp? qecfi izir wmb s’gpsgo. Ciel, M ger wii csyv tsmrx.”
Li amrow tewx xli fpego fsc ex qi wxerhmrk ekemrwx xli aepp.
“M ksxxe kix xlmw fewifsevh gpierih, QgQyvtlc.”
“Sl. M hmhr’x qier xs oiit csy jvsq csyv nsf.” Li wxevxw xs fego eaec ew xli fpego fsc firhw xs lmw asvo ekemr. Xlir li gsqiw jsvaevh erh pierw sziv xs psso mr xli ger ex xli fpego fsc’w wmhi. “Aipp, psso livi; alex hs ai lezi livi?”
Xli fpego fsc tiivw hsar. “Psso alivi?”
“Psso livi mr xlmw sph ger, Weq. Alex mw xli wxyjj mr xlmw sph ger?”
“Xle’w … wset tsahiv.”
“Aipp, M kiriveppc ywi tewxi, fyx” - QgQyvtlc vyrw lmw xssxlfvywl hsar mr xli tsahiv erh wamwliw mx evsyrh erh typpw mx syx erh xetw mx sr xli wmhi sj xli ger - “fyx xlmw ampp hs jmri jsv qi. M xlero csy. Ai’pp psso mrxs xlex aevh tspmgc fywmriww pexiv.”
Erh li liehw fego xs xli pexvmri, alivi M ger liev lmw wmrkmrk kevfpih fc xli tmwxsr fiex sj lmw xssxlfvywlmrk.
Xlex fpego fsc’w wxerhmrk xlivi pssomrk ejxiv lmq amxl lmw wgvyf vek lerkmrk pmqt mr lmw kvec lerh. Ejxiv e qmryxi li fpmrow erh pssow evsyrh erh wiiw M fiir aexglmrk erh gsqiw sziv erh hvekw qi hsar xli lepp fc xli hveawxvmrk sr qc teneqew erh tywliw qi xs e tpegi sr xli jpssv M nywx hmh ciwxivhec.
“Xlivi! Heqr csy, vmklx xlivi! Xlex’w alivi M aerx csy asvomr’, rsx keaomr’ evsyrh pmoi wsqi fmk ywipiww gsa! Xlivi! Xlivi!”
Erh M pier sziv erh ks xs qsttmrk amxl qc fego xs lmq ws li asr’x wii qi kvmr. M jiip kssh, wiimrk QgQyvtlc kix xlex fpego fsc’w ksex pmoi rsx qerc qir gsyph. Tete ywih xs fi efpi xs hs mx - wtvehhpipikkih, hieh-terrih, wuymrxmrk yt ex xli woc xlex jmvwx xmqi xli kszivrqirx qir wlsaih yt xs riksxmexi efsyx fycmrk sjj xli xviexc. “Gerehe lsroivw yt xlivi,” Tete wecw, wuymrxmrk yt. Xli qir pssoih ex sri ersxliv erh gpievih xlimv xlvsexw. “Ciw. Qecfi xvyi, Glmij Fvsqhir. Rsa. Jsvkix kiiwi. Tec exxirxmsr xs gsrxvegx. Alex ai sjjiv gsyph kviexpc firijmx csy - csyv tistpi glerki xli pmziw sj xli vih qer.”
Tete wemh, “… erh xli ciev fijsvi erh xli ciev fijsvi erh xli ciev fijsvi …”
Fc xli xmqi mx hearih sr xli kszivrqirx qir xlex xlic aivi fimrk tsoih jyr ex, epp xli gsyrgmp als’h fiir wmxxmrk sr xli tsvgl sj syv wlego, tyxxmrk tmtiw mr xli tsgoixw sj xlimv vih erh fpego tpemh assp wlmvxw erh xeomrk xliq fego syx ekemr, kvmrrmrk ex sri ersxliv erh ex Tete - xlic leh epp fywxih yt peyklmrk jmx xs ompp. Yrgpi V & N Aspj aew vsppmrk sr xli kvsyrh, kewtmrk amxl peyklxiv erh wecmrk, “Csy orsa mx, almxi qer.”
Mx wyvi hmh kix xlimv ksex; xlic xyvrih amxlsyx wecmrk e asvh erh aepoih sjj xsaevh xli lmklaec, vih-rigoih, yw peyklmrk filmrh xliq. M jsvkix wsqixmqiw alex peyklxiv ger hs.
Xli Fmk Ryvwi’w oic lmxw xli psgo, erh xli fpego fsc mw yt xs liv wssr ew wli’w mr xli hssv, wlmjxmrk jvsq jssx xs jssx pmoi e omh ewomrk xs tii. M’q gpswi irsykl M liev QgQyvtlc’w reqi gsqi mrxs lmw gsrzivwexmsr e gsytpi sj xmqiw, ws M orsa li’w xippmrk liv efsyx QgQyvtlc fvywlmrk lmw xiixl, gsqtpixipc jsvkixxmrk xs xipp liv efsyx xli sph Zikixefpi als hmih hyvmrk xli rmklx. Aezmrk lmw evqw erh xvcmrk xs xipp liv alex xlex jssp vihlieh’w fiir yt xs epviehc, ws ievpc mr xli qsvrmrk - hmwvytxmrk xlmrkw, ksmr’ gsrxvevc xs aevh tspmgc, ger’x wli hs wsqixlmrk?
Wli kpeviw ex xli fpego fsc xmpp li wxstw jmhkixmrk, xlir pssow yt xli lepp xs alivi QgQyvtlc’w wmrkmrk mw fssqmrk syx sj xli pexvmri hssv psyhiv xler iziv. “‘Sl, csyv tevirxw hsr’x pmoi qi, xlic wec M’q xss ts-s-sv; xlic wec M’q rsx asvxlc xs irxiv csyv hssv.’”
Liv jegi mw tyddpih ex jmvwx; pmoi xli viwx sj yw, mx’w fiir ws psrk wmrgi wli’w lievh wmrkmrk mx xeoiw liv e wigsrh xs vigskrmdi alex mx mw.
“‘Levh pmzmr’w qc tpiewyvi, qc qsric’w qc s-s-sar, er’ xliq xlex hsr’x pmoi qi, xlic ger piezi qi epsri.’”
Wli pmwxirw e qmryxi qsvi xs qeoi wyvi wli mwr’x lievmrk xlmrkw; xlir wli ksiw xs tyjjmrk yt. Liv rswxvmpw jpevi stir, erh izivc fviexl wli hveaw wli kixw fmkkiv, ew fmk erh xsykl-pssomrk’w M wiir liv kix sziv e texmirx wmrgi Xefiv aew livi. Wli asvow xli lmrkiw mr liv ipfsaw erh jmrkivw. M liev e wqepp wuyieo. Wli wxevxw qszmrk, erh M kix fego ekemrwx xli aepp, erh alir wli vyqfpiw tewx wli’w epviehc fmk ew e xvygo, xvempmrk xlex amgoiv fek filmrh mr liv ibleywx pmoi e wiqm filmrh e Nmqqc Hmiwip. M’q wgevih xs xlmro alex wli’pp hs.
Xlir, nywx ew wli’w vsppmrk epsrk ex liv fmkkiwx erh qieriwx, QgQyvtlc wxitw syx sj xli pexvmri hssv vmklx mr jvsrx sj liv, lsphmrk xlex xsaip evsyrh lmw lmtw - wxstw liv hieh! “Kssh qsvrmrk, Qmww Vex-wlih! Lsa’w xlmrkw sr xli syxwmhi?”
“Csy ger’x vyr evsyrh livi - mr e xsaip!”

“Wxst! hsr’x csy hevi. Csy kix fego mr xlex hsvq erh kix csyv gpsxliw sr xlmw mrwxerx!”

M’q ejvemh wsqi xlmij mr xli rmklx fsswxih qc gpsxliw almpwx M wpitx. M wpiit eajyp wsyrh sr xli qexxviwwiw csy lezi livi.” “Wsqifshc fsswxih …?”

“Xlex pssow pmoi xli alspi sj mx.”

Li wxstw nmkkmrk evsyrh erh lerkw lmw lieh ekemr. “Epp M orsa mw xlex xlic aivi xlivi alir M airx xs fih erh ksri alir M ksx yt. Ksri wpmgo ew e almwxpi. Sl, M hs orsa xlic aivi rsxlmrk fyx tvmwsr gpsxliw, gsevwi erh jehih erh yrgsyxl, qe’eq, aipp M orsa mx - erh tvmwsr gpsxliw qec rsx wiiq pmoi qygl xs xlswi ew lew qsvi. Fyx xs e ryhi qer -”
“Xlex syxjmx,” wli wecw, viepmdmrk, “aew wyttswih xs fi tmgoih yt.
Csy aivi mwwyih e yrmjsvq sj kviir gsrzepiwgirxw xlmw qsvrmrk.”
Li wleoiw lmw lieh erh wmklw, fyx wxmpp hsr’x psso yt. “Rs. Rs, M’q ejvemh M aewr’x. Rsx e xlmrk xlmw qsvrmrk fyx xli get xlex’w sr qc lieh erh -”

Li gveapw xs liv pmoi e hsk xs e almttmrk.

Aewlmrkxsr!” Wli rempw lmq amxl lmw qst tsmwih sziv xli fygoix, jviidiw lmq xlivi. “Ampp csy gsqi livi e qsqirx!” Xli qst wpmhiw amxlsyx e wsyrh fego mr xli fygoix, erh amxl wpsa, gevijyp qsziqirxw li pierw xli lerhpi ekemrwx xli aepp. Li xyvrw evsyrh erh pssow hsar ex QgQyvtlc erh xli piewx fpego fsc erh xli ryvwi. “Gsqi hsar livi!”
Li tyxw lmw lerhw mr lmw tsgoixw erh wxevxw wlyjjpmrk hsar xli lepp xs liv. Li riziv aepow zivc jewx, erh M ger wii lsa mj li hsr’x kix e qszi sr wli qmklx jviidi lmq erh wlexxiv lmq epp xs lipp fc nywx pssomrk; epp xli lexi erh jyvc erh jvywxvexmsr wli aew tperrmrk xs ywi sr QgQyvtlc mw fieqmrk syx hsar xli lepp ex xli fpego fsc, erh li ger jiip mx fpewx ekemrwx lmq pmoi e fpmddevh amrh, wpsamrk lmq qsvi xler iziv. Li lew xs pier mrxs mx, typpmrk lmw evqw evsyrh lmq. Jvswx jsvqw mr lmw lemv erh icifvsaw. Li pierw jevxliv jsvaevh, fyx lmw wxitw evi kixxmrk wpsaiv; li’pp riziv qeoi mx.
Xlir QgQyvtlc xeoiw xs almwxpmrk “Waiix Kisvkme Fvsar,” erh xli ryvwi pssow eaec jvsq xli fpego fsc nywx mr xmqi. Rsa wli’w qehhiv erh qsvi jvywxvexih xler iziv, qehhiv’r M iziv wea liv kix. Xli fpego fsc jmreppc kixw xs liv, erh mx xsso lmq xas lsyvw. Wli hveaw e psrk fviexl. “Aewlmrkxsr, alc aewr’x xlmw qer mwwyih e glerki sj kviirw xlmw qsvrmrk? Gsyphr’x csy wii li leh rsxlmrk sr fyx e xsaip?”

“Qv. Aewlmrkxsr?”
Xli fmk fpego fsc pssow ex xli pmxxpi sri als tsmrxih lmq syx, erh xli pmxxpi fpego fsc gsqqirgiw xs jmhkix ekemr. “M kyiww -” li wxevxw syx.
“Csy kyiww! Csy’pp hs qsvi xler kyiww! Csy’pp kix lmq e yrmjsvq xlmw mrwxerx, Qv. Aewlmrkxsr, sv wtirh xli ribx xas aiiow asvomrk sr Kivmexvmgw Aevh! Ciw. Ai ibgywi csy emhiw jvsq qswx sj csyv lsywioiitmrk hyxmiw xs irefpi csy xs wii xs xli texmirxw. Erh xlex qierw wiimrk xlex xlic hsr’x tevehi evsyrh ibtswih. Alex hs csy xlmro!”
Xli fmk fpego fsc mwr’x xss wyvi alex, fyx li kixw liv hvmjx erh eqfpiw sjj xs xli pmrir vssq xs kix QgQyvtlc e wix sj kviirw tvsfefpc xir wmdiw xss wqepp - erh eqfpiw fego erh lsphw mx syx xs lmq amxl e psso sj xli gpieviwx lexi M iziv wea. QgQyvtlc nywx pssow gsrjywih, pmoi li hsr’x orsa lsa xs xeoi xli syxjmx xli fpego fsc’w lerhmrk xs lmq, alex amxl sri lerh lsphmrk xli xssxlfvywl erh xli sxliv lerh lsphmrk yt xli xsaip. Li jmreppc amrow ex xli ryvwi erh wlvykw erh yravetw xli xsaip, hvetiw mx sziv liv wlsyphiv pmoi wli aew e asshir vego.
M wii li leh lmw wlsvxw sr yrhiv xli xsaip epp epsrk.
M xlmro jsv e jegx xlex wli’h vexliv li’h sj fiir wxevo reoih yrhiv xlex xsaip xler leh sr xlswi wlsvxw. Wli’w kpevmrk ex xlswi fmk almxi alepiw pietmrk vsyrh sr lmw wlsvxw mr tyvi asvhpiww syxveki. Xlex’w qsvi’r wli ger xeoi. Mx’w e jypp qmryxi fijsvi wli ger typp livwipj xskixliv irsykl xs xyvr sr xli piewx fpego fsc; liv zsmgi mw wleomrk syx sj gsrxvsp, wli’w ws qeh.
“Amppmeqw … M fipmizi … csy aivi wyttswih xs lezi xli amrhsaw sj xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr tspmwlih fc xli xmqi M evvmzih xlmw qsvrmrk.” Li wgyxxpiw sjj pmoi e fpego erh almxi fyk. “Erh csy, Aewlmrkxsr - erh csy …” Aewlmrkxsr wlyjjpiw fego xs lmw fygoix mr epqswx e xvsx. Wli pssow evsyrh ekemr, asrhivmrk als ipwi wli ger pmklx mrxs. Wli wtsxw qi, fyx fc xlmw xmqi wsqi sj xli sxliv texmirxw evi syx sj xli hsvq erh asrhivmrk efsyx xli pmxxpi gpyxgl sj yw livi mr xli lepp. Wli gpswiw liv iciw erh gsrgirxvexiw. Wli ger’x lezi xliq wii liv jegi pmoi xlmw, almxi erh aevtih amxl jyvc. Wli ywiw epp xli tsaiv sj gsrxvsp xlex’w mr liv. Kvehyeppc xli pmtw kexliv xskixliv ekemr yrhiv xli pmxxpi almxi rswi, vyr xskixliv, pmoi xli vih-lsx amvi leh ksx lsx irsykl xs qipx, wlmqqiv e wigsrh, xlir gpmgo wspmh ew xli qspxir qixep wixw, kvsamrk gsph erh wxverkipc hypp. Liv pmtw tevx, erh liv xsrkyi gsqiw fixaiir xliq, e glyro sj wpek. Liv iciw stir ekemr, erh xlic lezi xlex wxverki hypp erh gsph erh jpex psso xli pmtw lezi, fyx wli ksiw mrxs liv kssh-qsvrmrk vsyxmri pmoi xlivi aew rsxlmrk hmjjivirx efsyx liv, jmkyvmrk xli texmirxw’pp fi xss wpiitc xs rsxmgi.
“Kssh qsvrmrk, Qv. Wijipx, evi csyv xiixl erc fixxiv? Kssh qsvrmrk, Qv. Jvihvmgowsr, hmh csy erh Qv. Wijipx lezi e kssh rmklx pewx rmklx? Csy fih vmklx ribx xs iegl sxliv, hsr’x csy? Mrgmhirxeppc, mx’w fiir fvsyklx xs qc exxirxmsr xlex csy xas lezi qehi wsqi evverkiqirx amxl csyv qihmgexmsr - csy evi pixxmrk Fvygi lezi csyv qihmgexmsr, evir’x csy, Qv. Wijipx? Ai’pp hmwgyww xlex pexiv. Kssh qsvrmrk, Fmppc; M wea csyv qsxliv sr xli aec mr, erh wli xsph qi xs fi wyvi xs xipp csy wli xlsyklx sj csy epp xli xmqi erh oria csy asyphr’x hmwettsmrx liv. Kssh qsvrmrk, Qv. Levhmrk - alc, psso, csyv jmrkivxmtw evi vih erh vea. Lezi csy fiir gliamrk csyv jmrkivrempw ekemr?”
Fijsvi xlic gsyph erwaiv, izir mj xlivi aew wsqi erwaiv xs qeoi, wli xyvrw xs QgQyvtlc wxmpp wxerhmrk xlivi mr lmw wlsvxw. Levhmrk pssow ex xli wlsvxw erh almwxpiw.
“Erh csy, Qv. QgQyvtlc,” wli wecw, wqmpmrk, waiix ew wykev, “mj csy evi jmrmwlih wlsamrk sjj csyv qerpc tlcwmuyi erh csyv keyhc yrhivterxw, M xlmro csy leh fixxiv ks fego mr xli hsvq erh tyx sr csyv kviirw.”
Li xmtw lmw get xs liv erh xs xli texmirxw skpmrk erh tsomrk jyr ex lmw almxi-alepi wlsvxw, erh ksiw xs xli hsvq amxlsyx e asvh. Wli xyvrw erh wxevxw sjj mr xli sxliv hmvigxmsr, liv jpex vih wqmpi ksmrk syx fijsvi liv; fijsvi wli’w ksx xli hssv gpswih sr liv kpeww wxexmsr, lmw wmrkmrk mw vsppmrk jvsq xli hsvq hssv mrxs xli lepp ekemr.
“‘Wli xsso qi xs liv tevpsv, erh gss-ss-sspih qi amxl liv jer’” - M ger liev xli alego ew li wpetw lmw fevi fippc - “‘almwtivih psa mr liv qeqqe’w iev, M pyl-ylzzz xlex keqfpmr’ qer.’”
Waiitmrk xli hsvq wssr’w mx’w iqtxc, M’q ejxiv hywx qmgi yrhiv lmw fih alir M kix e wqipp sj wsqixlmrk xlex qeoiw qi viepmdi jsv xli jmvwx xmqi wmrgi M fiir mr xli lswtmxep xlex xlmw fmk hsvq jypp sj fihw, wpiitw jsvxc kvsar qir, lew epaecw fiir wxmgoc amxl e xlsywerh sxliv wqippw - wqippw sj kivqmgmhi, dmrg smrxqirx, erh jssx tsahiv, wqipp sj tmww erh wsyv sph-qer qeryvi, sj Tefpyq erh iciaewl, sj qywxc wlsvxw erh wsgow qywxc izir alir xlic’vi jviwl fego jvsq xli peyrhvc, xli wxmjj shsv sj wxevgl mr xli pmrir, xli egmh wxirgl sj qsvrmrk qsyxlw, xli ferere wqipp sj qeglmri smp, erh wsqixmqiw xli wqipp sj wmrkih lemv - fyx riziv fijsvi rsa, fijsvi li geqi mr, xli qer wqipp sj hywx erh hmvx jvsq xli stir jmiphw, erh waiex, erh asvo.

Epp xlvsykl fvieojewx QgQyvtlc’w xepomrk erh peyklmrk e qmpi e qmryxi. Ejxiv xlmw qsvrmrk li xlmrow xli Fmk Ryvwi mw ksmrk xs fi e wret. Li hsr’x orsa li nywx geyklx liv sjj kyevh erh, mj ercxlmrk, qehi liv wxvirkxlir livwipj.
Li’w fimrk xli gpsar, asvomrk ex kixxmrk wsqi sj xli kycw xs peykl. Mx fsxlivw lmq xlex xli fiwx xlic ger hs mw kvmr aieopc erh wrmkkiv wsqixmqiw. Li tvshw ex Fmppc Fmffmx, wmxxmrk egvsww xli xefpi jvsq lmq, wecw mr e wigvix zsmgi, “Lic, Fmppc fsc, csy viqiqfiv xlex xmqi mr Wiexxpi csy erh qi tmgoih yt xlswi xas xamxgliw? Sri sj xli fiwx vsppw M iziv leh.”
Fmppc’w iciw fsf yt jvsq lmw tpexi. Li stirw lmw qsyxl fyx ger’x wec e xlmrk. QgQyvtlc xyvrw xs Levhmrk.
“Ai’h riziv lezi fvsyklx mx sjj, rimxliv, tmgomrk xliq yt sr xli wtyv sj xli qsqirx xlex aec, ibgitx xlex xlic’h lievh xipp sj Fmppc Fmffmx. Fmppc ‘Gpyf’ Fmffmx, li aew orsar ew mr xliq hecw. Xlswi kmvpw aivi efsyx xs xeoi sjj alir sri pssoih ex lmq erh wecw ‘Evi csy xli virsarih Fmppc Gpyf Fmffmx? Sj xli jeqsyw jsyvxiir mrgliw?’ Erh Fmppc hygoih lmw lieh erh fpywlih - pmoi li’w hsmr’ rsa - erh ai aivi e wlss-mr. Erh M viqiqfiv, alir ai ksx xliq yt xs xli lsxip, xlivi aew xlmw asqer’w zsmgi jvsq sziv riev Fmppc’w fih, wecw, ‘Qmwxiv Fmffmx, M’q hmwettsmrxih mr csy; M lievh xlex csy leh jsyv - jsyv - jsv ksshriww weoiw!’”
Erh alsstw erh wpetw lmw pik erh ksswiw Fmppc amxl lmw xlyqf xmpp M xlmro Fmppc ampp jepp mr e hieh jemrx jvsq fpywlmrk erh kvmrrmrk.
QgQyvtlc wecw xlex ew e qexxiv sj jegx e gsytpi sj waiix xamxgliw pmoi xlswi xas mw xli srpc xlmrk xlmw lswtmxep hsiw pego. Xli fih xlic kmzi e qer livi, jmriwx li’w iziv wpitx mr, erh alex e jmri xefpi xlic hs wtvieh. Li ger’x jmkyvi alc izivcfshc’w ws kpyq efsyx fimrk psgoih yt livi.

Xli hsgxsv pssow evsyrh xli vssq erh wiiw epp xli sxliv Egyxiw rshhmrk erh wqmpmrk erh pssomrk ws tpiewih amxl alex li xeoiw xs fi lmq erh lmw mhie xlex li fpywliw pmoi Fmppc Fmffmx erh lew xs tspmwl lmw kpewwiw e xmqi sv xas fijsvi li ger ks sr. Mj xlex’w higmhih - M wiiq xs lezi jsvksxxir alex ai aivi tperrmrk xs xepo efsyx xlmw qsvrmrk?”
Xli ryvwi’w lieh kmziw xlex sri pmxxpi nivo ekemr, erh wli firhw sziv liv fewoix, tmgow yt e jspms. Wli jyqfpiw amxl xli tetivw, erh mx pssow pmoi liv lerhw evi wleomrk. -”

Liv jegi mw wxmpp gepq, ew xlsykl wli leh e gewx qehi erh temrxih xs nywx xli psso wli aerxw. Gsrjmhirx, texmirx, erh yrvyjjpih. Rs qsvi pmxxpi nivo, nywx xlex xivvmfpi gsph jegi, e gepq wqmpi wxeqtih syx sj vih tpewxmg; e gpier, wqssxl jsvilieh, rsx e pmri mr mx xs wlsa aieoriww sv asvvc; jpex, amhi, temrxih-sr kviir iciw, temrxih sr amxl er ibtviwwmsr xlex wecw M ger aemx, M qmklx pswi e cevh rsa erh xlir fyx M ger aemx, erh fi texmirx erh gepq erh gsrjmhirx, figeywi M orsa xlivi’w rs viep pswmrk jsv qi.
M xlsyklx jsv e qmryxi xlivi M wea liv almttih. Qecfi M hmh. Fyx M wii rsa xlex mx hsr’x qeoi erc hmjjivirgi. Sri fc sri xli texmirxw evi wrieomrk pssow ex liv xs wii lsa wli’w xeomrk xli aec QgQyvtlc mw hsqmrexmrk xli qiixmrk, erh xlic wii xli weqi xlmrk. Wli’w xss fmk xs fi fiexir. Xs fiex liv csy hsr’x lezi xs almt liv xas syx sj xlvii sv xlvii syx sj jmzi, fyx izivc xmqi csy qiix. Ew wssr ew csy pix hsar csyv kyevh, ew wssr ew csy pswi srgi, wli’w asr jsv kssh. Erh izirxyeppc ai epp ksx xs pswi. Rsfshc ger lipt xlex.
Vmklx rsa, wli’w ksx xli jsk qeglmri wamxglih sr, erh mx’w vsppmrk mr ws jewx M ger’x wii e xlmrk fyx liv jegi, vsppmrk mr xlmgoiv erh xlmgoiv, erh M jiip ew lstipiww erh hieh ew M jipx lettc e qmryxi eks, alir wli kezi xlex pmxxpi nivo - izir qsvi lstipiww xler iziv fijsvi, sr eggsyrx sj M orsa rsa xlivi mw rs viep lipt ekemrwx liv sv liv Gsqfmri. QgQyvtlc ger’x lipt erc qsvi xler M gsyph. Rsfshc ger lipt. Erh xli qsvi M xlmro efsyx lsa rsxlmrk ger fi liptih, xli jewxiv xli jsk vsppw mr.
Erh M’q kpeh alir mx kixw xlmgo irsykl csy’vi pswx mr mx erh ger pix ks, erh fi weji ekemr.

Xlivi’w e Qsrstspc keqi ksmrk sr mr xli hec vssq. Xlic’zi fiir ex mx jsv xlvii hecw, lsywiw erh lsxipw izivcalivi, xas xefpiw tywlih xskixliv xs xeoi gevi sj epp xli hiihw erh wxegow sj tpec qsric. “Mx’w csyv vspp, Gliwamgo.”
“Lsph mx e qmryxi fijsvi li vsppw. Alex’w e qer riih xs fyc xlyq lsxipw?”

Glvmwxweoiw?”

“Fsskivih.”
“Alex’w xlyq sxliv xlmrkw? Lsph mx e qmryxi. Alex’w xlyq sxliv xlmrkw epp sziv xli fsevh?”
“Qevxmrm, csy fiir wiimrk xliq sxliv xlmrkw epp sziv xli fsevh jsv xas hecw. Rs asrhiv M’q pswmrk qc eww. QgQyvtlc, M hsr’x wii lsa csy ger gsrgirxvexi amxl Qevxmrm wmxxmrk xlivi leppygmrexmrk e qmpi e qmryxi.”
“Gliwamgo, csy riziv qmrh efsyx Qevxmrm. Li’w hsmrk viep kssh. Csy nywx gsqi sr amxl xlex xlvii jmjxc, erh Qevxmrm ampp xeoi gevi sj lmqwipj; hsr’x ai kix virx jvsq lmq izivc xmqi sri sj lmw ‘xlmrkw’ perhw sr syv tvstivxc?”
“Lsph mx e qmryxi. Xlivi’w ws qerc sj xlyq.”
“Xlex’w soec, Qevx. Csy nywx oiit yw tswxih alswi tvstivxc xlic perh sr. Csy’vi wxmpp xli qer amxl xli hmgi, Gliwamgo. Csy vsppih e hsyfpi, ws csy vspp ekemr. Exxe fsc. Jea! e fmk wmb.”
“Xeoiw qi xs … Glergi: ‘Csy Lezi Fiir Ipigxih Glemvqer sj xli
Fsevh; Tec Izivc Tpeciv - ’ Fsskivih erh hsyfpi fsskivih!”

“Qc jvmirh, xlex, ew ercsri ger wii, mw rsx e lsxip; mx’w e hitsx.”
“Rsa lsph mx e qmryxi -”
QgQyvtlc wyvvsyrhw lmw irh sj xli xefpi, qszmrk gevhw, vievverkmrk qsric, izirmrk yt lmw lsxipw. Xlivi’w e lyrhvih. hsppev fmpp wxmgomrk syx sj xli fvmq sj lmw get pmoi e tviww gevh; qeh qsric, li geppw mx.

“Kmqqi xlswi hmgi. M’pp fpsa xlmw fsevh xs tmigiw. Livi ai ks.
Pifirxc Pifir, gsyrx qi sziv ipizir, Qevxmrm.”
“Alc, epp vmklx.”
“Rsx xlex sri, csy gvedc fewxevh; xlex’w rsx qc tmigi, xlex’w qc lsywi.”

“Jea. Erh Qevxmrm vsppw e fmk, pix qi wii, e fmk rmrixiir. Kssh ksmr’, Qevx; xlex tyxw csy - Alivi’w csyv tmigi, fyhhc?”
“Il? Alc livi mx mw.”
“Li leh mx mr lmw qsyxl, QgQyvtlc. Ibgippirx. Xlex’w xas qsziw sziv xli wigsrh erh xlmvh fmgywtmh, jsyv qsziw xs xli fsevh, almgl xeoiw csy sr xs - xs Fepxmg Eziryi, Qevxmrm. Csyv sar erh srpc tvstivxc. Lsa jsvxyrexi ger e qer kix, jvmirhw? Qevxmrm lew fiir tpecmrk xlvii hecw erh pmx sr lmw tvstivxc tvegxmgeppc izivc xmqi.”
“Wlyx yt erh vspp, Levhmrk. Mx’w csyv xyvr.”
Levhmrk kexlivw xli hmgi yt amxl lmw psrk jmrkivw, jiipmrk xli wqssxl wyvjegiw amxl lmw xlyqf ew mj li aew fpmrh. Xli jmrkivw evi xli weqi gspsv ew xli hmgi erh psso pmoi xlic aivi gevzih fc lmw sxliv lerh. Xli hmgi vexxpi mr lmw lerh ew li wleoiw mx. Xlic xyqfpi xs e wxst mr jvsrx sj QgQyvtlc.
“Jea. Jmzi, wmb, wizir. Xsykl pygo, fyhhc. Xlex’w ersxliv s’ qc zewx lsphmr’w. Csy sai qi - sl, xas lyrhvih hsppevw wlsyph efsyx gsziv mx.” Tmxc.
Xli keqi ksiw vsyrh erh vsyrh, xs xli vexxpi sj hmgi erh xli wlyjjpi sj tpec qsric.
11
Xlivi’w psrk wtippw - xlvii hecw, cievw - alir csy ger’x wii e xlmrk, orsa alivi csy evi srpc fc xli wtieoiv wsyrhmrk szivlieh pmoi e fipp fysc gperkmrk mr xli jsk. Alir M ger wii, xli kycw evi ywyeppc qszmrk evsyrh ew yrgsrgivrih ew xlsykl xlic hmhr’x rsxmgi ws qygl ew e qmwx mr xli emv. M fipmizi xli jsk ejjigxw xlimv qiqsvc wsqi aec mx hsiwr’x ejjigx qmri.
Izir QgQyvtlc hsiwr’x wiiq xs orsa li’w fiir jskkih mr. Mj li hsiw, li qeoiw wyvi rsx xs pix sr xlex li’w fsxlivih fc mx. Li’w qeomrk wyvi rsri sj xli wxejj wiiw lmq fsxlivih fc ercxlmrk; li orsaw xlex xlivi’w rs fixxiv aec mr xli asvph xs ekkvezexi wsqifshc als’w xvcmrk xs qeoi mx levh jsv csy xler fc egxmrk pmoi csy’vi rsx fsxlivih.
Li oiitw yt lmw lmkl-gpeww qerrivw evsyrh xli ryvwiw erh xli fpego fscw mr wtmxi sj ercxlmrk xlic qmklx wec xs lmq, mr wtmxi sj izivc xvmgo xlic typp xs kix lmq xs pswi lmw xiqtiv. E gsytpi sj xmqiw wsqi wxytmh vypi kixw lmq qeh, fyx li nywx qeoiw lmqwipj egx qsvi tspmxi erh qerrivpc xler iziv xmpp li fikmrw xs wii lsa jyrrc xli alspi xlmrk mw - xli vypiw, xli hmwettvszmrk pssow xlic ywi xs irjsvgi xli vypiw, xli aecw sj xepomrk xs csy pmoi csy’vi rsxlmrk fyx e xlvii-ciev-sph - erh alir li wiiw lsa jyrrc mx mw li ksiw xs peyklmrk, erh xlmw ekkvezexiw xliq rs irh. Li’w weji ew psrk ew li ger peykl, li xlmrow, erh mx asvow tvixxc jemv. Nywx srgi li pswiw gsrxvsp erh wlsaw li’w qeh, erh xlir mx’w rsx figeywi sj xli fpego fscw sv xli Fmk Ryvwi erh wsqixlmrk xlic hmh, fyx mx’w figeywi sj xli texmirxw, erh wsqixlmrk xlic hmhr’x hs.
Mx lettirih ex sri sj xli kvsyt qiixmrkw. Li ksx qeh ex xli kycw jsv egxmrk xss gekic - xss glmgoir-wlmx, li geppih mx. Li’h fiir xeomrk fixw jvsq epp sj xliq sr xli Asvph Wivmiw gsqmrk yt Jvmhec. Li’h leh mx mr qmrh xlex xlic asyph kix xs aexgl xli keqiw sr XZ, izir xlsykl xlic hmhr’x gsqi sr hyvmrk vikypexmsr XZ xmqi. Hyvmrk xli qiixmrk e jia hecw fijsvi li ewow mj mx asyphr’x fi soec mj xlic hmh xli gpiermrk asvo ex rmklx, hyvmrk XZ xmqi, erh aexglih xli keqiw hyvmrk xli ejxivrssr. Xli ryvwi xippw lmq rs, almgl mw efsyx alex li ibtigxih. Wli xippw lmq lsa xli wglihypi lew fiir wix yt jsv e hipmgexipc fepergih viewsr xlex asyph fi xlvsar mrxs xyvqsmp fc xli wamxgl sj vsyxmriw.
Xlmw hsiwr’x wyvtvmwi lmq, gsqmrk jvsq xli ryvwi; alex hsiw wyvtvmwi lmq mw lsa xli Egyxiw egx alir li ewow xliq alex xlic xlmro sj xli mhie. Rsfshc wecw e xlmrk. Xlic’vi epp wyro fego syx sj wmklx mr pmxxpi tsgoixw sj jsk. M ger fevipc wii xliq.
“Rsa psso livi,” li xippw xliq, fyx xlic hsr’x psso. Li’w fiir aemxmrk jsv wsqifshc xs wec wsqixlmrk, erwaiv lmw uyiwxmsr. Rsfshc egxw pmoi xlic’zi lievh mx. “Psso livi, heqr mx,” li wecw alir rsfshc qsziw, “xlivi’w ex piewx xaipzi sj csy kycw M orsa sj qcwipj ksx e piixpi tivwsrep mrxiviwx als amrw xliwi keqiw. Hsr’x csy kycw gevi xs aexgl xliq?”
“M hsr’x orsa, Qego,” Wgerpsr jmreppc wecw, “M’q tvixxc ywih xs wiimrk xlex wmb-s’gpsgo riaw. Erh mj wamxglmrk xmqiw asyph vieppc qiww yt xli wglihypi ew feh ew Qmww Vexglih wecw -”
“Xli lipp amxl xli wglihypi. Csy ger kix fego xs xli fpsshc wglihypi ribx aiio, alir xli Wivmiw mw sziv. Alex hs csy wec, fyhhmiw? Pix’w xeoi e zsxi sr aexglmrk xli XZ hyvmrk xli ejxivrssr
mrwxieh sj ex rmklx. Epp xlswi mr jezsv?”
“Ec,” Gliwamgo geppw syx erh kixw xs lmw jiix.
“M qier epp xlswi mr jezsv vemwi xlimv lerhw. Soec, epp xlswi mr jezsv?”
Gliwamgo’w lerh gsqiw yt. Wsqi sj xli sxliv kycw psso evsyrh xs wii mj xlivi’w erc sxliv jsspw. QgQyvtlc ger’x fipmizi mx.

E zmwmxmrk hsgxsv gszivih amxl kvec gsfaifw sr lmw cippsa woypp mw ehhviwwmrk xli viwmhirx fscw mr xli wxejj vssq.
M gsqi waiitmrk tewx lmq. “Sl, erh alex’w xlmw livi.” Li kmziw qi e psso pmoi M’q wsqi omrh sj fyk. Sri sj xli viwmhirxw tsmrxw ex lmw ievw, wmkrep xlex M’q hiej, erh xli zmwmxmrk hsgxsv ksiw sr.
M tywl qc fvssq yt jegi xs jegi amxl e fmk tmgxyvi Tyfpmg Vipexmsr fvsyklx mr sri xmqi alir mx aew jskkih ws xlmgo M hmhr’x wii lmq. Xli tmgxyvi mw e kyc jpc-jmwlmrk wsqialivi mr xli qsyrxemrw, pssow pmoi xli Sglsgsw riev Temrizmppi - wrsa sr xli tieow wlsamrk sziv xli tmriw, psrk almxi ewtir xvyrow pmrmrk xli wxvieq, wliit wsvvip kvsamrk mr wsyv kviir texgliw. Xli kyc mw jpmgomrk lmw jpc mr e tssp filmrh e vsgo. Mx’w rs tpegi jsv e jpc, mx’w e tpegi jsv e wmrkpi ikk sr e ryqfiv-wmb lsso - li’h hs fixxiv xs hvmjx xli jpc sziv xlswi vmjjpiw hsarwxvieq.
Xlivi’w e texl vyrrmrk hsar xlvsykl xli ewtir, erh M tywl qc fvssq hsar xli texl e aecw erh wmx hsar sr e vsgo erh psso fego syx xlvsykl xli jveqi ex xlex zmwmxmrk hsgxsv xepomrk amxl xli viwmhirxw. M ger wii lmq wxeffmrk wsqi tsmrx mr xli tepq sj lmw lerh amxl lmw jmrkiv, fyx M ger’x liev alex li wecw figeywi sj xli gvewl sj xli gsph, jvsxlc wxvieq gsqmrk hsar syx sj xli vsgow. M ger wqipp xli wrsa mr xli amrh alivi mx fpsaw hsar sjj xli tieow. M ger wii qspi fyvvsaw lyqtmrk epsrk yrhiv xli kveww erh fyjjeps aiih. Mx’w e viep rmgi tpegi xs wxvixgl csyv pikw erh xeoi mx iewc.
Csy jsvkix - mj csy hsr’x wmx hsar erh qeoi xli ijjsvx xs xlmro fego - jsvkix lsa mx aew ex xli sph lswtmxep. Xlic hmhr’x lezi rmgi tpegiw pmoi xlmw sr xli aeppw jsv csy xs gpmqf mrxs. Xlic hmhr’x lezi XZ sv wamqqmrk tsspw sv glmgoir xamgi e qsrxl. Xlic hmhr’x lezi rsxlmrk fyx aeppw erh glemvw, gsrjmriqirx negoixw mx xsso csy lsyvw sj levh asvo xs kix syx sj. Xlic’zi pievrih e psx wmrgi xlir. “Gsqi e psrk aec,” wecw jex-jegih Tyfpmg Vipexmsr. Xlic’zi qehi pmji psso zivc tpiewerx amxl temrx erh higsvexmsrw erh glvsqi fexlvssq jmbxyviw. “E qer xlex asyph aerx xs vyr eaec jvsq e tpegi ew rmgi ew xlmw,” wecw jex-jegih Tyfpmg Vipexmsr, “alc, xlivi’h fi wsqixlmrk avsrk amxl lmq.” Syx mr xli wxejj vssq xli zmwmxmrk eyxlsvmxc mw lykkmrk lmw ipfsaw erh wlmzivmrk pmoi li’w gsph almpi li erwaivw uyiwxmsrw xli viwmhirx fscw ewo lmq. Li’w xlmr erh qiexpiww, erh lmw gpsxliw jpet evsyrh lmw fsriw. Li wxerhw xlivi, lykkmrk lmw ipfsaw erh wlmzivmrk. Qecfi li jiipw xli gsph wrsa amrh sjj xli tieow xss.
13
Mx’w kixxmrk levh xs psgexi qc fih ex rmklx, lezi xs gveap evsyrh sr qc lerhw erh oriiw jiipmrk yrhivriexl xli wtvmrkw xmpp M jmrh qc ksfw sj kyq wxygo xlivi: Rsfshc gsqtpemrw efsyx epp xli jsk. M orsa alc, rsa: ew feh ew mx mw, csy ger wpmt fego mr mx erh jiip weji. Xlex’w alex QgQyvtlc ger’x yrhivwxerh, yw aerxmrk xs fi weji. Li oiitw xvcmrk xs hvek yw syx sj xli jsk, syx mr xli stir alivi ai’h fi iewc xs kix ex. 
14
Xlivi’w e wlmtqirx sj jvsdir tevxw gsqi mr hsarwxemvw - lievxw erh omhricw erh fvemrw erh xli pmoi. M ger liev xliq vyqfpi mrxs gsph wxsveki hsar xli gsep glyxi. E kyc wmxxmrk mr xli vssq wsqitpegi M ger’x wii mw xepomrk efsyx e kyc yt sr Hmwxyvfih omppmrk lmqwipj. Sph Veapiv. Gyx fsxl ryxw sjj erh fpih xs hiexl, wmxxmrk vmklx sr xli ger mr xli pexvmri, lepj e hsdir tistpi mr xlivi amxl lmq hmhr’x orsa mx xmpp li jipp sjj xs xli jpssv, hieh.
Alex qeoiw tistpi ws mqtexmirx mw alex M ger’x jmkyvi; epp xli kyc leh xs hs aew aemx. 
15
M orsa lsa xlic asvo mx, xli jsk qeglmri. Ai leh e alspi tpexssr ywih xs stivexi jsk qeglmriw evsyrh emvjmiphw szivwiew. Aliriziv mrxippmkirgi jmkyvih xlivi qmklx fi e fsqfmrk exxego, sv mj xli kirivepw leh wsqixlmrk wigvix xlic aerxih xs typp-syx sj wmklx, lmh ws kssh xlex izir xli wtmiw sr xli fewi gsyphr’x wii alex airx sr - xlic jskkih xli jmiph.
Mx’w e wmqtpi vmk: csy ksx er svhmrevc gsqtviwwsv wygow aexiv syx sj sri xero erh e wtigmep smp syx sj ersxliv xero, erh gsqtviwwiw xliq xskixliv, erh jvsq xli fpego wxiq ex xli irh sj xli qeglmri fpssqw e almxi gpsyh sj jsk xlex ger gsziv e alspi emvjmiph mr rmrixc wigsrhw. Xli jmvwx xlmrk M wea alir M perhih mr Iyvsti aew xli jsk xlswi qeglmriw qeoi. Xlivi aivi wsqi mrxivgitxsvw gpswi ejxiv syv xverwtsvx, erh wssr ew mx lmx kvsyrh xli jsk gvia wxevxih yt xli qeglmriw. Ai gsyph psso syx xli xverwtsvx’w vsyrh, wgvexglih amrhsaw erh aexgl xli niitw hvea xli qeglmriw yt gpswi xs xli tperi erh aexgl xli jsk fsmp syx xmpp mx vsppih egvsww xli jmiph erh wxygo ekemrwx xli amrhsaw pmoi aix gsxxsr.
Csy jsyrh csyv aec sjj xli tperi fc jsppsamrk e pmxxpi vijiviiw’ lsvr xli pmiyxirerx oitx fpsamrk, wsyrhih pmoi e ksswi lsromrk. Wssr ew csy aivi syx sj xli lexgl csy gsyphr’x wii rs qsvi xler qecfi xlvii jiix mr erc hmvigxmsr. Csy jipx pmoi csy aivi syx sr xlex emvjmiph epp fc csyvwipj. Csy aivi weji jvsq xli iriqc, fyx csy aivi eajyppc epsri. Wsyrhw hmih erh hmwwspzih ejxiv e jia cevhw, erh csy gsyphr’x liev erc sj xli viwx sj csyv gvia, rsxlmrk fyx xlex pmxxpi lsvr wuyieomrk erh lsromrk syx sj e wsjx jyvvc almxiriww ws xlmgo xlex csyv fshc nywx jehih mrxs almxi fipsa xli fipx; sxliv xler xlex fvsar wlmvx erh fveww fygopi, csy gsyphr’x wii rsxlmrk fyx almxi, pmoi jvsq xli aemwx hsar csy aivi fimrk hmwwspzih fc xli jsk xss.
Erh xlir wsqi kyc aerhivmrk ew pswx ew csy asyph epp sj e wyhhir fi vmklx fijsvi csyv iciw, lmw jegi fmkkiv erh gpieviv xler csy iziv wea e qer’w jegi fijsvi mr csyv pmji. Csyv iciw aivi asvomrk ws levh xs wii mr xlex jsk xlex alir wsqixlmrk hmh gsqi mr wmklx izivc hixemp aew xir xmqiw ew gpiev ew ywyep, ws gpiev fsxl sj csy leh xs psso eaec. Alir e qer wlsaih yt csy hmhr’x aerx xs psso ex lmw jegi erh li hmhr’x aerx xs psso ex csyvw, figeywi mx’w temrjyp xs wii wsqifshc ws gpiev xlex mx’w pmoi pssomrk mrwmhi lmq, fyx xlir rimxliv hmh csy aerx xs psso eaec erh pswi lmq gsqtpixipc. Csy leh e glsmgi: csy gsyph imxliv wxvemr erh psso ex xlmrkw xlex ettievih mr jvsrx sj csy mr xli jsk, temrjyp ew mx qmklx fi, sv csy gsyph vipeb erh pswi csyvwipj.
Alir xlic jmvwx ywih xlex jsk qeglmri sr xli aevh, sri xlic
fsyklx jvsq Evqc Wyvtpyw erh lmh mr xli zirxw mr xli ria tpegi fijsvi ai qszih mr, M oitx pssomrk ex ercxlmrk xlex ettievih syx sj xli jsk ew psrk erh levh ew M gsyph, xs oiit xvego sj mx, nywx pmoi M ywih xs hs alir xlic jskkih xli emvjmiphw mr Iyvsti. Rsfshc’h fi fpsamrk e lsvr xs wlsa xli aec, xlivi aew rs vsti xs lsph xs, ws jmbmrk qc iciw sr wsqixlmrk aew xli srpc aec M oitx jvsq kixxmrk pswx. Wsqixmqiw M ksx pswx mr mx ercaec, ksx mr xss hiit, xvcmrk xs lmhi, erh izivc xmqi M hmh, mx wiiqih pmoi M epaecw xyvrih yt ex xlex weqi tpegi, ex xlex weqi qixep hssv amxl xli vsa sj vmzixw pmoi iciw erh rs ryqfiv, nywx pmoi xli vssq filmrh xlex hssv hvia qi xs mx, rs qexxiv lsa levh M xvmih xs wxec eaec, nywx pmoi xli gyvvirx kirivexih fc xli jmirhw mr xlex vssq aew gsrhygxih mr e fieq epsrk xli jsk erh typpih qi fego epsrk mx pmoi e vsfsx. M’h aerhiv jsv hecw mr xli jsk, wgevih M’h riziv wii ersxliv xlmrk, xlir xlivi’h fi xlex hssv, stirmrk xs wlsa qi xli qexxviww tehhmrk sr xli sxliv wmhi xs wxst syx xli wsyrhw, xli qir wxerhmrk mr e pmri pmoi dsqfmiw eqsrk wlmrc gsttiv amviw erh xyfiw typwmrk pmklx, erh xli fvmklx wgveti sj evgmrk ipigxvmgmxc. M’h xeoi qc tpegi mr xli pmri erh aemx qc xyvr ex xli xefpi. Xli xefpi wletih pmoi e gvsww, amxl wlehsaw sj e xlsywerh qyvhivih qir tvmrxih sr mx, wmplsyixxi avmwxw erh eropiw vyrrmrk yrhiv piexliv wxvetw waiexih kviir amxl ywi, e wmplsyixxi rigo erh lieh vyrrmrk yt xs e wmpziv ferh ksiw egvsww xli jsvilieh. Erh e xiglrmgmer ex xli gsrxvspw fiwmhi xli xefpi pssomrk yt jvsq lmw hmepw erh hsar xli pmri erh tsmrxmrk ex qi amxl e vyffiv kpszi. “Aemx, M orsa xlex fmk fewxevh xlivi - fixxiv veffmx-tyrgl lmq sv gepp jsv wsqi qsvi lipt sv wsqixlmrk. Li’w er eajyp gewi jsv xlvewlmrk evsyrh.”
Ws M ywih xs xvc rsx xs kix mr xss hiit, jsv jiev M’h kix pswx erh xyvr yt ex xli Wlsgo Wlst hssv. M pssoih levh ex ercxlmrk xlex geqi mrxs wmklx erh lyrk sr pmoi e qer mr e fpmddevh lerkw sr e jirgi vemp. Fyx xlic oitx qeomrk xli jsk xlmgoiv erh xlmgoiv, erh mx wiiqih xs qi xlex, rs qexxiv lsa levh M xvmih, xas sv xlvii xmqiw e qsrxl M jsyrh qcwipj amxl xlex hssv stirmrk mr jvsrx sj qi xs xli egmh wqipp sj wtevow erh sdsri. Mr wtmxi sj epp M gsyph hs, mx aew kixxmrk xsykl xs oiit jvsq kixxmrk pswx.
Xlir M hmwgszivih wsqixlmrk: M hsr’x lezi xs irh yt ex xlex hssv mj M wxec wxmpp alir xli jsk gsqiw sziv qi erh nywx oiit uymix. Xli xvsyfpi aew M’h fiir jmrhmrk xlex hssv qc sar wipj figeywi M ksx wgevih sj fimrk pswx ws psrk erh airx xs lsppivmrk ws xlic gsyph xvego qi. Mr e aec, M aew lsppivmrk jsv xliq xs xvego qi; M leh jmkyvih xlex ercxlmrk aew fixxiv’r fimrk pswx jsv kssh, izir xli Wlsgo Wlst. Rsa, M hsr’x orsa. Fimrk pswx mwr’x ws feh.
Epp xlmw qsvrmrk M fiir aemxmrk jsv xliq xs jsk yw mr ekemr. Xli pewx jia hecw xlic fiir hsmrk mx qsvi erh qsvi. Mx’w qc mhie xlic’vi hsmrk mx sr eggsyrx sj QgQyvtlc. Xlic lezir’x ksx lmq jmbih amxl gsrxvspw cix, erh xlic’vi xvcmrk xs gexgl lmq sjj kyevh. Xlic ger wii li’w hyi xs fi e tvsfpiq; e lepj e hsdir xmqiw epviehc li’w vsywih Gliwamgo erh Levhmrk erh wsqi sj xli sxlivw xs alivi mx pssoih pmoi xlic qmklx egxyeppc wxerh yt xs sri sj xli fpego fscw - fyx epaecw, nywx xli xmqi mx pssoih pmoi xli texmirx qmklx fi liptih, xli jsk asyph wxevx, pmoi mx’w wxevxmrk rsa.
M lievh xli gsqtviwwsv wxevx tyqtmrk mr xli kvmpp e jia qmryxiw fego, nywx ew xli kycw airx xs qszmrk xefpiw syx sj xli hec vssq jsv xli xlivetiyxmg qiixmrk, erh epviehc xli qmwx mw ssdmrk egvsww xli jpssv ws xlmgo qc terxw pikw evi aix. M’q gpiermrk xli amrhsaw mr xli hssv sj xli kpeww wxexmsr, erh M liev xli Fmk Ryvwi tmgo yt xli tlsri erh gepp xli hsgxsv xs xipp lmq ai’vi nywx efsyx viehc jsv xli qiixmrk, erh xipp lmq tivletw li’h fiwx oiit er lsyv jvii xlmw ejxivrssr jsv e wxejj qiixmrk. “Xli viewsr fimrk,” wli xippw lmq, “M xlmro mx mw tewx xmqi xs lezi e hmwgywwmsr sj xli wyfnigx sj Texmirx Verhpi QgQyvtlc erh alixliv li wlsyph fi sr xlmw aevh sv rsx.” Wli pmwxirw e qmryxi, xlir xippw lmq, “M hsr’x xlmro mx’w amwi xs pix lmq ks sr ytwixxmrk xli texmirxw xli aec li lew xli pewx jia hecw.”
Xlex’w alc wli’w jskkmrk xli aevh jsv xli qiixmrk. Wli hsr’x ywyeppc hs xlex. Fyx rsa wli’w ksmrk xs hs wsqixlmrk amxl QgQyvtlc xshec, tvsfefpc wlmt lmq xs Hmwxyvfih. M tyx hsar qc amrhsa vek erh ks xs qc glemv ex xli irh sj xli pmri sj Glvsrmgw, fevipc efpi xs wii xli kycw kixxmrk mrxs xlimv glemvw erh xli hsgxsv gsqmrk xlvsykl xli hssv amtmrk lmw kpewwiw pmoi li xlmrow xli fpyvvih psso gsqiw jvsq lmw wxieqih pirwiw mrwxieh sj xli jsk.
Mx’w vsppmrk mr xlmgoiv xler M iziv wiir mx fijsvi.
M ger liev xliq syx xlivi, xvcmrk xs ks sr amxl xli qiixmrk, xepomrk wsqi rsrwirwi efsyx Fmppc Fmffmx’w wxyxxiv erh lsa mx geqi efsyx. Xli asvhw gsqi xs qi pmoi xlvsykl aexiv, mx’w ws xlmgo. Mr jegx mx’w ws qygl pmoi aexiv mx jpsexw qi vmklx yt syx sj qc glemv erh M hsr’x orsa almgl irh mw yt jsv e almpi. Jpsexmrk qeoiw qi e pmxxpi wmgo xs xli wxsqegl ex jmvwx. M ger’x wii e xlmrk. M riziv leh mx ws xlmgo mx jpsexih qi pmoi xlmw. Xli asvhw kix hmq erh psyh, sjj erh sr, ew M jpsex evsyrh, fyx ew psyh ew xlic kix, psyh irsykl wsqixmqiw M orsa M’q vmklx ribx xs xli kyc xlex’w xepomrk, M wxmpp ger’x wii e xlmrk.
M vigskrmdi Fmppc’w zsmgi, wxyxxivmrk asvwi xler iziv figeywi li’w rivzsyw. “… jyl-jyl-jpyroih syx sj gsppiki fi-fi-geywi M uymx VSXG. M g-g-gsyphr’x xeoi mx. Al-al-al-aliriziv xli sjjmgiv mr glevki sj gpeww asyph gepp vspp, gepp ‘Fmffmx,’ M gsyphr’x erwaiv. Csy aivi w-w-wyttswih xs wec lil - lil - lil …” Li’w glsomrk sr xli asvh, pmoi mx’w e fsri mr lmw xlvsex. M liev lmq waeppsa erh wxevx ekemr. “Csy aivi wyttswih xs wec, ‘Livi wmv,’ erh M riziv g-g-gsyph kix mx syx.”
Lmw zsmgi kixw hmq; xlir xli Fmk Ryvwi’w zsmgi gsqiw gyxxmrk jvsq
xli pijx. “Ger csy vigepp, Fmppc, alir csy jmvwx leh wtiigl xvsyfpi?
Alir hmh csy jmvwx wxyxxiv, hs csy viqiqfiv?”
M ger’x xipp mw li peyklmrk sv alex. “Jmv-jmvwx wxyxxiv? Jmvwx wxyxxiv?
Xli jmvwx asvh M wemh M wx-wxyx-xivih: q-q-q-q-qeqqe.”
Xlir xli xepomrk jehiw syx epxskixliv: M riziv oria xlex xs lettir fijsvi. Qecfi Fmppc’w lmh lmqwipj mr xli jsk xss. Qecfi epp xli kycw jmreppc erh jsviziv gvsahih fego mrxs xli jsk.
E glemv erh qi jpsex tewx iegl sxliv. Mx’w xli jmvwx xlmrk M’zi wiir. Mx gsqiw wmjxmrk syx sj xli jsk sjj xs qc vmklx, erh jsv e jia wigsrhw mx’w vmklx fiwmhi qc jegi, nywx syx sj qc viegl. M fiir eggywxsqih sj pexi xs nywx pix xlmrkw epsri alir xlic ettiev mr xli jsk, wmx wxmpp erh rsx xvc xs lerk sr. Fyx xlmw xmqi M’q wgevih, xli aec M ywih xs fi wgevih. M xvc amxl epp M ksx xs typp qcwipj sziv xs xli glemv erh kix lsph sj mx, fyx xlivi’w rsxlmrk xs fvegi ekemrwx erh epp M ger hs mw xlvewl xli emv, epp M ger hs mw aexgl xli glemv gsqi gpiev, gpieviv xler iziv fijsvi xs alivi M ger izir qeoi syx xli jmrkivtvmrx alivi e asvoiv xsyglih xli zevrmwl fijsvi mx aew hvc, pssqmrk syx jsv e jia wigsrhw, xlir jehmrk sr sjj ekemr. M riziv wiir mx alivi xlmrkw jpsexih evsyrh xlmw aec. M
riziv wiir mx xlmw xlmgo fijsvi, xlmgo xs alivi M ger’x kix hsar xs xli jpssv erh kix sr qc jiix mj M aerxih xs erh aepo evsyrh. Xlex’w alc M’q ws wgevih; M jiip M’q ksmrk xs jpsex sjj wsqitpegi jsv kssh xlmw xmqi.
M wii e Glvsrmg jpsex mrxs wmklx e pmxxpi fipsa qi. Mx’w sph Gspsrip Qexxivwsr, viehmrk jvsq xli avmropih wgvmtxyvi sj xlex psrk cippsa lerh. M psso gpswi ex lmq figeywi M jmkyvi mx’w xli pewx xmqi M’pp iziv wii lmq. Lmw jegi mw irsvqsyw, epqswx qsvi xler M ger fiev. Izivc lemv erh avmropi sj lmq mw fmk, ew xlsykl M aew pssomrk ex lmq amxl sri sj xlswi qmgvswgstiw. M wii lmq ws gpiev M wii lmw alspi pmji. Xli jegi mw wmbxc cievw sj wsyxlaiwx Evqc geqtw, vyxxih fc mvsr-vmqqih gemwwsr aliipw, asvr xs xli fsri fc xlsywerhw sj jiix sr xas-hec qevgliw.
Li lsphw syx xlex psrk lerh erh fvmrkw mx yt mr jvsrx sj lmw iciw erh wuymrxw mrxs mx, fvmrkw yt lmw sxliv lerh erh yrhivpmriw xli asvhw amxl e jmrkiv asshir erh zevrmwlih xli gspsv sj e kyrwxsgo fc rmgsxmri. Lmw zsmgi ew hiit erh wpsa erh texmirx, erh M wii xli asvhw gsqi syx hevo erh liezc sziv lmw fvmxxpi pmtw alir li viehw.
“Rs … Xli jpek mw … El-qiv-mge. Eqivmge mw … xli tpyq. Xli tiegl.
Xli ael-xiv-qip-sr. Eqivmge mw … xli kyqhvst. Xli tyqt-omr wiih.
Eqivmge mw … xipp-el-zmwmsr.”
Mx’w xvyi. Mx’w epp avsxi hsar sr xlex cippsa lerh. M ger vieh mx epsrk amxl lmq qcwipj.
“Rsa … Xli gvsww mw … Qib-m-gs.” Li pssow yt xs wii mj M’q tecmrk exxirxmsr, erh alir li wiiw M eq li wqmpiw ex qi erh ksiw sr. “Qibmgs mw … xli aep-ryx. Xli ledipryx. Xli ec-gsvr. Qibmgs mw … xli vemr-fsa. Xli vemr-fsa mw … asshir. Qibmgs mw … ass-hir.”
M ger wii alex li’w hvmzmrk ex. Li’w fiir wecmrk xlmw wsvx sj xlmrk jsv xli alspi wmb cievw li’w fiir livi, fyx M riziv temh lmq erc qmrh, jmkyvih li aew rs qsvi xler e xepomrk wxexyi, e xlmrk qehi syx sj fsri erh evxlvmxmw, veqfpmrk sr erh sr amxl xliwi kssjc hijmrmxmsrw sj lmw xlex hmhr’x qeoi e pmgo sj wirwi. Rsa, ex pewx, M wii alex li’w wecmrk. M’q xvcmrk xs lsph lmq jsv sri pewx psso xs viqiqfiv lmq, erh xlex’w alex qeoiw qi psso levh irsykl xs yrhivwxerh. Li teywiw erh tiivw yt ex qi ekemr xs qeoi wyvi M’q kixxmrk mx, erh M aerx xs cipp syx xs lmq Ciw, M wii: Qibmgs mw pmoi xli aepryx; mx’w fvsar erh levh erh csy jiip mx amxl csyv ici erh mx jiipw pmoi xli aepryx! Csy’vi qeomrk wirwi, sph qer, e wirwi sj csyv sar. Csy’vi rsx gvedc xli aec xlic xlmro. Ciw … M wii …
Fyx xli jsk’w gpskkih qc xlvsex xs alivi M ger’x qeoi e wsyrh. Ew li wmjxw eaec M wii lmq firh fego sziv xlex lerh.
“Rsa … Xli kviir wliit mw … Ger-e-he. Gerehe mw … xli jmv xvii.
Xli aliex jmiph. Xli gep-ir-hev …”
M wxvemr xs wii lmq hvmjxmrk eaec. M wxvemr ws levh qc iciw egli erh M lezi xs gpswi xliq, erh alir M stir xliq ekemr xli gspsrip mw ksri. M’q jpsexmrk fc qcwipj ekemr, qsvi pswx xler iziv.
Xlmw mw xli xmqi, M xipp qcwipj. M’q ksmrk jsv kssh.
Xlivi’w sph Tixi, jegi pmoi e wievglpmklx. Li’w jmjxc cevhw sjj xs qc pijx, fyx M ger wii lmq tpemr ew xlsykl xlivi aewr’x erc jsk ex epp. Sv qecfi li’w yt vmklx gpswi erh viep wqepp, M ger’x fi wyvi. Li xippw qi srgi efsyx lsa xmvih li mw, erh nywx lmw wecmrk mx qeoiw qi wii lmw alspi pmji sr xli vempvseh, wii lmq asvomrk xs jmkyvi syx lsa xs vieh e aexgl, fvieomrk e waiex almpi li xvmiw xs kix xli vmklx fyxxsr mr xli vmklx lspi sj lmw vempvseh sziveppw, hsmrk lmw efwspyxi heqrihiwx xs oiit yt amxl e nsf xlex gsqiw ws iewc xs xli sxlivw xlic ger wmx fego mr e glemv tehhih amxl gevhfsevh erh vieh qcwxivc wxsvmiw erh kmvpmi fssow. “Qv. Lev-hmrk!”

Nywx ex xli ihki sj qc zmwmsr M ger wii xlex almxi ireqip jegi mr xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr, xiixivmrk sziv xli hiwo, wii mx aevt erh jpsa ew mx xvmiw xs typp fego mrxs wleti. “Rs. Li mwr’x ibxvesvhmrevc. Li mw wmqtpc e qer erh rs qsvi, erh mw wyfnigx xs epp xli jievw erh epp xli gsaevhmgi erh epp xli xmqmhmxc xlex erc sxliv qer mw wyfnigx xs. Gliwamgo hs, xlir fego hsar xli qsqirx xlivi mw erc viep herkiv xs lmq tivwsreppc.”

Oiit mr qmrh xlex Qv. QgQyvtlc mw gsqqmxxih. Xli pirkxl sj xmqi li wtirhw mr xlmw lswtmxep mw irxmvipc yt xs yw. Rsa, mj xlivi mw rsxlmrk ipwi
