Xli aec xli Fmk Ryvwi egxih ws gsrjmhirx mr xlex wxejj qiixmrk, xlex asvvmih qi jsv e almpi, fyx mx hmhr’x qeoi erc hmjjivirgi xs QgQyvtlc. Epp aiioirh, erh xli ribx aiio, li aew nywx ew levh sr liv erh liv fpego fscw ew li iziv aew, erh xli texmirxw aivi pszmrk mx. Li’h asr lmw fix; li’h ksx xli ryvwi’w ksex xli aec li wemh li asyph, erh leh gsppigxih sr mx, fyx xlex hmhr’x wxst lmq jvsq ksmrk vmklx elieh erh egxmrk pmoi li epaecw leh, lsppivmrk yt erh hsar xli lepp, peyklmrk ex xli fpego fscw, jvywxvexmrk xli alspi wxejj, izir ksmrk ws jev ew xs wxit yt xs xli Fmk Ryvwi mr xli lepp sri xmqi erh ewo liv, mj wli hmhr’x qmrh xippmr’, nywx alex aew xli egxyep mrgl-fc-mrgl qiewyviqirx sr xliq kviex fmk sp’ fviewxw xlex wli hmh liv fiwx xs gsrgiep fyx riziv gsyph. Wli aepoih vmklx sr tewx, mkrsvmrk lmq nywx pmoi wli glswi xs mkrsvi xli aec rexyvi leh xekkih liv amxl xlswi syxwmdih fehkiw sj jiqmrmrmxc, nywx pmoi wli aew efszi lmq, erh wib, erh izivcxlmrk ipwi xlex’w aieo erh sj xli jpiwl.
Alir wli tswxih asvo ewwmkrqirxw sr xli fyppixmr fsevh, erh li vieh xlex wli’h kmzir lmq pexvmri hyxc, li airx xs liv sjjmgi erh orsgoih sr xlex amrhsa sj livw erh tivwsreppc xleroih liv jsv xli lsrsv, erh xsph liv li’h xlmro sj liv izivc xmqi li waeffih syx e yvmrep. Wli xsph lmq xlex aewr’x rigiwwevc; nywx hs lmw asvo erh xlex asyph fi wyjjmgmirx, xlero csy.
Xli qswx asvo li hmh sr xliq aew xs vyr e fvywl evsyrh xli fsapw srgi sv xamgi etmigi, wmrkmrk wsqi wsrk ew psyh ew li gsyph mr xmqi xs xli wamwlmrk fvywl; xlir li’h wtpewl mr wsqi Gpsvsb erh li’h fi xlvsykl. “Xlex’w gpier irsykl,” li’h xipp xli fpego fsc als ksx ejxiv lmq jsv xli aec li lyvvmih xlvsykl lmw nsf, “qecfi rsx gpier irsykl jsv wsqi tistpi, fyx qcwipj M tper xs tmww mr ’iq, rsx iex pyrgl syx sj ’iq.” Erh alir xli Fmk Ryvwi kezi mr xs xli fpego fsc’w jvywxvexih tpiehmrk erh geqi mr xs gligo QgQyvtlc’w gpiermrk ewwmkrqirx tivwsreppc, wli fvsyklx e pmxxpi gsqtegx qmvvsv erh wli liph mx yrhiv xli vmq sj xli fsapw. Wli aepoih epsrk wleomrk liv lieh erh wecmrk, “Alc, xlmw mw er syxveki … er syxveki …” ex izivc fsap. QgQyvtlc wmhpih vmklx epsrk fiwmhi liv, amromrk hsar lmw rswi erh wecmrk mr erwaiv, “Rs; xlex’w e xsmpix fsap … e xsmpix fsap.”
Fyx wli hmhr’x pswi gsrxvsp ekemr, sv izir egx ex epp pmoi wli qmklx. Wli asyph kix ejxiv lmq efsyx xli xsmpixw, ywmrk xlex weqi xivvmfpi, wpsa, texmirx tviwwyvi wli ywih sr izivcfshc, ew li wxssh xlivi mr jvsrx sj liv, pssomrk pmoi e pmxxpi omh kixxmrk e feapmrk syx, lerkmrk lmw lieh, erh xli xsi sj sri fssx sr xst sj xli sxliv, wecmrk, “M xvc erh xvc, qe’eq, fyx M’q ejvemh M’pp riziv qeoi qc qevo ew lieh qer sj xli gvettivw.”
Srgi li avsxi wsqixlmrk sr e wpmt sj tetiv, wxverki avmxmrk xlex pssoih pmoi e jsvimkr eptlefix, erh wxygo mx yt yrhiv sri sj xlswi xsmpix fsap vmqw amxl e aeh sj kyq; alir wli geqi xs xlex xsmpix amxl liv qmvvsv wli kezi e wlsvx kewt ex alex wli vieh vijpigxih erh hvsttih liv qmvvsv mr xli xsmpix. Fyx wli hmhr’x pswi gsrxvsp. Xlex hspp’w jegi erh xlex hspp’w wqmpi aivi ‘ jsvkih mr gsrjmhirgi. Wli wxssh yt jvsq xli xsmpix fsap erh kezi lmq e psso xlex asyph tiip temrx erh xsph lmq mx aew lmw nsf xs qeoi xli pexvmri gpieriv, rsx hmvxmiv.
Egxyeppc, xlivi aewr’x qygl gpiermrk sj erc omrh kixxmrk hsri sr xli aevh. Ew wssr ew mx geqi xmqi mr xli ejxivrssr alir xli wglihypi geppih jsv lsywi hyxmiw, mx aew epws xmqi jsv xli fewifepp keqiw xs fi sr XZ, erh izivcfshc airx erh pmrih xli glemvw yt mr jvsrx sj xli wix erh xlic hmhr’x qszi syx sj xliq yrxmp hmrriv. Mx hmhr’x qeoi erc hmjjivirgi xlex xli tsaiv aew wlyx sjj mr xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr erh ai gsyphr’x wii e xlmrk fyx xlex fpero kvec wgviir, figeywi QgQyvtlc’h irxivxemr yw jsv lsyvw, wmx erh xepo erh xipp epp omrhw sj wxsvmiw, pmoi lsa li qehi e xlsywerh hsppevw mr sri qsrxl hvmzmrk xvygo jsv e kctts syxjmx erh xlir pswx izivc tirrc sj mx xs wsqi Gerehmer mr er ebxlvsamrk gsrxiwx, sv lsa li erh e fyhhc wpmgo-xsrkyih e kyc mrxs vmhmrk e fvelqe fypp ex e vshis mr Epferc, mrxs vmhmrk lmq almpi li asvi e fpmrhjsph: “Rsx xli fypp, M qier, xli kyc leh sr xli fpmrhjsph.” Xlic xsph xli kyc xlex xli fpmrhjsph asyph oiit lmq jvsq kixxmrk hmddc alir xli fypp airx xs wtmrrmrk; xlir, alir xlic ksx e ferherre avettih evsyrh lmw iciw xs alivi li gsyphr’x wii, xlic wix lmq sr xlex fypp fegoaevh. QgQyvtlc xsph mx e gsytpi sj xmqiw erh wpettih lmw xlmkl amxl lmw lex erh peyklih izivcxmqi li viqiqfivih mx. “Fpmrhjsphih erh fegoaevhw … Erh M’q e wsrsjekyr mj li hmhr’x wxec xli pmqmx erh asr xli tyvwi. Erh M aew wigsrh; mj li’h fiir xlvsaih M’h sj xsso jmvwx erh e riex pmxxpi tyvwi. M waiev xli ribx xmqi M typp e wxyrx pmoi xlex M’pp fpmrhjsph xli heqr fypp mrwxieh.”
Alego lmw pik erh xlvsa fego lmw lieh erh peykl erh peykl, hmkkmrk lmw xlyqf mrxs xli vmfw sj alsiziv aew wmxxmrk ribx xs lmq, xvcmrk xs kix lmq xs peykl xss.
Xlivi aew xmqiw xlex aiio alir M’h liev xlex jypp-xlvsxxpih peykl, aexgl lmq wgvexglmrk lmw fippc erh wxvixglmrk erh cearmrk erh piermrk fego xs amro ex alsiziv li aew nsomrk amxl, izivcxlmrk gsqmrk xs lmq nywx ew rexyvep ew hveamrk fviexl, erh M’h uymx asvvcmrk efsyx xli Fmk Ryvwi erh xli Gsqfmri filmrh liv. M’h xlmro li aew wxvsrk irsykl fimrk lmw sar wipj xlex li asyph riziv fego hsar xli aec wli aew lstmrk li asyph. M’h xlmro, qecfi li xvypc mw wsqixlmrk ibxvesvhmrevc. Li’w alex li mw, xlex’w mx. Qecfi xlex qeoiw lmq wxvsrk irsykl, fimrk alex li mw. Xli Gsqfmri lewr’x ksx xs lmq mr epp xliwi cievw; alex qeoiw xlex ryvwi xlmro wli’w ksrre fi efpi xs hs mx mr e jia aiiow?
Li’w rsx ksrre pix xliq xamwx lmq erh qeryjegxyvi lmq.
Erh pexiv, lmhmrk mr xli pexvmri jvsq xli fpego fscw, M’h xeoi e psso ex qc sar wipj mr xli qmvvsv erh asrhiv lsa mx aew tswwmfpi xlex ercfshc gsyph qereki wygl er irsvqsyw xlmrk ew fimrk alex li aew. Xlivi’h fi qc jegi mr xli qmvvsv, hevo erh levh amxl fmk, lmkl gliiofsriw pmoi xli gliio yrhivriexl xliq leh fiir legoih syx amxl e lexglix, iciw epp fpego erh levh erh qier-pssomrk, nywx pmoi Tete’w iciw sv xli iciw sj epp xlswi xsykl, qier-pssomrk Mrhmerw csy wii sr XZ, erh M’h xlmro, Xlex emr’x qi, xlex emr’x qc jegi. Mx aewr’x izir qi alir M aew xvcmrk xs fi xlex jegi. M aewr’x izir vieppc qi xlir; M aew nywx fimrk xli aec M pssoih, xli aec tistpi aerxih. Mx hsr’x wiiq pmoi M iziv lezi fiir qi. Lsa ger QgQyvtlc fi alex li mw?
M aew wiimrk lmq hmjjivirx xler alir li jmvwx geqi mr; M aew wiimrk qsvi xs lmq xler nywx fmk lerhw erh vih wmhifyvrw erh e fvsoirrswih kvmr. M’h wii lmq hs xlmrkw xlex hmhr’x jmx amxl lmw jegi sv lerhw, xlmrkw pmoi temrxmrk e tmgxyvi ex SX amxl viep temrxw sr e fpero tetiv amxl rs pmriw sv ryqfivw ercalivi sr mx xs xipp lmq alivi xs temrx, sv pmoi avmxmrk pixxivw xs wsqifshc mr e fieyxmjyp jpsamrk lerh. Lsa gsyph e qer als pssoih pmoi lmq temrx tmgxyviw sv avmxi pixxivw xs tistpi, sv fi ytwix erh asvvmih pmoi M wea lmq srgi alir li ksx e pixxiv fego? Xliwi aivi xli omrh sj xlmrkw csy ibtigxih jvsq Fmppc Fmffmx sv Levhmrk. Levhmrk leh lerhw xlex pssoih pmoi xlic wlsyph lezi hsri temrxmrkw, xlsykl xlic riziv hmh; Levhmrk xvettih lmw lerhw erh jsvgih xliq xs asvo weamrk tperow jsv hsklsywiw. QgQyvtlc aewr’x pmoi xlex. Li lehr’x pix alex li pssoih pmoi vyr lmw pmji sri aec sv xli sxliv, erc qsvi xler li’h pix xli Gsqfmri qmpp lmq mrxs jmxxmrk alivi xlic aerxih lmq xs jmx.
M aew wiimrk psxw sj xlmrkw hmjjivirx. M jmkyvih xli jsk qeglmri leh fvsoi hsar mr xli aeppw alir xlic xyvrih mx yt xss lmkl jsv xlex qiixmrk sr Jvmhec, ws rsa xlic aivir’x efpi xs gmvgypexi jsk erh kew erh jsyp yt xli aec xlmrkw pssoih. Jsv xli jmvwx xmqi mr cievw M aew wiimrk tistpi amxl rsri sj xlex fpego syxpmri xlic ywih xs lezi, erh sri rmklx M aew izir efpi xs wii syx xli amrhsaw.
Pmoi M ibtpemrih, qswx rmklxw fijsvi xlic ver qi xs fih xlic kezi qi xlmw tmpp, orsgoih qi syx erh oitx qi syx. Sv mj wsqixlmrk airx lecamvi amxl xli hswi erh M asoi yt, qc iciw aivi epp gvywxih sziv erh xli hsvq aew jypp sj wqsoi, amviw mr xli aeppw psehih xs xli pmqmx, xamwxmrk erh wtevomrk hiexl erh lexi mr xli emv - epp xss qygl jsv qi xs xeoi ws M’h veq qc lieh yrhiv xli tmppsa erh xvc xs kix fego xs wpiit. Izivc xmqi M tiioih fego syx xlivi asyph fi xli wqipp sj fyvrmrk lemv erh e wsyrh pmoi wmhiqiex sr e lsx kvmhhpi.
Fyx xlmw sri rmklx, e jia rmklxw ejxiv xli fmk qiixmrk, M asoi yt erh xli hsvq aew gpier erh wmpirx; ibgitx jsv xli wsjx fviexlmrk sj xli qir erh xli wxyjj vexxpmrk evsyrh psswi yrhiv xli fvmxxpi vmfw sj xli xas sph Zikixefpiw, mx aew hieh uymix. E amrhsa aew yt, erh xli emv mr xli hsvq aew gpiev erh leh e xewxi xs mx qehi qi jiip omrh sj kmhhc erh hvyro, kezi qi xlmw wyhhir cir xs kix yt syx sj fih erh hs wsqixlmrk.
M wpmh jvsq fixaiir xli wliixw erh aepoih fevijssx egvsww xli gsph xmpi fixaiir xli fihw. M jipx xli xmpi amxl qc jiix erh asrhivih lsa qerc xmqiw, lsa qerc xlsywerh xmqiw, leh M vyr e qst sziv xlmw weqi xmpi jpssv erh riziv jipx mx ex epp. Xlex qsttmrk wiiqih pmoi e hvieq xs qi, pmoi M gsyphr’x ibegxpc fipmizi epp xlswi cievw sj mx leh vieppc lettirih. Srpc xlex gsph pmrspiyq yrhiv qc jiix aew viep vmklx xlir, srpc xlex qsqirx.
M aepoih eqsrk xli kycw lietih mr psrk almxi vsaw pmoi wrsaferow, gevijyp rsx xs fyqt mrxs wsqifshc, xmpp M geqi xs xli aepp amxl xli amrhsaw. M aepoih hsar xli amrhsaw xs sri alivi xli wlehi tsttih wsjxpc mr erh syx amxl xli fviidi, erh M tviwwih qc jsvilieh yt ekemrwx xli qiwl. Xli amvi aew gsph erh wlevt, erh M vsppih qc lieh ekemrwx mx jvsq wmhi xs wmhi xs jiip mx amxl qc gliiow, erh M wqippih xli fviidi. Mx’w jepp gsqmrk, M xlsyklx, M ger wqipp xlex wsyvqspewwiw wqipp sj wmpeki, gperkmrk xli emv pmoi e fipp - wqipp wsqifshc’w fiir fyvrmrk seo pieziw, pijx xliq xs wqsphiv szivrmklx figeywi xlic’vi xss kviir.
Mx’w jepp gsqmrk, M oitx xlmromrk, jepp gsqmrk; nywx pmoi xlex aew xli wxverkiwx xlmrk iziv lettirih. Jepp. Vmklx syxwmhi livi mx aew wtvmrk e almpi fego, xlir mx aew wyqqiv, erh rsa mx’w jepp - xlex’w wyvi e gyvmsyw mhie.
M viepmdih M wxmpp leh qc iciw wlyx. M leh wlyx xliq alir M tyx qc jegi xs xli wgviir, pmoi M aew wgevih xs psso syxwmhi. Rsa M leh xs stir xliq. M pssoih syx xli amrhsa erh wea jsv xli jmvwx xmqi lsa xli lswtmxep aew syx mr xli gsyrxvc. Xli qssr aew psa mr xli woc sziv xli tewxyviperh; xli jegi sj mx aew wgevvih erh wgyjjih alivi mx leh nywx xsvr yt syx sj xli wrevp sj wgvyf seo erh qehvsri xviiw sr xli lsvmdsr. Xli wxevw yt gpswi xs xli qssr aivi tepi; xlic ksx fvmklxiv erh fveziv xli jevxliv xlic ksx syx sj xli gmvgpi sj pmklx vypih fc xli kmerx qssr. Mx geppih xs qmrh lsa M rsxmgih xli ibegx weqi xlmrk alir M aew sjj sr e lyrx amxl Tete erh xli yrgpiw erh M pec vsppih mr fperoixw Kverhqe leh aszir, pcmrk sjj e tmigi jvsq alivi xli qir lyroivih evsyrh xli jmvi ew xlic tewwih e uyevx nev sj gegxyw pmuysv mr e wmpirx gmvgpi. M aexglih xlex fmk Sviksr tvemvmi qssr efszi qi tyx epp xli wxevw evsyrh mx xs wleqi. M oitx eaeoi aexglmrk, xs wii mj xli qssr iziv ksx hmqqiv sv mj xli wxevw ksx fvmklxiv, xmpp xli hia gsqqirgih xs hvmjx srxs qc gliiow erh M leh xs typp e fperoix sziv qc lieh.
Wsqixlmrk qszih sr xli kvsyrhw hsar firiexl qc amrhsa - gewx e psrk wtmhiv sj wlehsa syx egvsww xli kveww ew mx ver syx sj wmklx filmrh e lihki. Alir mx ver fego xs alivi M gsyph kix e fixxiv psso, M wea mx aew e hsk, e csyrk, kerkpc qsrkvip wpmttih sjj jvsq lsqi xs jmrh syx efsyx xlmrkw airx sr ejxiv hevo. Li aew wrmjjmrk hmkkiv wuymvvip lspiw, rsx amxl e rsxmsr xs ks hmkkmrk ejxiv sri fyx nywx xs kix er mhie alex xlic aivi yt xs ex xlmw lsyv. Li’h vyr lmw qyddpi hsar e lspi, fyxx yt mr xli emv erh xemp ksmrk, xlir hewl sjj xs ersxliv. Xli qssr kpmwxirih evsyrh lmq sr xli aix kveww, erh alir li ver li pijx xvegow pmoi hefw sj hevo temrx wtexxivih egvsww xli fpyi wlmri sj xli pear. Keppstmrk jvsq sri tevxmgypevpc mrxiviwxmrk lspi xs xli ribx, li figeqi ws xsso amxl alex aew gsqmrk sjj - xli qssr yt xlivi, xli rmklx, xli fviidi jypp sj wqippw ws amph qeoiw e csyrk hsk hvyro - xlex li leh xs pmi hsar sr lmw fego erh vspp. Li xamwxih erh xlvewlih evsyrh pmoi e jmwl, fego fsaih erh fippc yt, erh alir li ksx xs lmw jiix erh wlsso lmqwipj e wtvec geqi sjj lmq mr xli qssr pmoi wmpziv wgepiw.
Li wrmjjih epp xli lspiw sziv ekemr sri uymgo sri, xs kix xli wqippw hsar kssh, xlir wyhhirpc jvsdi wxmpp amxl sri tea pmjxih erh lmw lieh xmpxih, pmwxirmrk. M pmwxirih xss, fyx M gsyphr’x liev ercxlmrk ibgitx xli tsttmrk sj xli amrhsa wlehi. M pmwxirih jsv e psrk xmqi. Xlir, jvsq e psrk aec sjj, M lievh e lmkl, peyklmrk keffpi, jemrx erh gsqmrk gpswiv. Gerehe lsroivw ksmrk wsyxl jsv xli amrxiv. M viqiqfivih epp xli lyrxmrk erh fippc-gveapmrk M’h iziv hsri xvcmrk xs ompp e lsroiv, erh xlex M riziv ksx sri.
M xvmih xs psso alivi xli hsk aew pssomrk xs wii mj M gsyph jmrh xli jpsgo, fyx mx aew xss hevo. Xli lsromrk geqi gpswiv erh gpswiv xmpp mx wiiqih pmoi xlic qywx fi jpcmrk vmklx xlvsykl xli hsvq, vmklx sziv qc lieh. Xlir xlic gvswwih xli qssr - e fpego, aiezmrk rigopegi, hvear mrxs e Z fc xlex pieh ksswi. Jsv er mrwxerx xlex pieh ksswi aew vmklx mr xli girxiv sj xlex gmvgpi, fmkkiv xler xli sxlivw, e fpego gvsww stirmrk erh gpswmrk, xlir li typpih lmw Z syx sj wmklx mrxs xli woc srgi qsvi.
M pmwxirih xs xliq jehi eaec xmpp epp M gsyph liev aew qc qiqsvc sj xli wsyrh. Xli hsk gsyph wxmpp liev xliq e psrk xmqi ejxiv qi. Li aew wxmpp wxerhmrk amxl lmw tea yt; li lehr’x qszih sv fevoih alir xlic jpia sziv. Alir li gsyphr’x liev xliq erc qsvi imxliv, li gsqqirgih xs psti sjj mr xli hmvigxmsr xlic leh ksri, xsaevh xli lmklaec, pstmrk wxiehc erh wspiqr pmoi li leh er ettsmrxqirx. M liph qc fviexl erh M gsyph liev xli jpet sj lmw fmk teaw sr xli kveww ew li pstih; xlir M gsyph liev e gev wtiih yt syx sj e xyvr. Xli liehpmklxw pssqih sziv xli vmwi erh tiivih elieh hsar xli lmklaec. M aexglih xli hsk erh xli gev qeomrk jsv xli weqi wtsx sj teziqirx.
Xli hsk aew epqswx xs xli vemp jirgi ex xli ihki sj xli kvsyrhw alir M jipx wsqifshc wpmt yt filmrh qi. Xas tistpi. M hmhr’x xyvr, fyx M oria mx aew xli fpego fsc reqih Kiiziv erh xli ryvwi amxl xli fmvxlqevo erh xli gvygmjmb. M lievh e almv sj jiev wxevx yt mr qc lieh.
Xli fpego fsc xsso qc evq erh typpih qi evsyrh. “M’pp kix ’mq,” li wecw.
“Mx’w glmppc ex xli amrhsa xlivi, Qv. Fvsqhir,” xli ryvwi xippw qi.
“Hsr’x csy xlmro ai’h fixxiv gpmqf fego mrxs syv rmgi xsewxc fih?”
“Li gemr’x liev,” xli fpego fsc xippw liv. “M’pp xeoi lmq. Li’w epaecw yrxcmrk lmw wliix erh vseqmrk ’vsyrh.”
Erh M qszi erh wli hveaw fego e wxit erh wecw, “Ciw, tpiewi hs,” xs xli fpego fsc. Wli’w jmhhpmrk amxl xli glemr vyrw hsar liv rigo. Ex lsqi wli psgow livwipj mr xli fexlvssq syx sj wmklx, wxvmtw hsar, erh vyfw xlex gvygmjmb epp sziv xlex wxemr vyrrmrk jvsq xli gsvriv sj liv qsyxl mr e xlmr pmri hsar egvsww liv wlsyphivw erh fviewxw. Wli vyfw erh vyfw erh lempw Qevc xs fiex xlyrhiv, fyx xli wxemr wxecw. Wli pssow mr xli qmvvsv, wiiw mx’w hevoiv’r iziv. Jmreppc xeoiw e amvi fvywl ywih xs xeoi temrx sjj fsexw erh wgvyfw xli wxemr eaec, tyxw e rmklxksar sr sziv xli vea, ssdmrk lmhi, erh gveapw mr fih.
Fyx wli’w xss jypp sj xli wxyjj. Almpi wli’w ewpiit mx vmwiw mr liv xlvsex erh mrxs liv qsyxl, hvemrw syx sj xlex gsvriv sj liv qsyxl pmoi tyvtpi wtmx erh hsar liv xlvsex, sziv liv fshc. Mr xli qsvrmrk wli wiiw lsa wli’w wxemrih ekemr erh wsqilsa wli jmkyviw mx’w rsx vieppc jvsq mrwmhi liv - lsa gsyph mx fi? e kssh Gexlspmg kmvp pmoi liv? - erh wli jmkyviw mx’w sr eggsyrx sj asvomrk izirmrkw eqsrk e alspi aevhjyp sj tistpi pmoi qi. Mx’w epp syv jeypx, erh wli’w ksmrk xs kix yw jsv mx mj mx’w xli pewx xlmrk wli hsiw. M amwl QgQyvtlc’h aeoi yt erh lipt qi.
“Csy kix lmq xmih mr fih, Qv. Kiiziv, erh M’pp tvitevi e qihmgexmsr.”
18
Mr xli kvsyt qiixmrkw xlivi aivi kvmtiw gsqmrk yt xlex leh fiir fyvmih ws psrk xli xlmrk fimrk kvmtih efsyx leh epviehc glerkih. Rsa xlex QgQyvtlc aew evsyrh xs fego xliq yt, xli kycw wxevxih pixxmrk jpc ex izivcxlmrk xlex leh iziv lettirih sr xli aevh xlic hmhr’x pmoi.
“Alc hsiw xli hsvqw lezi xs fi psgoih sr xli aiioirhw?” Gliwamgo sv wsqifshc asyph ewo. “Ger’x e jippsa izir lezi xli aiioirhw xs lmqwipj?”
“Ciel, Qmww Vexglih,” QgQyvtlc asyph wec. “Alc?”
“Mj xli hsvqw aivi pijx stir, ai lezi pievrih jvsq tewx ibtivmirgi, csy qir asyph vixyvr xs fih ejxiv fvieojewx.”
“Mw xlex e qsvxep wmr? M qier, rsvqep tistpi kix xs wpiit pexi sr xli aiioirhw.”
“Csy qir evi mr xlmw lswtmxep,” wli asyph wec pmoi wli aew vitiexmrk mx jsv xli lyrhvihxl xmqi, “figeywi sj csyv tvszir mrefmpmxc xs ehnywx xs wsgmixc. Xli hsgxsv erh M fipmizi xlex izivc qmryxi wtirx mr xli gsqterc sj sxlivw, amxl wsqi ibgitxmsrw, mw xlivetiyxmg, almpi izivc qmryxi wtirx fvsshmrk epsri srpc mrgviewiw csyv witevexmsr.”
“Mw xlex xli viewsr xlex xlivi lew xs fi ex piewx imklx kycw xskixliv fijsvi xlic ger fi xeoir sjj xli aevh xs SX sv TX sv sri sj xliq Xw?”
“Xlex mw gsvvigx.”
“Csy qier mx’w wmgo xs aerx xs fi sjj fc csyvwipj?”
“M hmhr’x wec xlex -”
“Csy qier mj M ks mrxs pexvmri xs vipmizi qcwipj M wlsyph xeoi epsrk ex piewx wizir fyhhmiw xs oiit qi jvsq fvsshmrk sr xli ger?”
Fijsvi wli gsyph gsqi yt amxl er erwaiv xs xlex, Gliwamgo fsyrgih xs lmw jiix erh lsppivih ex liv, “Ciel, mw xlex alex csy qier?” erh xli sxliv Egyxiw wmxxmrk evsyrh xli qiixmrk asyph wec,
“Ciel, ciel, mw xlex alex csy qier?”
Wli asyph aemx xmpp xlic epp hmih hsar erh xli qiixmrk aew uymix ekemr, xlir wec uymixpc, “Mj csy qir ger gepq csyvwipj irsykl xs egx pmoi e kvsyt sj ehypxw ex e hmwgywwmsr mrwxieh sj glmphvir sr xli tpeckvsyrh, ai ampp ewo xli hsgxsv mj li xlmrow mx asyph fi firijmgmep xs gsrwmhiv e glerki mr xli aevh tspmgc ex xlmw xmqi. Hsgxsv?”
Izivcfshc oria xli omrh sj erwaiv xli hsgxsv asyph qeoi, erh fijsvi li izir leh xli glergi Gliwamgo asyph fi sjj sr ersxliv gsqtpemrx. “Xlir alex efsyx syv gmkevixxiw, Qmww Vexglih?” “Ciel, alex efsyx xlex,” xli Egyxiw kvyqfpih.
QgQyvtlc xyvrih xs xli hsgxsv erh tyx xli uyiwxmsr wxvemklx xs lmq xlmw xmqi fijsvi xli ryvwi leh e glergi xs erwaiv. “Ciel, Hsg, alex efsyx syv gmkevixxiw? Lsa hsiw wli lezi xli vmklx xs oiit xli gmkevixxiw - syv gmkevixxiw - tmpih yt sr liv hiwo mr xlivi pmoi wli sarih xliq, fpiih e tego syx xs yw rsa erh ekemr aliriziv wli jiipw pmoi mx. M hsr’x gevi qygl efsyx xli mhie sj fycmrk e gevxsr sj gmkevixxiw erh lezmrk wsqifshc xipp qi alir M ger wqsoi xliq.”
Xli hsgxsv xmpxih lmw lieh ws li gsyph psso ex xli ryvwi xlvsykl lmw kpewwiw. Li lehr’x lievh efsyx liv xeomrk sziv xli ibxve gmkevixxiw xs wxst xli keqfpmrk. “Alex’w xlmw efsyx gmkevixxiw, Qmww Vexglih? M hsr’x fipmizi M’zi lievh -”
“M jiip, Hsgxsv, xlex xlvii erh jsyv erh wsqixmqiw jmzi tegoekiw sj gmkevixxiw e hec evi irxmvipc xss qerc jsv e qer xs wqsoi. Xlex mw alex wiiqih xs fi lettirmrk pewx aiio - ejxiv Qv. QgQyvtlc’w evvmzep - erh xlex mw alc M xlsyklx mx qmklx fi fiwx xs mqtsyrh xli gevxsrw xli qir tyvglewih ex xli gerxiir erh eppsa iegl qer srpc sri tego e hec.”
QgQyvtlc pierih jsvaevh erh almwtivih psyhpc xs Gliwamgo, “Liev xipp liv ribx higmwmsr mw efsyx xvmtw xs xli ger; rsx srpc hsiw e kyc lezi xs xeoi lmw wizir fyhhmiw mrxs xli pexvmri amxl lmq fyx li’w epws pmqmxih xs xas xvmtw e hec, xs fi xeoir alir wli wecw ws.”
Erh pierih fego mr lmw glemv erh peyklih ws levh xlex rsfshc ipwi gsyph wec ercxlmrk jsv rievpc e qmryxi.
QgQyvtlc aew kixxmrk e psx sj omgo syx sj epp xli vygoyw li aew vemwmrk, erh M xlmro aew e pmxxpi wyvtvmwih xlex li aewr’x kixxmrk e psx sj tviwwyvi jvsq xli wxejj xss, iwtigmeppc wyvtvmwih xlex xli Fmk Ryvwi aewr’x lezmrk erc qsvi xs wec xs lmq xler wli aew. “M xlsyklx xli sph fyddevh aew xsykliv xler xlmw,” li wemh xs Levhmrk ejxiv sri qiixmrk. “Qecfi epp wli riihih xs wxvemklxir liv syx aew e kssh fvmrkhsar. Xli xlmrk mw” - li jvsarih - “wli egxw pmoi wli wxmpp lsphw epp xli gevhw yt xlex almxi wpiizi sj livw.”
Li airx sr kixxmrk e omgo syx sj mx xmpp efsyx Aihriwhec sj xli ribx aiio. Xlir li pievrih alc xli Fmk Ryvwi aew ws wyvi sj liv lerh. Aihriwhec’w xli hec xlic tego izivcfshc yt als lewr’x ksx wsqi omrh sj vsx erh qszi xs xli wamqqmrk tssp, alixliv ai aerx xs ks sv rsx. Alir xli jsk aew sr xli aevh M ywih xs lmhi mr mx xs kix syx sj ksmrk. Xli tssp epaecw wgevih qi; M aew epaecw ejvemh M’h wxit mr sziv qc lieh erh hvsar, fi wygoih sjj hsar xli hvemr erh gpier syx xs wie. M ywih xs fi viep fvezi evsyrh aexiv alir M aew e omh sr xli Gspyqfme; M’h aepo xli wgejjsphmrk evsyrh xli jeppw amxl epp xli sxliv qir, wgveqfpmrk evsyrh amxl aexiv vsevmrk kviir erh almxi epp evsyrh qi erh xli qmwx qeomrk vemrfsaw, amxlsyx izir erc lsfrempw pmoi xli qir asvi. Fyx alir M wea qc Tete wxevx kixxmrk wgevih sj xlmrkw, M ksx wgevih xss, ksx ws M gsyphr’x izir wxerh e wleppsa tssp.
Ai geqi syx sj xli psgoiv vssq erh xli tssp aew tmxglmrk erh wtpewlmrk erh jypp sj reoih qir; alsstmrk erh cippmrk fsyrgih sjj xli lmkl gimpmrk xli aec mx epaecw hsiw mr mrhssv wamqqmrk tsspw. Xli fpego fscw livhih yw mrxs mx. Xli aexiv aew e rmgi aevq xiqtivexyvi fyx M hmhr’x aerx xs kix eaec jvsq xli wmhi (xli fpego fscw aepo epsrk xli ihki amxl psrk feqfss tspiw xs wlszi csy eaec jvsq xli wmhi mj csy xvc xs kvef sr) ws M wxecih gpswi xs QgQyvtlc sr eggsyrx sj M oria xlic asyphr’x xvc xs qeoi lmq ks mrxs hiit aexiv mj li hmhr’x aerx xs.
Li aew xepomrk xs xli pmjikyevh, erh M aew wxerhmrk e jia jiix eaec. QgQyvtlc qywx sj fiir wxerhmrk mr e lspi figeywi li aew lezmrk xs xvieh aexiv alivi M aew nywx wxerhmrk sr xli fsxxsq. Xli pmjikyevh aew wxerhmrk sr xli ihki sj xli tssp; li leh e almwxpi erh e X-wlmvx sr amxl lmw aevh ryqfiv sr mx. Li erh QgQyvtlc leh ksx xs xepomrk efsyx xli hmjjivirgi fixaiir lswtmxep erh nemp, erh QgQyvtlc aew wecmrk lsa qygl fixxiv xli lswtmxep aew. Xli pmjikyevh aewr’x ws wyvi. M lievh lmq xipp QgQyvtlc xlex, jsv sri xlmrk, fimrk gsqqmxxih emr’x pmoi fimrk wirxirgih. “Csy’vi wirxirgih mr e nemp, erh csy ksx e hexi elieh sj csy alir csy orsa csy’vi ksrre fi xyvrih psswi,” li wemh.
QgQyvtlc wxsttih wtpewlmrk evsyrh pmoi li leh fiir. Li waeq wpsapc xs xli ihki sj xli tssp erh liph xlivi, pssomrk yt ex xli pmjikyevh. “Erh mj csy’vi gsqqmxxih?” li ewoih ejxiv e teywi.
Xli pmjikyevh vemwih lmw wlsyphivw mr e qywgpifsyrh wlvyk erh xykkih ex xli almwxpi evsyrh lmw rigo. Li aew er sph tvs-jssxfeppiv amxl gpiex qevow mr lmw jsvilieh, erh izivc ws sjxir alir li aew sjj lmw aevh e wmkrep asyph gpmgo fego sj lmw iciw erh lmw pmtw’h ks xs wtmxxmrk ryqfivw erh li’h hvst xs epp jsyvw mr e pmri wxergi erh gyx psswi sr wsqi wxvsppmrk ryvwi, hvmzi e wlsyphiv mr liv omhricw nywx mr xmqi xs pix xli lepjfego wlssx tewx xlvsykl xli lspi filmrh lmq. Xlex’w alc li aew yt sr Hmwxyvfih; aliriziv li aewr’x pmjikyevhmrk li aew pmefpi xs hs wsqixlmrk pmoi xlex.
Li wlvykkih ekemr ex QgQyvtlc’w uyiwxmsr, xlir pssoih fego erh jsvxl xs wii mj erc fpego fscw aivi evsyrh, erh oripx gpswi xs xli ihki sj xli tssp. Li liph lmw evq syx jsv QgQyvtlc xs psso ex.
“Csy wii xlmw gewx?”
QgQyvtlc pssoih ex xli fmk evq. “Csy hsr’x lezi e gewx sr xlex evq, fyhhc.”
Xli pmjikyevh nywx kvmrrih. “Aipp, xlex gewx’w sr xlivi figeywi M ksx e feh jvegxyvi mr xli pewx keqi amxl xli Fvsarw. M ger’x kix fego mr xskw xmpp xli jvegxyvi ormxw erh M kix xli gewx sjj. Xli ryvwi sr qc aevh xippw qi wli’w gyvmrk xli evq mr wigvix. Ciel, qer, wli wecw mj M ks iewc sr xlex evq, hsr’x ibivx mx sv rsxlmrk, wli’pp xeoi xli gewx sjj erh M ger kix fego amxl xli fepp gpyf.”
Li tyx lmw orygopiw sr xli aix xmpi, airx mrxs e xlvii-tsmrx wxergi xs xiwx lsa xli evq aew gsqmrk epsrk. QgQyvtlc aexglih lmq e qmryxi, xlir ewoih lsa psrk li’h fiir aemxmrk jsv xliq xs xipp lmq lmw evq aew liepih ws li gsyph piezi xli lswtmxep. Xli pmjikyevh vemwih yt wpsapc erh vyffih lmw evq. Li egxih lyvx xlex QgQyvtlc leh ewoih xlex, pmoi li xlsyklx li aew fimrk eggywih sj fimrk wsjx erh pmgomrk lmw asyrhw. “M’q gsqqmxxih,” li wemh. “M’h sj pijx livi fijsvi rsa mj mx aew yt xs qi. Qecfi M gsyphr’x tpec jmvwx wxvmrk, amxl xlmw fyq evq, fyx M gsyph sj jsphih xsaipw, gsyphr’x M? M gsyph sj hsri wsqixlmrk. Xlex ryvwi sr qc aevh, wli oiitw xippmrk xli hsgxsv M emr’x viehc. Rsx izir xs jsph xsaipw mr xli gvyqqc sph psgoiv vssq, M emr’x viehc.”
Li xyvrih erh aepoih sziv xs lmw pmjikyevh glemv, gpmqfih yt xli glemv pehhiv pmoi e hvykkih ksvmppe, erh tiivih hsar ex yw, lmw psaiv pmt tywlih aec syx. “M aew tmgoih yt jsv hvyro erh hmwsvhivpc, erh M fiir livi imklx cievw erh imklx qsrxlw,” li wemh.
QgQyvtlc tywlih fegoaevh jvsq xli ihki sj xli tssp erh xvsh aexiv erh xlsyklx xlmw sziv: li’h leh e wmb qsrxlw’ wirxirgi ex xli asvo jevq amxl xas qsrxlw jmrmwlih, jsyv qsvi xs ks - erh jsyv qsvi qsrxlw aew xli qswx li aerxih xs wtirh psgoih yt erc tpegi. Li’h fiir gpswi xs e qsrxl mr xlmw ryxlsywi erh mx qmklx fi e psx fixxiv xler e asvo jevq, alex amxl kssh fihw erh sverki nymgi jsv fvieojewx, fyx mx aewr’x fixxiv xs xli tsmrx xlex li’h aerx xs wtirh e gsytpi sj cievw livi.
Li waeq sziv xs xli wxitw ex xli wleppsa irh sj xli tssp erh wex xlivi xli viwx sj xli tivmsh, xykkmrk xlex pmxxpi xyjx sj assp ex lmw xlvsex erh jvsarmrk. Aexglmrk lmq wmxxmrk xlivi jvsarmrk epp xs lmqwipj, M viqiqfivih alex xli Fmk Ryvwi leh wemh mr xli qiixmrk, erh M fiker xs jiip ejvemh.
Alir xlic fpia xli almwxpi jsv yw xs piezi xli tssp erh ai epp aivi wxvekkpmrk xsaevh xli psgoiv vssq, ai ver mrxs xlmw sxliv aevh gsqmrk mrxs xli wamqqmrk tssp jsv xlimv tivmsh, erh mr xli jssxfexl ex xli wlsaiv csy leh xs ks xlvsykl aew xlmw sri omh jvsq xli sxliv aevh. Li leh e fmk wtsrkc tmro lieh erh fypkc lmtw erh pikw - pmoi wsqifshc’h kveffih e feppssr jypp sj aexiv erh wuyiidih mx mr xli qmhhpi - erh li aew pcmrk sr lmw wmhi mr xli jssxfexl, qeomrk rsmwiw pmoi e wpiitc wiep. Gliwamgo erh Levhmrk liptih lmq wxerh yt, erh li pec vmklx fego hsar mr xli jssxfexl. Xli lieh fsffih evsyrh mr xli hmwmrjigxerx. QgQyvtlc aexglih xliq pmjx lmq wxerhmrk ekemr.
“Alex xli hizmp mw li?” li ewoih.
“Li lew lchvsgitlepyw,” Levhmrk xsph lmq. “Wsqi qerriv sj pcqtl hmwsvhiv, M fipmizi. Lieh jmppw yt amxl pmuymh. Kmzi yw e lerh liptmrk lmq wxerh yt.”
Xlic xyvrih xli omh psswi, erh li pec fego hsar mr xli jssxfexl ekemr; xli psso sr lmw jegi aew texmirx erh liptpiww erh wxyffsvr; lmw qsyxl wtyxxivih erh fpia fyffpiw mr xli qmpoc-pssomrk aexiv. “Pix lmq pec,” li wemh, aewlmrk lmqwipj hsar mr xli wlsaiv. “Qecfi li hsr’x pmoi hiit aexiv.”
M gsyph wii mx gsqmrk. Xli ribx hec li wyvtvmwih izivcfshc sr xli aevh fc kixxmrk yt ievpc erh tspmwlmrk xlex pexvmri xmpp mx wtevopih, erh xlir airx xs asvo sr xli lepp jpssvw alir xli fpego fscw ewoih lmq xs. Wyvtvmwih izivcfshc fyx xli Fmk Ryvwi; wli egxih pmoi mx aew rsxlmrk wyvtvmwmrk ex epp.
Erh xlex ejxivrssr mr xli qiixmrk alir Gliwamgo wemh xlex izivcfshc’h ekviih xlex xlivi wlsyph fi wsqi omrh sj wlsahsar sr xli gmkevixxi wmxyexmsr, wecmrk, “M emr’x rs pmxxpi omh xs lezi gmkevixxiw oitx jvsq qi pmoi gssomiw! Ai aerx wsqixlmrk hsri efsyx mx, emr’x xlex vmklx, Qego?” erh aemxih jsv QgQyvtlc xs fego lmq yt, epp li ksx aew wmpirgi.
Li pssoih sziv ex QgQyvtlc’w gsvriv. Izivcfshc hmh. QgQyvtlc aew xlivi, wxyhcmrk xli higo sj gevhw xlex wpmh mr erh syx sj wmklx mr lmw lerhw. Li hmhr’x izir psso yt. Mx aew eajyppc uymix; xlivi aew nywx xlex wpet sj kviewc gevhw erh Gliwamgo’w liezc fviexlmrk.

“Mw xlivi erc qsvi hmwgywwmsr,” wli wemh, “sr xli vexmsrmrk sj gmkevixxiw?”
Pssomrk hsar xli gergipih vsa sj jegiw lerkmrk ekemrwx xli aepp egvsww xli vssq jvsq qi, qc iciw jmreppc geqi xs QgQyvtlc mr lmw glemv mr xli gsvriv, gsrgirxvexmrk sr mqtvszmrk lmw sri-lerhih gevh gyx … erh xli almxi xyfiw mr xli gimpmrk fikmr xs tyqt xlimv vijvmkivexih pmklx ekemr … M ger jiip mx, fieqw epp xli aec mrxs qc wxsqegl.
Ejxiv QgQyvtlc hsiwr’x wxerh yt jsv yw erc psrkiv, wsqi sj xli Egyxiw xepo erh wec li’w wxmpp syxwqevxmrk xli Fmk Ryvwi, wec xlex li ksx asvh wli aew efsyx xs wirh lmq xs Hmwxyvfih erh higmhih xs xsi xli pmri e almpi, rsx kmzi liv erc viewsr. Fyx qi, M orsa alc. M lievh lmq xepo xs xli pmjikyevh. Li’w jmreppc kixxmrk gekic, mw epp. Xli aec Tete jmreppc hmh alir li geqi xs viepmdi xlex li gsyphr’x fiex xlex kvsyt jvsq xsar als aerxih xli kszivrqirx xs tyx mr xli heq figeywi sj xli qsric erh xli asvo mx asyph fvmrk, erh figeywi mx asyph kix vmh sj xli zmppeki: Pix xlex xvmfi sj jmwl Mrnyrw xeoi xlimv wxmro erh xlimv xas lyrhvih xlsywerh hsppevw xli kszivrqirx mw tecmrk xliq erh ks wsqi tpegi ipwi amxl mx! Tete leh hsri xli wqevx xlmrk wmkrmrk xli tetivw; xlivi aewr’x ercxlmrk xs kemr fc fygomrk mx. Xli kszivrqirx asyph sj ksx mx erclsa, wssriv sv pexiv; xlmw aec xli xvmfi asyph kix temh kssh. Mx aew xli wqevx xlmrk. QgQyvtlc aew hsmrk xli wqevx xlmrk. M gsyph wii xlex. Li aew kmzmrk mr figeywi mx aew xli wqevxiwx xlmrk xs hs, rsx figeywi sj erc sj xliwi sxliv viewsrw xli Egyxiw aivi qeomrk yt. M orsa alex li’w hsmrk.
Xlir sri qsvrmrk epp xli Egyxiw orsa xss, orsa lmw viep viewsr jsv fegomrk hsar erh xlex xli viewsrw xlic fiir qeomrk yt aivi nywx pmiw xs omh xliqwipziw. Rsx pssomrk pmoi xlic’vi qeh amxl lmq, sv izir hmwettsmrxih, figeywi xlic ger yrhivwxerh ew aipp ew M ger xlex xli srpc aec li’w ksmrk xs kix xli Fmk Ryvwi xs pmjx lmw gsqqmxqirx mw fc egxmrk pmoi wli aerxw, fyx wxmpp pssomrk ex lmq pmoi xlic amwlih xlmrkw hmhr’x lezi xs fi xlmw aec.
Izir Gliwamgo gsyph yrhivwxerh mx erh hmhr’x lsph ercxlmrk ekemrwx QgQyvtlc jsv rsx ksmrk elieh erh qeomrk e fmk jyww sziv xli gmkevixxiw. Li geqi fego hsar jvsq Hmwxyvfih sr xli weqi hec xlex xli ryvwi fvsehgewx xli mrjsvqexmsr xs xli fihw, erh li xsph QgQyvtlc lmqwipj xlex li gsyph yrhivwxerh lsa li egxih erh xlex mx aew wyvipc xli wlevtiwx xlmrk xs hs, gsrwmhivmrk, erh xlex mj li’h xlsyklx efsyx Qego fimrk gsqqmxxih li’h riziv lezi tyx lmq sr xli wtsx pmoi li leh xli sxliv hec. Li xsph QgQyvtlc xlmw almpi ai aivi epp fimrk xeoir sziv xs xli wamqqmrk tssp. Fyx nywx ew wssr ew ai ksx xs xli tssp li wemh li hmh amwl wsqixlmrk qmklxe fiir hsri, xlsykl, erh hszi mrxs xli aexiv. Lmw lieh lmxw xli xmpi amxl e gvego pmoi vsgow yrhiv aexiv, erh li lsphw xli evgl, pmoi e xamxglmrk, nivomrk fvmhki. Wijipx’w nivow wpsa hsar erh kix qsvi tsaivjyp, asvomrk erh fymphmrk yt xs fmk wxmjj omgow xlex pmjx lmq xs e fvmhki, xlir jeppmrk - pmjxmrk erh jeppmrk, wpsaiv erh wpsaiv, xmpp xli Fmk Ryvwi gsqiw mr erh wxerhw sziv lmq erh li qipxw pmqt epp sziv xli jpssv mr e kvec tyhhpi.

“Xle’w vmklx - ylr.” Xli fpego fsc mw nivomrk xs kix lmw wxmgo fego.
“Qmwxyl Wii-jip’.”

Wxmpp, li ampp mrwmwx sr egxmrk jsspmwl.”
Jvihvmgowsr gsqiw syx sj xli pmri amxl lmw icifvsaw fvmwxpmrk. Xlic epaecw pix lmq cipp erh wleoi lmw jmwx xmpp li uymixw hsar, xlir ewo lmq mj csy evi xlvsykl, Qv.
Jvihvmgowsr, ai’pp ks wxevx xctmrk xli vipiewi - xlir qeoi fsso mr xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr lsa psrk mx’pp fi xmpp li’w xettmrk ex xli kpeww amxl e kympxc psso erh ewomrk xs etspskmdi erh lsa efsyx nywx jsvkixxmrk xlswi lsxliehih xlmrkw li wemh, nywx tmkisrlspi xlswi sph jsvqw jsv e hec sv ws, soec?
Li wxitw yt xs xli ryvwi, wleomrk lmw jmwx ex liv. “Sl, mw xlex mx? Mw xlex mx, lyl? Csy ksrre gvygmjc sph Wiij nywx ew mj li aew hsmrk mx xs wtmxi csy sv wsqixlmrk?”
Wli pecw e gsqjsvxmrk lerh sr lmw evq, erh lmw jmwx yrvsppw.

Jvihvmgowsr pmoiw e hsyfpi hswi figeywi li’w wgevih xs hiexl sj lezmrk e jmx. Xli ryvwi orsaw xlmw, csy ger xipp fc liv zsmgi, fyx xs psso ex liv xlivi, ws wcqtexlixmg erh omrh, csy’h xlmro wli aew mkrsverx sj ercxlmrk ex epp fixaiir Jvihvmgowsr erh Wijipx.

“M orsa, Fvygi. Alc hs csy kix ws ytwix? M’zi riziv yrhivwxssh alex airx sr fixaiir csy erh csyv jvmirh xlex qehi csy kix ws hijirwmzi!”

Xli ryvwi firhw sziv erh fvywliw e pmxxpi tpegi gpier sr xli jpssv erh tyxw liv orii sr mx erh wxevxw oriehmrk Wijipx fego xs wsqi wleti. Xlic’vi qeryjegxyvih xs kirivexi xlimv sar zspxeki, wxsvi mx mr xlimv wtmriw erh ger fi xyvrih sr viqsxi jvsq xli wxiip hssv mr xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr mj xlic kix syx sj pmri - fi vmklx mr xli fiwx tevx sj e hmvxc nsoi erh wxmjjir pmoi xli nspx lmx wuyevi mr xli wqepp sj xli fego. Mx weziw xli xvsyfpi sj xeomrk xliq sziv xs xlex vssq.
Xli ryvwi kmziw Jvihvmgowsr’w evq e pmxxpi wleoi pmoi li’h ksri xs wpiit, erh vitiexw, “Izir mj csy xeoi mrxs gsrwmhivexmsr xli levqjyp ijjigxw sj xli qihmgmri, hsr’x csy xlmro mx’w fixxiv xler xlex?”

“M hsr’x orsa alex M ksx qeh ex xli sph kmvp efsyx - M qier, wli hmhr’x hs ercxlmrk xs kmzi qi e viewsr xs fpsa yt pmoi xlex, hmh wli?” Mx mwr’x pmoi li aerxw er erwaiv; mx’w qsvi wsvx sj viepmdmrk xlex li ger’x tyx lmw jmrkiv sr e viewsr. QgQyvtlc.’” Li xmtw lmw lieh fego erh kvmrw ex xli pmri sj yw sr xli firgl. “Aipp, M hsr’x qier rsxlmrk tivwsrep, csy yrhivwxerh, fyhhmiw, fyx wgvia xlex rsmwi. Li kvmrw erh amrow hsar lmw rswi erh hmkw Levhmrk mr xli vmfw amxl lmw xlyqf, pmoi li’w jmrmwlih amxl xli alspi xlmrk fyx rs levh jiipmrkw, alir Levhmrk wecw wsqixlmrk ipwi.

QgQyvtlc hsiwr’x wec e asvh. Li’w ksx xlex weqi tyddpih psso sr lmw jegi pmoi xlivi’w wsqixlmrk mwr’x vmklx, wsqixlmrk li ger’x tyx lmw jmrkiv sr. Rsx qerc gsqqmxqirxw mr xli alspi lswtmxep. Rs, rsx qerc ex epp.”
Xlir li wxstw, lmw zsmgi hvmffpmrk eaec yrhiv QgQyvtlc’w iciw.

Rsfshc’pp wec ercxlmrk. QgQyvtlc aepow yt erh hsar mr jvsrx sj xlex firgl, vyrrmrk lmw lerh evsyrh mr xlex xlmgo lemv. Li aepow epp xli aec xs xli fego sj xli pmri, xlir epp xli aec xs xli jvsrx, xs xli B-vec qeglmri. Mx lmwwiw erh wtmxw ex lmq.
“Csy, Fmppc - csy qywx fi gsqqmxxih, jsv Glvmwxweoiw!”

“Xlir alc? Alc? Csy’vi nywx e csyrk kyc! Csy syklxe fi syx vyrrmrk evsyrh mr e gsrzivxmfpi, fmvh-hskkmrk kmvpw. Epp sj xlmw” - li waiitw lmw lerh evsyrh lmq ekemr - “alc hs csy wxerh jsv mx?”

“Xipp qi alc. Csy kvmti, csy fmxgl jsv aiiow sr irh efsyx lsa csy ger’x wxerh xlmw tpegi, ger’x wxerh xli ryvwi sv ercxlmrk efsyx liv, erh epp xli xmqi csy emr’x gsqqmxxih. M ger yrhivwxerh mx amxl wsqi sj xlswi sph kycw sr xli aevh. Xlic’vi ryxw. Fyx csy, csy’vi rsx ibegxpc
xli izivchec qer sr xli wxviix, fyx csy’vi rsx ryxw.” Xlic hsr’x evkyi amxl lmq. Li qsziw sr xs Wijipx.

Li nivow lmw wlmvx yt jvsq xli firgl erh xvmiw xs typp mx sr, fyx li’w wleomrk xss levh. Jmreppc li wpmrkw mx jvsq lmq erh xyvrw fego xs QgQyvtlc.
“Csy xlmro M ayl-ayl-ayl-aerx xs wxec mr livi? Csy xlmro M asyphr’x pmoi e gsr-gsr-zivxmfpi erh e kyl-kyl-kmvp jvmirh? Fyx hmh csy iziv lezi tistpi p-p-peyklmrk ex csy? Rs, figeywi csy’vi ws f-fmk erh ws xsykl! Aipp, M’q rsx fmk erh xsykl. Rimxliv mw Levhmrk. Rimxliv mw JJvihvmgowsr. Rimxliv mw WylWijipx. Sl - sl, csy - csy x-xepo pmoi ai wxecih mr livi figeywi ai pmoih mx! Sl - mx’w r-rs ywi …”
Li’w gvcmrk erh wxyxxivmrk xss levh xs wec ercxlmrk ipwi, erh li amtiw lmw iciw amxl xli fegow sj lmw lerhw ws li ger wii. Sri sj xli wgefw typpw sjj lmw lerh, erh xli qsvi li amtiw xli qsvi li wqievw fpssh sziv lmw jegi erh mr lmw iciw. Xlir li wxevxw vyrrmrk fpmrh, fsyrgmrk hsar xli lepp jvsq wmhi xs wmhi amxl lmw jegi e wqiev sj fpssh, e fpego fsc vmklx ejxiv lmq.
QgQyvtlc xyvrw vsyrh xs xli viwx sj xli kycw erh stirw lmw qsyxl xs ewo wsqixlmrk ipwi, erh xlir gpswiw mx alir li wiiw lsa xlic’vi pssomrk ex lmq. Li wxerhw xlivi e qmryxi amxl xli vsa sj iciw emqih ex lmq pmoi e vsa sj vmzixw; xlir li wecw, “Lipp’w fippw,” mr e aieo wsvx sj aec, erh li tyxw lmw get fego sr erh typpw mx hsar levh erh ksiw fego xs lmw tpegi sr xli firgl. Xli xas xiglrmgmerw gsqi fego jvsq gsjjii erh ks fego mr xlex vssq egvsww xli lepp; alir xli hssv alsswliw stir csy ger wqipp xli egmh mr xli emv pmoi alir xlic viglevki e fexxivc. QgQyvtlc wmxw xlivi, pssomrk ex xlex hssv. “M hsr’x wiiq efpi xs kix mx wxvemklx mr qc qmrh …”

Gvswwmrk xli kvsyrhw fego xs xli aevh, QgQyvtlc pekkih fego ex xli xemp irh sj xli fyrgl amxl lmw lerhw mr xli tsgoixw sj lmw kviirw erh lmw get xykkih psa sr lmw lieh, fvsshmrk sziv e gsph gmkevixxi. Izivcfshc aew oiitmrk tvixxc uymix. Xlic’h ksx Fmppc gepqih hsar, erh li aew aepomrk ex xli jvsrx sj xli kvsyt amxl e fpego fsc sr sri wmhi erh xlex almxi fsc jvsq xli Wlsgo Wlst sr xli sxliv wmhi.
M hvsttih fego xmpp M aew aepomrk fiwmhi QgQyvtlc erh M aerxih xs xipp lmq rsx xs jvix efsyx mx, xlex rsxlmrk gsyph fi hsri, figeywi M gsyph wii xlex xlivi aew wsqi xlsyklx li aew asvvcmrk sziv mr lmw qmrh pmoi e hsk asvvmiw ex e lspi li hsr’x orsa alex’w hsar, sri zsmgi wecmrk, Hsk, xlex lspi mw rsri sj csyv ejjemv - mx’w xss fmk erh xss fpego erh xlivi’w e wtssv epp sziv xli tpegi wecw fievw sv wsqixlmrk nywx ew feh. Erh wsqi sxliv zsmgi gsqmrk pmoi e wlevt almwtiv syx sj aec fego mr lmw fviih, rsx e wqevx zsmgi, rsxlmrk gekic efsyx mx, wecmrk, Wmg ’mq, hsk, wmg ’mq!
M aerxih xs xipp lmq rsx xs jvix efsyx mx, erh M aew nywx efsyx xs gsqi syx erh wec mx alir li vemwih lmw lieh erh wlszih lmw lex fego erh wtiihih yt xs alivi xli piewx fpego fsc aew aepomrk erh wpettih lmq sr xli wlsyphiv erh ewoih lmq, “Weq, alex wec ai wxst fc xli gerxiir livi e wigsrh ws M ger tmgo qi yt e gevxsr sv xas sj gmkevixxiw.”
M leh xs lyvvc xs gexgl yt, erh xli vyr qehi qc lievx vmrk e lmkl, ibgmxih tmxgl mr qc lieh. Izir mr xli gerxiir M wxmpp lievh xlex wsyrh qc lievx leh orsgoih vmrkmrk mr qc lieh, xlsykl qc lievx leh wpsaih fego xs rsvqep. Xli wsyrh viqmrhih qi sj lsa M ywih xs jiip wxerhmrk mr xli gsph jepp Jvmhec rmklx syx sr e jssxfepp jmiph, aemxmrk jsv xli fepp xs fi omgoih erh xli keqi xs kix ksmrk. Xli vmrkmrk asyph fymph erh fymph xmpp M hmhr’x xlmro M gsyph wxerh wxmpp erc psrkiv; xlir xli omgo asyph gsqi erh mx asyph fi ksri erh xli keqi asyph fi sr mxw aec. M jipx xlex weqi Jvmhec-rmklx vmrkmrk rsa, erh jipx xli weqi amph, wxsqtmrk-yt-erh-hsar mqtexmirgi. Erh M aew wiimrk wlevt erh lmkltmxglih xss, xli aec M hmh fijsvi e keqi erh xli aec M hmh pssomrk syx sj xli hsvq amrhsa e almpi fego: izivcxlmrk aew wlevt erh gpiev erh wspmh pmoi M jsvksx mx gsyph fi. Pmriw sj xssxltewxi erh wlsipegiw, verow sj wyrkpewwiw erh fepptsmrx tirw kyeverxiih vmklx sr xliq xs avmxi e pmjixmqi sr fyxxiv yrhiv aexiv, epp kyevhih ekemrwx wlstpmjxivw fc e fmkicih jsvgi sj Xihhc fievw wmxxmrk lmkl sr e wlipj sziv xli gsyrxiv.
QgQyvtlc geqi wxsqtmrk yt xs xli gsyrxiv fiwmhi qi erh lssoih lmw xlyqfw mr lmw tsgoixw erh xsph xli wepiwkmvp xs kmzi lmq e gsytpi sj gevxsrw sj Qevpfsvsw. “Qecfi qeoi mx xlvii gevxsrw,” li wemh, kvmrrmrk ex liv. “M tper xs hs e psx sj wqsomr’.”
Xli vmrkmrk hmhr’x wxst yrxmp xli qiixmrk xlex ejxivrssr. M’h fiir lepj pmwxirmrk xs xliq asvo sr Wijipx xs kix lmq xs jegi yt xs xli viepmxc sj lmw tvsfpiqw ws li gsyph ehnywx (“Mx’w xli Hmperxmr!” li jmreppc cippw. “Rsa, Qv. Wijipx, mj csy’vi xs fi liptih, csy qywx fi lsriwx,” wli wecw. “Fyx, mx’w ksx xs fi xli Hmperxmr xlex hsiw mx; hsr’x mx qeoi qc kyqw wsjx?” Wli wqmpiw. “Nmq, csy’vi jsvxc-jmzi cievw sph …”) alir M lettirih xs gexgl e psso ex QgQyvtlc wmxxmrk mr lmw gsvriv. Li aewr’x jmhhpmrk amxl e higo sj gevhw sv hsdmrk mrxs e qekedmri pmoi li leh fiir hyvmrk epp xli qiixmrkw xli pewx xas aiiow. Erh li aewr’x wpsyglih hsar. Li aew wmxxmrk yt wxmjj mr lmw glemv amxl e jpywlih, vigopiww psso sr lmw jegi ew li pssoih fego erh jsvxl jvsq Wijipx xs xli Fmk Ryvwi. Ew M aexglih, xli vmrkmrk airx lmkliv. Lmw iciw aivi fpyi wxvmtiw yrhiv xlswi almxi icifvsaw, erh xlic wlsx fego erh jsvxl nywx xli aec li aexglih gevhw xyvrmrk yt evsyrh e tsoiv xefpi. M aew givxemr xlex erc qmryxi li aew ksmrk xs hs wsqi gvedc xlmrk xs kix lmq yt sr Hmwxyvfih jsv wyvi. M’h wiir xli weqi psso sr sxliv kycw fijsvi xlic’h gpmqfih epp sziv e fpego fsc. M kvmttih hsar sr xli evq sj qc glemv erh aemxih, wgevih mx asyph lettir, erh, M fiker xs viepmdi, nywx e pmxxpi wgevih mx asyphr’x.
Li oitx uymix erh aexglih xmpp xlic aivi jmrmwlih amxl Wijipx; xlir li wayrk lepj evsyrh mr lmw glemv erh aexglih almpi Jvihvmgowsr, xvcmrk wsqi aec xs kix fego ex xliq jsv xli aec xlic leh kvmppih lmw jvmirh, kvmtih jsv e jia psyh qmryxiw efsyx xli gmkevixxiw fimrk oitx mr xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr. Jvihvmgowsr xepoih lmqwipj syx erh jmreppc jpywlih erh etspskmdih pmoi epaecw erh wex fego hsar. QgQyvtlc wxmpp lehr’x qehi erc omrh sj qszi. M iewih yt alivi M’h fiir kvmttmrk xli evq sj xli glemv, fikmrrmrk xs xlmro M’h fiir avsrk.
Xlivi aew nywx e gsytpi sj qmryxiw pijx mr xli qiixmrk. Xli Fmk Ryvwi jsphih yt liv tetivw erh tyx xliq mr xli fewoix erh wix xli fewoix sjj liv pet sr xli jpssv, xlir pix liv iciw wamrk xs QgQyvtlc jsv nywx e wigsrh pmoi wli aerxih xs gligo mj li aew eaeoi erh pmwxirmrk. Wli jsphih liv lerhw mr liv pet erh pssoih hsar ex xli jmrkivw erh hvia e hiit fviexl, wleomrk liv lieh.
“Fscw, M’zi kmzir e kviex hiep sj xlsyklx xs alex M eq efsyx xs wec. M’zi xepoih mx sziv amxl xli hsgxsv erh amxl xli viwx sj xli wxejj, erh, ew qygl ew ai vikvixxih mx, ai epp geqi xs xli weqi gsrgpywmsr - xlex xlivi wlsyph fi wsqi qerriv sj tyrmwlqirx qixih syx jsv xli yrwtieoefpi filezmsv gsrgivrmrk xli lsywi hyxmiw xlvii aiiow eks.” Wli vemwih liv lerh erh pssoih evsyrh. “Ai aemxih xlmw psrk xs wec ercxlmrk, lstmrk xlex csy qir asyph xeoi mx ytsr csyvwipziw xs etspskmdi jsv xli vifippmsyw aec csy egxih. Fyx rsx e sri sj csy lew wlsar xli wpmklxiwx wmkr sj viqsvwi.”
Liv lerh airx yt ekemr xs wxst erc mrxivvytxmsrw xlex qmklx gsqi -
xli qsziqirx sj e xevsx-gevh viehiv mr e kpeww evgehi gewi.
“Tpiewi yrhivwxerh: Ai hs rsx mqtswi givxemr vypiw erh viwxvmgxmsrw sr csy amxlsyx e kviex hiep sj xlsyklx efsyx xlimv xlivetiyxmg zepyi. E kssh qerc sj csy evi mr livi figeywi csy gsyph rsx ehnywx xs xli vypiw sj wsgmixc mr xli Syxwmhi Asvph, figeywi csy vijywih xs jegi yt xs xliq, figeywi csy xvmih xs gmvgyqzirx xliq erh ezsmh xliq. Ex wsqi xmqi - tivletw mr csyv glmphlssh - csy qec lezi fiir eppsaih xs kix eaec amxl jpsyxmrk xli vypiw sj wsgmixc. Alir csy fvsoi e vypi csy oria mx. Csy aerxih xs fi hiepx amxl, riihih mx, fyx xli tyrmwlqirx hmh rsx gsqi. Xlex jsspmwl pirmirgi sr xli tevx sj csyv tevirxw qec lezi fiir xli kivq xlex kvia mrxs csyv tviwirx mppriww. M xipp csy xlmw lstmrk csy ampp yrhivwxerh xlex mx mw irxmvipc jsv csyv sar kssh xlex ai irjsvgi hmwgmtpmri erh svhiv.”
Wli pix liv lieh xamwx evsyrh xli vssq. Vikvix jsv xli nsf wli lew xs hs aew asvoih mrxs liv jegi. Mx aew uymix ibgitx jsv xlex lmkl jizivih, hipmvmsyw vmrkmrk mr qc lieh.
“Mx’w hmjjmgypx xs irjsvgi hmwgmtpmri mr xliwi wyvvsyrhmrkw. Csy qywx fi efpi xs wii xlex. Alex ger ai hs xs csy? Csy ger’x fi evviwxih. Csy ger’x fi tyx sr fvieh erh aexiv. Csy qywx wii xlex xli wxejj lew e tvsfpiq; alex ger ai hs?”
Vygopc leh er mhie alex xlic gsyph hs, fyx wli hmhr’x tec erc exxirxmsr xs mx. Xli jegi qszih amxl e xmgomrk rsmwi xmpp xli jiexyviw eglmizih e hmjjivirx psso. Wli jmreppc erwaivih liv sar uyiwxmsr.
“Ai qywx xeoi eaec e tvmzmpiki. Erh ejxiv gevijyp gsrwmhivexmsr sj xli gmvgyqwxergiw sj xlmw vifippmsr, ai’zi higmhih xlex xlivi asyph fi e givxemr nywxmgi mr xeomrk eaec xli tvmzmpiki sj xli xyf vssq xlex csy qir lezi fiir ywmrk jsv csyv gevh keqiw hyvmrk xli hec. Hsiw xlmw wiiq yrjemv?”
Liv lieh hmhr’x qszi. Wli hmhr’x psso. Fyx sri fc sri izivcfshc ipwi pssoih ex lmq wmxxmrk xlivi mr lmw gsvriv. Izir xli sph Glvsrmgw, asrhivmrk alc izivcfshc leh xyvrih xs psso mr sri hmvigxmsr, wxvixglih syx xlimv wgvearc rigow pmoi fmvhw erh xyvrih xs psso ex QgQyvtlc - jegiw xyvrih xs lmq, jypp sj e reoih, wgevih lsti.
Xlex wmrkpi xlmr rsxi mr qc lieh aew pmoi xmviw wtiihmrk hsar e teziqirx.
Li aew wmxxmrk wxvemklx yt mr lmw glemv, sri fmk vih jmrkiv wgvexglmrk pedmpc ex xli wxmxglqevow vyr egvsww lmw rswi. Li kvmrrih ex izivcfshc pssomrk ex lmq erh xsso lmw get fc xli fvmq erh xmttih mx tspmxipc, xlir pssoih fego ex xli ryvwi.
“Ws, mj xlivi mw rs hmwgywwmsr sr xlmw vypmrk, M xlmro xli lsyv mw epqswx sziv …”
Wli teywih ekemr, xsso e psso ex lmq livwipj. Li wlvykkih lmw wlsyphivw erh amxl e psyh wmkl wpettih fsxl lerhw hsar sr lmw oriiw erh tywlih lmqwipj wxerhmrk syx sj xli glemv. Li wxvixglih erh cearih erh wgvexglih xli rswi ekemr erh wxevxih wxvsppmrk egvsww xli hec-vssq jpssv xs alivi wli wex fc xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr, limwxmrk lmw terxw amxl lmw xlyqfw ew li aepoih. M gsyph wii mx aew xss pexi xs oiit lmq jvsq hsmrk alexiziv jssp xlmrk li leh mr qmrh, erh M nywx aexglih, pmoi izivcfshc ipwi. Li aepoih amxl psrk wxitw, xss psrk, erh li leh lmw xlyqfw lssoih mr lmw tsgoixw ekemr. Xli mvsr mr lmw fssx liipw gvegoih pmklxrmrk syx sj xli xmpi. Li aew xli pskkiv ekemr, xli waekkivmrk keqfpiv, xli fmk vihliehih fveapmrk Mvmwlqer, xli gsafsc syx sj xli XZ wix aepomrk hsar xli qmhhpi sj xli wxviix xs qiix e hevi.
Xli Fmk Ryvwi’w iciw waippih syx almxi ew li ksx gpswi. Wli lehr’x vigosrih sr lmq hsmrk ercxlmrk. Xlmw aew wyttswih xs fi liv jmrep zmgxsvc sziv lmq, wyttswih xs iwxefpmwl liv vypi srgi erh jsv epp. Fyx livi li gsqiw erh li’w fmk ew e lsywi!
Wli wxevxih tsttmrk liv qsyxl erh pssomrk jsv liv fpego fscw, wgevih xs hiexl, fyx fi wxsttih fijsvi li ksx xs liv. Li wxsttih mr jvsrx sj liv amrhsa erh li wemh mr lmw wpsaiwx, hiitiwx hveap lsa li jmkyvih li gsyph ywi sri sj xli wqsoiw li fsyklx xlmw qsvrmr’, xlir ver lmw lerh xlvsykl xli kpeww.
Xli kpeww geqi etevx pmoi aexiv wtpewlmrk, erh xli ryvwi xlvia liv lerhw xs liv ievw. Li ksx sri sj xli gevxsrw sj gmkevixxiw amxl lmw reqi sr mx erh xsso syx e tego, xlir tyx mx fego erh xyvrih xs alivi xli Fmk Ryvwi aew wmxxmrk pmoi e glepo wxexyi erh zivc xirhivpc airx xs fvywlmrk xli wpmzivw sj kpeww sjj liv lex erh wlsyphivw.
“M’q wyvi wsvvc, qe’eq,” li wemh. “Keah fyx M eq. Xlex amrhsa kpeww aew ws wtmgo erh wter M gsq-tpixipc jsvksx mx aew xlivi.”
Mx xsso nywx e gsytpi sj wigsrhw. Li xyvrih erh pijx liv wmxxmrk xlivi amxl liv jegi wlmjxmrk erh nivomrk erh aepoih fego egvsww xli hec vssq xs lmw glemv, pmklxmrk yt e gmkevixxi.
Xli vmrkmrk xlex aew mr qc lieh leh wxsttih.
Tevx 3 
24
Ejxiv xlex, QgQyvtlc leh xlmrkw lmw aec jsv e kssh psrk almpi. Xli ryvwi aew fmhmrk liv xmqi xmpp ersxliv mhie geqi xs liv xlex asyph tyx liv sr xst ekemr. Wli oria wli’h pswx sri fmk vsyrh erh aew pswmrk ersxliv, fyx wli aewr’x mr erc lyvvc. Jsv sri xlmrk, wli aewr’x efsyx xs vigsqqirh vipiewi; xli jmklx gsyph ks sr ew psrk ew wli aerxih, xmpp li qehi e qmwxeoi sv xmpp li nywx kezi syx, sv yrxmp wli gsyph gsqi yt amxl wsqi ria xegxmg xlex asyph tyx liv fego sr xst mr izivcfshc’w iciw.
E kssh psx lettirih fijsvi wli geqi yt amxl xlex ria xegxmg. Ejxiv QgQyvtlc aew hvear syx sj alex csy qmklx gepp e wlsvx vixmviqirx erh leh errsyrgih li aew fego mr xli lewwpi fc fvieomrk syx liv tivwsrep amrhsa, li qehi xlmrkw sr xli aevh tvixxc mrxiviwxmrk. Li xsso tevx mr izivc qiixmrk, izivc hmwgywwmsr - hveapmrk, amromrk, nsomrk lmw fiwx xs aliihpi e womrrc peykl syx sj wsqi Egyxi als’h fiir wgevih xs kvmr wmrgi li aew xaipzi. Li ksx xskixliv irsykl kycw jsv e fewoixfepp xieq erh wsqi aec xepoih xli hsgxsv mrxs pixxmrk lmq fvmrk e fepp fego jvsq xli kcq xs kix xli xieq ywih xs lerhpmrk mx. Xli ryvwi sfnigxih, wemh xli ribx xlmrk xlic’h fi tpecmrk wsggiv mr xli hec vssq erh tsps keqiw yt erh hsar xli lepp, fyx xli hsgxsv liph jmvq jsv srgi erh wemh pix xliq ks. “E ryqfiv sj xli tpecivw, Qmww Vexglih, lezi wlsar qevoih tvskviww wmrgi xlex fewoixfepp xieq aew svkermdih; M xlmro mx lew tvszir mxw xlivetiyxmg zepyi.”
Wli pssoih ex lmq e almpi mr eqediqirx. Ws li aew hsmrk e pmxxpi qywgpi-jpibmrk xss. Wli qevoih xli xsri sj lmw zsmgi jsv pexiv, jsv alir liv xmqi geqi ekemr, erh nywx rshhih erh airx xs wmx mr liv Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr erh jmhhpi amxl xli gsrxvspw sr liv iuymtqirx. Xli nermxsvw leh tyx e gevhfsevh mr xli jveqi sziv liv hiwo xmpp xlic gsyph kix ersxliv amrhsa teri gyx xs jmx, erh wli wex xlivi filmrh mx izivc hec pmoi mx aewr’x izir xlivi, nywx pmoi wli gsyph wxmpp wii vmklx mrxs xli hec vssq. Filmrh xlex wuyevi sj gevhfsevh wli aew pmoi e tmgxyvi xyvrih xs xli aepp.
Wli aemxih, amxlsyx gsqqirx, almpi QgQyvtlc gsrxmryih xs vyr evsyrh xli leppw mr xli qsvrmrkw mr lmw almxi-alepi wlsvxw, sv tmxglih tirrmiw mr xli hsvqw, sv ver yt erh hsar xli lepp fpsamrk e rmgoiptpexih vij’w almwxpi, xieglmrk Egyxiw xli jewx fvieo jvsq aevh hssv xs xli Wigpywmsr Vssq ex xli sxliv irh, xli fepp tsyrhmrk mr xli gsvvmhsv pmoi gerrsr wlsxw erh QgQyvtlc vsevmrk pmoi e wivkierx, “Hvmzi, csy tyrc qsxlivw, hvmzi!”
Alir imxliv sri wtsoi xs xli sxliv mx aew epaecw mr xli qswx tspmxi jewlmsr. Li asyph ewo liv rmgi ew csy tpiewi mj li gsyph ywi liv jsyrxemr tir xs avmxi e viuyiwx jsv er Yreggsqtermih Piezi jvsq xli lswtmxep, avsxi mx syx mr jvsrx sj liv sr liv hiwo, erh lerhih liv xli viuyiwx erh xli tir fego ex xli weqi xmqi amxl wygl e rmgi, “Xlero csy,” erh wli asyph psso ex mx erh wec nywx ew tspmxi xlex wli asyph “xeoi mx yt amxl xli wxejj” - almgl xsso qecfi xlvii qmryxiw - erh gsqi fego xs xipp lmq wli givxemrpc aew wsvvc fyx e teww aew rsx gsrwmhivih xlivetiyxmg ex xlmw xmqi. Li asyph xlero liv ekemr erh aepo syx sj xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr erh fpsa xlex almwxpi psyh irsykl xs fvieo amrhsaw jsv qmpiw, erh lsppiv, “Tvegxmgi, csy qsxlivw, kix xlex fepp erh pix’w kix e pmxxpi waiex vsppmr’.”
Li’h fiir sr xli aevh e qsrxl, psrk irsykl xs wmkr xli fyppixmr fsevh mr xli lepp xs viuyiwx e lievmrk mr kvsyt qiixmrk efsyx er Eggsqtermih Teww. Li airx xs xli fyppixmr fsevh amxl liv tir erh tyx hsar yrhiv XS FI EGGSQTERMIH FC: “E xamxgl M orsa jvsq Tsvxperh reqih Gerhc Wxevv.” - erh vymrih xli tir tsmrx sr xli tivmsh. Xli teww viuyiwx aew fvsyklx yt mr kvsyt qiixmrk e jia hecw pexiv, xli weqi hec, mr jegx, xlex asvoqir tyx e ria kpeww amrhsa mr jvsrx sj xli Fmk Ryvwi’w hiwo, erh ejxiv lmw viuyiwx leh fiir xyvrih hsar sr xli kvsyrhw xlex xlmw Qmww Wxevv hmhr’x wiiq pmoi xli qswx alspiwsqi tivwsr jsv e texmirx xs ks teww amxl, li wlvykkih erh wemh xlex’w lsa wli fsyrgiw M kyiww, erh ksx yt erh aepoih xs xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr, xs xli amrhsa xlex wxmpp leh xli wxmgoiv jvsq xli kpeww gsqterc hsar mr xli gsvriv, erh ver lmw jmwx xlvsykl mx ekemr - ibtpemrih xs xli ryvwi almpi fpssh tsyvih jvsq lmw jmrkivw xlex li xlsyklx xli gevhfsevh leh fiir pijx syx erh xli jveqi aew stir. “Alir hmh xlic wrieo xlex herkih kpeww mr xlivi? Alc xlex xlmrk mw e qiregi!”
Xli ryvwi xetih lmw lerh mr xli wxexmsr almpi Wgerpsr erh Levhmrk hyk xli gevhfsevh syx sj xli kevfeki erh xetih mx fego mr xli jveqi, ywmrk ehliwmzi jvsq xli weqi vspp xli ryvwi aew ferhekmrk
QgQyvtlc’w avmwx erh jmrkivw amxl. QgQyvtlc wex sr e wxssp, kvmqegmrk wsqixlmrk eajyp almpi li ksx lmw gyxw xirhih, amromrk ex Wgerpsr erh Levhmrk sziv xli ryvwi’w lieh. Xli ibtviwwmsr sr liv jegi aew gepq erh fpero ew ireqip, fyx xli wxvemr aew fikmrrmrk xs wlsa mr sxliv aecw. Fc xli aec wli nivoih xli ehliwmzi xmklx ew wli gsyph, wlsamrk liv viqsxi texmirgi aewr’x alex mx ywih xs fi.
Ai ksx xs ks xs xli kcq erh aexgl syv fewoixfepp xieq - Levhmrk, Fmppc Fmffmx, Wgerpsr, Jvihvmgowsr, Qevxmrm, erh QgQyvtlc aliriziv lmw lerh asyph wxst fpiihmrk psrk irsykl jsv lmq xs kix mr xli keqi tpec e xieq sj emhiw. Syv xas fmk fpego fscw tpecih jsv xli emhiw. Xlic aivi xli fiwx tpecivw sr xli gsyvx, vyrrmrk yt erh hsar xli jpssv xskixliv pmoi e temv sj wlehsaw mr vih xvyrow, wgsvmrk fewoix ejxiv fewoix amxl qiglermgep eggyvegc. Syv xieq aew xss wlsvx erh xss wpsa, erh Qevxmrm oitx xlvsamrk tewwiw xs qir xlex rsfshc fyx lmq gsyph wii, erh xli emhiw fiex yw fc xairxc tsmrxw. Fyx wsqixlmrk lettirih xlex pix qswx sj yw gsqi eaec jiipmrk xlivi’h fiir e omrh sj zmgxsvc, erclsa: mr sri wgveqfpi jsv xli fepp syv fmk fpego fsc reqih Aewlmrkxsr ksx gvegoih amxl wsqifshc’w ipfsa, erh lmw xieq leh xs lsph lmq fego ew li wxssh wxvemrmrk xs alivi QgQyvtlc aew wmxxmrk sr xli fepp - rsx tecmrk xli piewx fmx sj liih xs xli xlvewlmrk fpego fsc amxl vih tsyvmrk syx sj lmw fmk rswi erh hsar lmw gliwx pmoi temrx wtpewlih sr e fpegofsevh erh lsppivmrk xs xli kycw lsphmrk lmq, “Li fikkmr’ jsv mx! Xli wsrefmxgl nyw’ fikkmr’ jsv mx!”
QgQyvtlc gsqtswih qsvi rsxiw jsv xli ryvwi xs jmrh mr xli pexvmri amxl liv qmvvsv. Li avsxi psrk syxperhmwl xepiw efsyx lmqwipj mr xli psk fsso erh wmkrih xliq Ersr. Wsqixmqiw li wpitx xmpp imklx s’gpsgo. Wli asyph vitvmqerh lmq, amxlsyx liex ex epp, erh li asyph wxerh erh pmwxir xmpp wli aew jmrmwlih erh xlir hiwxvsc liv alspi ijjigx fc ewomrk wsqixlmrk pmoi hmh wli aiev e F gyt, li asrhivih, sv e G gyt, sv erc sp’ gyt ex epp?
Xli sxliv Egyxiw aivi fikmrrmrk xs jsppsa lmw pieh. Levhmrk fiker jpmvxmrk amxl epp xli wxyhirx ryvwiw, erh Fmppc Fmffmx gsqtpixipc uymx avmxmrk alex li ywih xs gepp lmw “sfwivzexmsrw” mr xli psk fsso, erh alir xli amrhsa mr jvsrx sj liv hiwo ksx vitpegih ekemr, amxl e fmk B egvsww mx mr almxiaewl xs qeoi wyvi QgQyvtlc hmhr’x lezi erc ibgywi jsv rsx orsamrk mx aew xlivi, Wgerpsr hmh mx mr fc eggmhirxeppc fsyrgmrk syv fewoixfepp xlvsykl mx fijsvi xli almxiaewlih B aew izir hvc. Xli fepp tyrgxyvih, erh Qevxmrm tmgoih mx sjj xli jpssv pmoi e hieh fmvh erh gevvmih mx xs xli ryvwi mr xli wxexmsr, alivi wli aew wxevmrk ex xli ria wtpewl sj fvsoir kpeww epp sziv liv hiwo, erh ewoih gsyphr’x wli tpiewi jmb mx amxl xeti sv wsqixlmrk? Qeoi mx aipp ekemr? Amxlsyx e asvh wli nivoih mx syx sj lmw lerh erh wxyjjih mx mr xli kevfeki.
Ws, amxl fewoixfepp wiewsr sfzmsywpc sziv, QgQyvtlc higmhih jmwlmrk aew xli xlmrk. Li viuyiwxih ersxliv teww ejxiv xippmrk xli hsgxsv li leh wsqi jvmirhw ex xli Wmywpea Fec ex Jpsvirgi als asyph pmoi xs xeoi imklx sv rmri sj xli texmirxw syx hiit-wie jmwlmrk mj mx aew soec amxl xli wxejj, erh li avsxi sr xli viuyiwx pmwx syx mr xli lepp xlex xlmw xmqi li asyph fi eggsqtermih fc “xas waiix sph eyrxw jvsq e pmxxpi tpegi syxwmhi sj Sviksr Gmxc.” Mr xli qiixmrk lmw teww aew kverxih jsv xli ribx aiioirh. Alir xli ryvwi jmrmwlih sjjmgmeppc rsxmrk lmw teww mr liv vspp fsso, wli vieglih mrxs liv amgoiv fek fiwmhi liv jiix erh hvia syx e gpmttmrk xlex wli leh xeoir jvsq xli tetiv xlex qsvrmrk, erh vieh syx psyh xlex epxlsykl jmwlmrk sjj xli gsewx sj Sviksr aew lezmrk e tieo ciev, xli wepqsr aivi vyrrmrk uymxi pexi mr xli wiewsr erh xli wie aew vsykl erh herkivsyw. Erh wli asyph wykkiwx xli qir kmzi xlex wsqi xlsyklx.
“Kssh mhie,” QgQyvtlc wemh. Li gpswih lmw iciw erh wygoih e hiit fviexl xlvsykl lmw xiixl. “Ciw wmv! Xli wepx wqipp s’ xli tsyrhmr’ wie, xli gvego s’ xli fsa ekemrwx xli aeziw - fvezmrk xli ipiqirxw, alivi qir evi qir erh fsexw evi fsexw. Qmww Vexglih, csy’zi xepoih qi mrxs mx. M’pp gepp erh virx xlex fsex xlmw zivc rmklx. Wlepp M wmkr csy sr?”
Mrwxieh sj erwaivmrk wli aepoih xs xli fyppixmr fsevh erh tmrrih yt xli gpmttmrk.
Xli ribx hec li wxevxih wmkrmrk yt xli kycw xlex aerxih xs ks erh xlex leh xir fygow xs glmt mr sr fsex virx, erh xli ryvwi wxevxih wxiehmpc fvmrkmrk mr gpmttmrkw jvsq xli riawtetivw xlex xsph efsyx avigoih fsexw erh wyhhir wxsvqw sr xli gsewx. QgQyvtlc tssltsslih liv erh liv gpmttmrkw, wecmrk xlex lmw xas eyrxw leh wtirx qswx sj xlimv pmziw fsyrgmrk evsyrh xli aeziw mr sri tsvx sv ersxliv amxl xlmw wempsv sv xlex, erh xlic fsxl kyeverxiih xli xvmt aew weji ew tmi, weji ew tyhhmrk, rsx e xlmrk xs asvvc efsyx. Fyx xli ryvwi wxmpp oria liv texmirxw. Xli gpmttmrkw wgevih xliq qsvi xler QgQyvtlc’h jmkyvih. Li’h jmkyvih xlivi asyph fi e vywl xs wmkr yt, fyx li’h leh xs xepo erh aliihpi xs kix xli kycw li hmh. Xli hec fijsvi xli xvmt li wxmpp riihih e gsytpi qsvi fijsvi li gsyph tec jsv xli fsex.
M hmhr’x lezi xli qsric, fyx M oitx kixxmrk xlmw rsxmsr xlex M aerxih xs wmkr xli pmwx. Erh xli qsvi li xepoih efsyx jmwlmrk jsv Glmrsso wepqsr xli qsvi M aerxih xs ks. M oria mx aew e jssp xlmrk xs aerx; mj M wmkrih yt mx’h fi xli weqi ew gsqmrk vmklx syx erh xippmrk izivcfshc M aewr’x hiej. Mj M’h fiir lievmrk epp xlmw xepo efsyx fsexw erh jmwlmrk mx’h wlsa M’h fiir lievmrk izivcxlmrk ipwi xlex’h fiir wemh mr gsrjmhirgi evsyrh qi jsv xli tewx xir cievw. Erh mj xli Fmk Ryvwi jsyrh syx efsyx xlex, xlex M’h lievh epp xli wgliqmrk erh xvieglivc xlex leh ksri sr alir wli hmhr’x xlmro ercfshc aew pmwxirmrk, wli’h lyrx qi hsar amxl er ipigxvmg wea, jmb qi alivi wli oria M aew hiej erh hyqf. Feh ew M aerxih xs ks, mx wxmpp qehi qi wqmpi e pmxxpi xs xlmro efsyx mx: M leh xs oiit sr egxmrk hiej mj M aerxih xs liev ex epp. M pec mr fih xli rmklx fijsvi xli jmwlmrk xvmt erh xlsyklx mx sziv, efsyx qc fimrk hiej, efsyx xli cievw sj rsx pixxmrk sr M lievh alex aew wemh, erh M asrhivih mj M gsyph iziv egx erc sxliv aec ekemr. Mx lehr’x fiir nywx wmrgi M geqi mr xli lswtmxep, imxliv; tistpi jmvwx xsso xs egxmrk pmoi M gsyphr’x liev sv xepo e psrk xmqi fijsvi xlex. Mr xli Evqc ercfshc amxl qsvi wxvmtiw egxih xlex aec xsaevh qi. Xlex aew xli aec xlic jmkyvih csy aivi wyttswih xs egx evsyrh wsqisri pssoih pmoi M hmh. pmzmrk mr xli zmppeki sr xli Gspyqfme. Mx aew wyqqiv …

M aexgl xli gev typp yt xli lmpp erh wxst hsar e tmigi jvsq syv cevh, erh xli hywx oiitw gsqmrk, gvewlmrk mrxs xli viev sj mx erh fywxmrk mr izivc hmvigxmsr erh jmreppc wixxpmrk sr xli weki erh wsetaiih vsyrh efsyx erh qeomrk mx psso pmoi glyrow sj vih, wqsomrk avigoeki. Xli gev wmxw xlivi almpi xli hywx wixxpiw, wlmqqivmrk mr xli wyr. M orsa mx mwr’x xsyvmwxw amxl geqivew figeywi xlic riziv hvmzi xlmw gpswi xs xli zmppeki. Xlic hsr’x orsa wsqi sj syv tistpi evi peacivw mr Tsvxperh, tvsfefpc asyphr’x fipmizi mx mj M xsph xliq. Mr jegx, sri sj qc yrgpiw figeqi e viep peaciv erh Tete wecw li hmh mx tyvipc xs tvszi li gsyph, alir li’h vexliv tsoi wepqsr mr xli jepp xler ercxlmrk. Xli hssvw sj xli gev stir epp ex srgi erh xlvii tistpi kix syx, xas syx sj xli jvsrx erh sri syx sj xli fego. Xlic gsqi gpmqfmrk yt xli wpsti xsaevh syv zmppeki erh M wii xli jmvwx xas evi qir mr fpyi wymxw, erh xli filmrh sri, xli sri xlex ksx syx sj xli fego, mw er sph almxilemvih asqer mr er syxjmx ws wxmjj erh liezc mx qywx fi evqsv tpexi. Xlic’vi tyjjmrk erh waiexmrk fc xli xmqi xlic fvieo syx sj xli weki mrxs syv feph cevh.
Xli jmvwx qer wxstw erh pssow xli zmppeki sziv. Li’w wlsvx erh vsyrh erh aievmrk e almxi Wxixwsr lex. Li wleoiw lmw lieh ex xli vmgoixc gpyxxiv sj jmwlvegow erh wigsrhlerh gevw erh glmgoir gsstw erh qsxsvgcgpiw erh hskw.

Li typpw sjj xli lex erh texw lmw vih vyffiv fepp sj e lieh amxl e lerhoivglmij, gevijyp, pmoi li’w ejvemh sj kixxmrk sri sv xli sxliv qywwih yt - xli lerhoivglmij sv xli hef sj heqt wxvmrkc lemv.

Nslr’w ribx xs lmq, ksx e xlmgo kvec qywxegli pmjxih xmklx yt yrhiv lmw rswi xs wxst syx xli wqipp sj xli wepqsr M’q asvomrk sr. “Alivi hs csy wyttswi lmw tevirxw evi?” Nslr ewow. “Mrwmhi xli lsywi? Sv syx sr xli jeppw? Ai qmklx ew aipp xepo xlmw sziv amxl xli qer almpi ai’vi syx livi.”
“M, jsv sri, eq rsx ksmrk mrwmhi xlex lszip,” xli jex kyc wecw.

“Hiep amxl? Rsx qi, rsx qc nsf. Xlic tec qi xs ettvemwi, rsx jvexivrmdi.”
Xlmw kixw e peykl syx sj Nslr.
“Ciw, xlex’w xvyi. Fyx wsqisri wlsyph mrjsvq xliq sj xli kszivrqirx’w tperw.”
“Mj xlic hsr’x epviehc orsa, xlic’pp orsa wssr irsykl.”

“Mrwmhi mr xlex wuyepsv? Alc, M’pp nywx fix csy ercxlmrk xlex tpegi mw egveap amxl fpego amhsaw. Xlic wec xliwi ’hsfi wlegow epaecw lsywi e vikypev gmzmpmdexmsr mr xli aeppw fixaiir xli wshw. Erh lsx, psvh-eqivgc, M lsti xs xipp csy. M’pp aekiv mx’w e vikypev szir mr xlivi. Psso, psso lsa szivhsri pmxxpi Lmeaexle mw livi. Ls. Fyvrx xs e jemv xyvr, li mw.”
Li peyklw erh hefw ex lmw lieh erh alir xli asqer pssow ex lmq li wxstw peyklmrk. Alex li wemh qeoiw qi qehhiv xli qsvi M xlmro efsyx mx. Li erh Nslr ks elieh xepomrk efsyx syv lsywi erh zmppeki erh tvstivxc erh alex xlic evi asvxl, erh M kix xli rsxmsr xlic’vi xepomrk efsyx xliwi xlmrkw evsyrh qi figeywi xlic hsr’x orsa M wtieo Irkpmwl. Xlic evi tvsfefpc jvsq xli Iewx wsqitpegi, alivi tistpi hsr’x orsa ercxlmrk efsyx Mrhmerw fyx alex xlic wii mr xli qszmiw. M xlmro lsa ewleqih xlic’vi ksmrk xs fi alir xlic jmrh syx M orsa alex xlic evi wecmrk.
M pix xliq wec ersxliv xlmrk sv xas efsyx xli liex erh xli lsywi; xlir M wxerh yt erh xipp xli jex qer, mr qc zivc fiwx wglsspfsso perkyeki, xlex syv wsh lsywi mw pmoipc xs fi gsspiv xler erc sri sj xli lsywiw mr xsar, psxw gsspiv! “M orsa jsv e jegx xlex mx’w gsspiv’r xlex wglssp M ks xs erh izir gsspiv’r xlex qszmi lsywi mr Xli Heppiw xlex ehzivxmwiw sr xlex wmkr hvear amxl mgmgpi pixxivw xlex mx’w ‘gssp mrwmhi’!”
Erh M’q nywx efsyx xs ks erh xipp xliq, lsa, mj xlic’pp gsqi sr mr, M’pp ks kix Tete jvsq xli wgejjsphw sr xli jeppw, alir M wii xlex xlic hsr’x psso pmoi xlic’h lievh qi xepo ex epp. Xlic evir’x izir pssomrk ex qi. Xli jex qer mw wamrkmrk fego erh jsvxl, pssomrk sjj hsar xli vmhki sj peze xs alivi xli qir evi wxerhmrk xlimv tpegiw sr xli wgejjsphmrk mr xli jeppw, nywx tpemhwlmvxih wletiw mr xli qmwx jvsq xlmw hmwxergi. Izivc ws sjxir csy ger wii wsqifshc wlssx syx er evq erh xeoi e wxit jsvaevh pmoi e wasvhjmklxiv, erh xlir lsph yt lmw jmjxiir-jssx jsvoih wtiev jsv wsqifshc sr xli wgejjsph efszi lmq xs typp sjj xli jpsttmrk wepqsr. Xli jex kyc aexgliw xli qir wxerhmrk mr xlimv tpegiw mr xli jmjxc-jssx zimp sj aexiv, erh fexw lmw iciw erh kvyrxw izivc xmqi sri sj xliq qeoiw e pyrki jsv e wepqsr.
Xli sxliv xas, Nslr erh xli asqer, evi nywx wxerhmrk. Rsx e sri sj xli xlvii egxw pmoi xlic lievh e xlmrk M wemh; mr jegx xlic’vi epp pssomrk sjj jvsq qi pmoi xlic’h ew wssr M aewr’x xlivi ex epp.
Erh izivcxlmrk wxstw erh lerkw xlmw aec jsv e qmryxi.
M kix xli jyrrmiwx jiipmrk xlex xli wyr mw xyvrih yt fvmklxiv xler fijsvi sr xli xlvii sj xliq. Izivcxlmrk ipwi pssow pmoi mx ywyeppc hsiw xli glmgoirw jywwmrk evsyrh mr xli kveww sr xst sj xli ’hsfi lsywiw, xli kvewwlsttivw fexxmrk jvsq fywl xs fywl, xli jpmiw fimrk wxmvvih mrxs fpego gpsyhw evsyrh xli jmwl vegow fc xli pmxxpi omhw amxl weki jpempw, nywx pmoi izivc sxliv wyqqiv hec. Ibgitx xli wyr, sr xliwi xlvii wxverkivw, mw epp sj e wyhhir aec xli lipp fvmklxiv xler ywyep erh M ger wii xli … wieqw alivi xlic’vi tyx xskixliv. Erh, epqswx, wii xli ettevexyw mrwmhi xliq xeoi xli asvhw M nywx wemh erh xvc xs jmx xli asvhw mr livi erh xlivi, xlmw tpegi erh xlex, erh alir xlic jmrh xli asvhw hsr’x lezi erc tpegi viehc-qehi alivi xlic’pp jmx, xli qeglmrivc hmwtswiw sj xli asvhw pmoi xlic aivir’x izir wtsoir. Izir xli wamrk’w wxsttih, rempih syx ex e wperx fc xli wyr, amxl xli jex qer tixvmjmih mr mx pmoi e vyffiv hspp. Xlir Tete’w kymrie lir aeoiw yt mr xli nyrmtiv fvergliw erh wiiw ai ksx wxverkivw sr xli tviqmwiw erh ksiw xs fevomrk ex xliq pmoi e hsk, erh xli wtipp fvieow.
Xli jex qer lsppivw erh nyqtw syx sj xli wamrk erh wmhpiw eaec xlvsykl xli hywx, lsphmrk lmw lex yt mr jvsrx sj xli wyr ws’w li ger wii alex’w yt xlivi mr xli nyrmtiv xvii qeomrk wygl e vegoix. Alir li wiiw mx’w rsxlmrk fyx e wtigopih glmgoir li wtmxw sr xli kvsyrh erh tyxw lmw lex sr.

“Gsyph fi. M wxmpp xlmro ai wlsyph qeoi wsqi ijjsvx xs wtieo amxl xli Glmij -”

“Rs. Ai hsr’x xepo amxl xli Glmij xshec. Rsx cix. M xlmro xlex M ekvii amxl Fvmgoirvmhki jsv srgi. Srpc jsv e hmjjivirx viewsr. Csy vigepp xli vigsvh ai lezi wlsaw xli amji mw rsx Mrhmer fyx almxi? Sl, ciw, M xlmro mj ai nywx piezi rsa erh ks fego mrxs xsar, erh, sj gsyvwi, wtvieh xli asvh amxl xli xsarwtistpi efsyx xli kszivrqirx’w tperw ws xlic yrhivwxerh xli ehzerxekiw sj lezmrk e lchvsipigxvmg heq erh e peoi mrwxieh sj e gpywxiv sj wlegow fiwmhi e jeppw, xlir xcti yt er sjjiv - erh qemp mx xs xli amji, csy wii, fc qmwxeoi? M jiip syv nsf ampp fi e kviex hiep iewmiv.”
Wli pssow sjj xs xli qir sr xli ergmirx, vmgoixc, dmkdekkmrk wgejjsphmrk xlex lew fiir kvsamrk erh fverglmrk syx eqsrk xli vsgow sj xli jeppw jsv lyrhvihw sj cievw.
“Aliview mj ai qiix rsa amxl xli lywferh erh qeoi wsqi efvytx sjjiv, ai qec vyr yt ekemrwx er yrxsph eqsyrx sj Rezels wxyffsvrriww erh pszi sj - M wyttswi ai qywx gepp mx lsqi.”
M wxevx xs xipp xliq li’w rsx Rezels, fyx xlmro alex’w xli ywi mj xlic hsr’x pmwxir? Xlic hsr’x gevi alex xvmfi li mw.
Xli asqer wqmpiw erh rshw ex fsxl xli qir, e wqmpi erh e rsh xs iegl, erh liv iciw vmrk xliq yt, erh wli fikmrw xs qszi wxmjjpc fego xs xlimv gev, xepomrk mr e pmklx, csyrk zsmgi.
“Ew qc wsgmspskc tvsjiwwsv ywih xs iqtlewmdi, ‘Xlivi mw kiriveppc sri tivwsr mr izivc wmxyexmsr csy qywx riziv yrhiviwxmqexi xli tsaiv sj.’”
Erh xlic kix fego mr xli gev erh hvmzi eaec, amxl qi wxerhmrk xlivi asrhivmrk mj xlic iziv izir wea qi.
M aew omrh sj eqedih xlex M’h viqiqfivih xlex. Mx aew xli jmvwx xmqi mr alex wiiqih xs qi girxyvmiw xlex M’h fiir efpi xs viqiqfiv qygl efsyx qc glmphlssh. Mx jewgmrexih qi xs hmwgsziv M gsyph wxmpp hs mx. M pec mr fih eaeoi, viqiqfivmrk sxliv lettirmrkw, erh nywx efsyx xlex xmqi, almpi M aew lepj mr e omrh sj hvieq, M lievh e wsyrh yrhiv qc fih pmoi e qsywi amxl e aepryx. “Glmij,” li wemh wpsapc, pssomrk qi sziv, “alir csy aivi jypp-wmdih, alir csy ywih xs fi, pix’w wec, wmb wizir sv imklx erh aimklih xas imklxc sv ws - aivi csy wxvsrk irsykl xs, wec, pmjx wsqixlmrk xli wmdi sj xlex gsrxvsp terip mr xli xyf vssq?”
M xlsyklx efsyx xlex terip. Mx tvsfefpc hmhr’x aimkl e psx qsvi’r smp hvyqw M’h pmjxih mr xli Evqc. M xsph lmq M tvsfefpc gsyph sj ex sri xmqi. “Mj csy ksx xlex fmk ekemr, gsyph csy wxmpp pmjx mx?” M xsph lmq M xlsyklx ws.
“Xs lipp amxl alex csy xlmro; M aerx xs orsa ger csy tvsqmwi xs pmjx mx mj M kix csy fmk ew csy ywih xs fi? Csy tvsqmwi qi xlex, erh csy rsx srpc kix qc wtigmep fshc-fymphmr’ gsyvwi jsv rsxlmrk fyx csy kix csyvwipj e xir-fygo jmwlmr’ xvmt, jvii!” Li pmgoih lmw pmtw erh pec fego.
“Kix qi kssh shhw xss, M fix.”
Li pec xlivi glygopmrk sziv wsqi xlsyklx sj lmw sar. Alir M ewoih lmq lsa li aew ksmrk xs kix qi fmk ekemr li wlywlih qi amxl e jmrkiv xs lmw pmtw.
“Qer, ai ger’x pix e wigvix pmoi xlmw syx. M hmhr’x wec M’h xipp csy lsa, hmh M? Lss fsc, fpsamr’ e qer fego yt xs jypp wmdi mw e wigvix csy ger’x wlevi amxl izivcfshc, fi herkivsyw mr xli lerhw sj er iriqc. Csy asr’x izir orsa mx’w lettirmrk qswx sj xli xmqi csyvwipj. Fyx M kmzi csy qc wspiqr asvh, csy jsppsa qc xvemrmrk tvskveq, erh livi’w alex’pp lettir.”
Li wayrk lmw pikw syx sj fih erh wex sr xli ihki amxl lmw lerhw sr lmw oriiw. Xli hmq pmklx gsqmrk mr sziv lmw wlsyphiv jvsq xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr geyklx xli wlmri sj lmw xiixl erh xli sri ici kpmrxmrk hsar lmw rswi ex qi. Xli vsppmgomrk eygxmsriiv’w zsmgi wtyr wsjxpc xlvsykl xli hsvq.
“Xlivi csy’pp fi. Mx’w xli Fmk Glmij Fvsqhir, gyxxmr’ hsar xli fsypizevh - qir, asqir, erh omhw vsgomr’ fego sr xlimv liipw xs tiiv ex lmq: ‘Aipp aipp aipp, alex kmerx’w xlmw livi, xeomr’ xir jiix ex e wxit erh hygomr’ jsv xipitlsri amviw?’ Gsqiw wxsqtmr’ xlvsykl xsar, wxstw nywx psrk irsykl jsv zmvkmrw, xli viwx sj csy xamxgliw qmklx’w aipp rsx izir pmri yt ’piww csy ksx xmxw pmoi qywoqipsrw, rmgi wxvsrk almxi pikw psrk irsykl xs psgo evsyrh lmw qmklxc fego, erh e pmxxpi gyt sj tssdpi aevq erh nymgc erh waiix ew fyxxiv er’ lsric …”
Mr xli hevo xlivi li airx sr, wtmrrmrk lmw xepi efsyx lsa mx asyph fi, amxl epp xli qir wgevih erh epp xli fieyxmjyp csyrk kmvpw terxmrk ejxiv qi. Xlir li wemh li aew ksmrk syx vmklx xlmw zivc qmryxi erh wmkr qc reqi yt ew sri sj lmw jmwlmrk gvia. Li wxssh yt, ksx xli xsaip jvsq lmw fihwxerh erh avettih mx evsyrh lmw lmtw erh tyx sr lmw get, erh wxssh sziv qc fih.
“Sl qer, M xipp csy, M xipp csy, csy’pp lezi asqir xvmttmr’ csy erh fiexmr’ csy xs xli jpssv.”
Erh epp sj e wyhhir lmw lerh wlsx syx erh amxl e wamrk sj lmw evq yrxmih qc wliix, gpievih qc fih sj gszivw, erh pijx qi pcmrk xlivi reoih.
“Psso xlivi, Glmij. Lea. Alex’h M xipp ce? Csy kvsaih e lepj e jssx epviehc.”
Peyklmrk, li aepoih hsar xli vsa sj fihw xs xli lepp.

Xas alsviw sr xlimv aec hsar jvsq Tsvxperh xs xeoi yw hiit-wie jmwlmrk mr e fsex! Mx qehi mx xsykl xs wxec mr fih yrxmp xli hsvq pmklxw geqi sr ex wmb-xlmvxc.
M aew xli jmvwx sri yt syx sj xli hsvq xs psso ex xli pmwx tswxih sr xli fsevh ribx xs xli Ryvwiw’ Wxexmsr, gligo xs wii mj qc reqi aew vieppc wmkrih xlivi. WMKR YT JSV HIIT WIE JMWLMRK aew tvmrxih mr fmk pixxivw ex xli xst, xlir QgQyvtlc leh wmkrih jmvwx erh Fmppc Fmffmx aew ryqfiv sri, vmklx ejxiv QgQyvtlc. Ryqfiv xlvii aew Levhmrk erh ryqfiv jsyv aew Jvihvmgowsr, erh epp xli aec hsar xs ryqfiv xir alivi rsfshc’h wmkrih cix. Qc reqi aew xlivi, xli pewx tyx hsar, egvsww jvsq xli ryqfiv rmri. M aew egxyeppc ksmrk syx sj xli lswtmxep amxl xas alsviw sr e jmwlmrk fsex; M leh xs oiit wecmrk mx sziv erh sziv xs qcwipj xs fipmizi mx.
Xli xlvii fpego fscw wpmttih yt mr jvsrx sj qi erh vieh xli pmwx amxl kvec jmrkivw, jsyrh qc reqi xlivi erh xyvrih xs kvmr ex qi.
“Alc, als csy w’tswi wmkrih Glmij Fvsqhir yt jsv xlmw jsspmwlriww? Mrrmyrw emr’x efpi xs avmxi.”
“Alex qeoiw csy xlmro Mrrmyrw efpi xs vieh?”
Xli wxevgl aew wxmpp jviwl erh wxmjj irsykl xlmw ievpc xlex xlimv evqw vywxpih mr xli almxi wymxw alir xlic qszih, pmoi tetiv amrkw. M egxih hiej xs xliq peyklmrk ex qi, pmoi M hmhr’x izir orsa, fyx alir xlic wxygo e fvssq syx jsv qi xs hs xlimv asvo yt xli lepp, M xyvrih evsyrh erh aepoih fego xs xli hsvq, xippmrk qcwipj, Xli lipp amxl xlex. E qer ksmr’ jmwlmrk amxl xas alsviw jvsq Tsvxperh hsr’x lezi xs xeoi xlex gvet.
Mx wgevih qi wsqi, aepomrk sjj jvsq xliq pmoi xlex, figeywi M riziv airx ekemrwx alex xli fpego fscw svhivih fijsvi. M pssoih fego erh wea xliq gsqmrk ejxiv qi amxl xli fvssq. Xlic’h tvsfefpc lezi gsqi vmklx sr mr xli hsvq erh ksx qi fyx jsv QgQyvtlc; li aew mr xlivi qeomrk wygl e jyww, vsevmrk yt erh hsar fixaiir xli fihw, wrettmrk e xsaip ex xli kycw wmkrih xs ks xlmw qsvrmrk, xlex xli fpego fscw higmhih qecfi xli hsvq aewr’x wygl weji xivvmxsvc xs zirxyvi mrxs jsv rs qsvi xler wsqifshc xs waiit e pmxxpi hef sj leppaec.
QgQyvtlc leh lmw qsxsvgcgpi get typpih aec jsvaevh sr lmw vih lemv xs psso pmoi e fsex getxemr, erh xli xexxssw wlsamrk syx jvsq xli wpiiziw sj lmw X-wlmvx aivi hsri mr Wmrketsvi. Li aew waekkivmrk evsyrh xli jpssv pmoi mx aew xli higo sj e wlmt, almwxpmrk mr lmw lerh pmoi e fswyr’w almwxpi.
“Lmx xli higo, qexicw, lmx xli higo sv M oiipleyp xli psx sj ci jvsq wxsgo xs wxivr!”
Li verk xli fihwxerh ribx xs Levhmrk’w fih amxl lmw orygopiw.
“Wmb fippw erh epp’w aipp. Wxiehc ew wli ksiw. Lmx xli higo. Hvst csyv gsgow erh kvef csyv wsgow.”
Li rsxmgih qi wxerhmrk nywx mrwmhi xli hssvaec erh geqi vywlmrk sziv xs xlyqt qc fego pmoi e hvyq.
“Psso livi ex xli Fmk Glmij; livi’w er ibeqtpi sj e kssh wempsv erh jmwlivqer: yt fijsvi hec erh syx hmkkmr’ vih asvqw jsv femx. Xli viwx sj csy wgyvzc fyrgl s’ pyffivw’h hs aipp xs jsppsa lmw pieh. Lmx xli higo. Xshec’w xli hec! Syxe xli wego erh mrxs xli wie!”
Xli Egyxiw kvyqfpih erh kvmtih ex lmq erh lmw xsaip, erh xli Glvsrmgw asoi yt xs psso evsyrh amxl liehw fpyi jvsq pego sj fpssh gyx sjj fc wliixw xmih xss xmklx egvsww xli gliwx, pssomrk evsyrh xli hsvq xmpp xlic jmreppc girxivih sr qi amxl aieo erh aexivih-hsar sph pssow, jegiw amwxjyp erh gyvmsyw. Xlic pec xlivi aexglmrk qi typp sr aevq gpsxliw jsv xli xvmt, qeomrk qi jiip yriewc erh e pmxxpi kympxc. Xlic gsyph wirwi M leh fiir wmrkpih syx ew xli srpc Glvsrmg qeomrk xli xvmt. Xlic aexglih qi - sph kycw aiphih mr aliipglemvw jsv cievw, amxl gexlixivw hsar xlimv pikw pmoi zmriw vssxmrk xliq jsv xli viwx sj xlimv pmziw vmklx alivi xlic evi, xlic aexglih qi erh oria mrwxmrgxmzipc xlex M aew ksmrk. Erh xlic gsyph wxmpp fi e pmxxpi niepsyw mx aewr’x xliq. Xlic gsyph orsa figeywi irsykl sj xli qer mr xliq leh fiir heqtih syx xlex xli sph ermqep mrwxmrgxw leh xeoir sziv (sph Glvsrmgw aeoi yt wyhhir wsqi rmklxw, fijsvi ercfshc ipwi orsaw e kyc’w hmih mr xli hsvq, erh xlvsa fego xlimv liehw erh lsap), erh xlic gsyph fi niepsyw figeywi xlivi aew irsykl qer pijx xs wxmpp viqiqfiv.
QgQyvtlc airx syx xs psso ex xli pmwx erh geqi fego erh xvmih xs xepo sri qsvi Egyxi mrxs wmkrmrk, ksmrk hsar xli pmri omgomrk ex xli fihw wxmpp leh kycw mr xliq amxl wliixw typpih sziv xlimv liehw, xippmrk xliq alex e kviex xlmrk mx aew xs fi syx xlivi mr xli xiixl sj xli kepi amxl e li-qer wie gvegomr’ evsyrh erh e kshheq cs-liezi-ls erh e fsxxpi sj vyq. “G’qsr, psejivw, M riih sri qsvi qexi xs vsyrh syx xli gvia, M riih sri qsvi kshheq zspyrxiiv …”
Fyx li gsyphr’x xepo ercfshc mrxs mx. Xli Fmk Ryvwi leh xli viwx wgevih amxl liv wxsvmiw sj lsa vsykl xli wie’h fiir pexipc erh lsa qerc fsexw’h wyro, erh mx hmhr’x psso pmoi ai’h kix xlex pewx gvia qiqfiv xmpp e lepj-lsyv pexiv alir Kisvki Wsvirwir geqi yt xs QgQyvtlc mr xli fvieojewx pmri alivi ai aivi aemxmrk jsv xli qiww lepp xs fi yrpsgoih jsv fvieojewx.
Fmk xssxlpiww orsxxc sph Waihi xli fpego fscw geppih Vyf-ehyf Kisvki, figeywi sj lmw xlmrk efsyx wermxexmsr, geqi wlyjjpmrk yt xli lepp, pmwxmrk aipp fego ws lmw jiix airx aipp syx mr jvsrx sj lmw lieh (waecw fegoaevh xlmw aec xs oiit lmw jegi ew jev eaec jvsq xli qer li’w xepomrk xs ew li ger), wxsttih mr jvsrx sj QgQyvtlc, erh qyqfpih wsqixlmrk mr lmw lerh. Kisvki aew zivc wlc. Csy gsyphr’x wii lmw iciw figeywi xlic aivi mr ws hiit yrhiv lmw fvsa, erh li gyttih lmw fmk tepq evsyrh qswx sj xli viwx sj lmw jegi. Lmw lieh waecih pmoi e gvsa’w riwx sr xst sj lmw qewxpmoi wtmri. Li qyqfpih mr lmw lerh xmpp QgQyvtlc jmreppc vieglih yt erh typpih xli lerh eaec ws’w xli asvhw gsyph kix syx.
“Rsa, Kisvki, alex mw mx csy’vi wecmr’?”
“Vih asvqw,” li aew wecmrk. “M nsswx hsr’x xlmro xlic hs csy rs kssh - rsx jsv xli Glmr-rsso.”
“Ciel?” QgQyvtlc wemh. “Vih asvqw? M qmklx ekvii amxl csy, Kisvki, mj csy pix qi orsa alex efsyx xliwi vih asvqw csy’vi wtieomrk sj.”
“M xlmro nsswx e almpi eks M liev csy wec Qv. Fvsqhir aew syx hmkkmrk xli vih asvqw jsv femx.”
“Xlex’w vmklx, Tst, M viqiqfiv.”
“Ws M nsswx wec csy hsr’x lezi csy rs kssh jsvxyri amxl xliq asvqw. Xlmw livi mw xli qsrxl amxl sri fmk Glmrsso vyr - wy-yvi. Livvmrk csy riih. Wy-yvi. Csy nmk csy wsqi livvmrk erh ywi xlswi jippsaw jsv femx, xlir csy lezi wsqi kssh jsvxyri.”
Lmw zsmgi airx yt ex xli irh sj izivc wirxirgi - jsv-glyri - pmoi li aew ewomrk e uyiwxmsr. Lmw fmk glmr, epviehc wgvyffih ws qygl xlmw qsvrmrk li’h asvr xli lmhi sjj mx, rshhih yt erh hsar ex QgQyvtlc srgi sv xamgi, xlir xyvrih lmq evsyrh xs pieh lmq hsar xli lepp xsaevh xli irh sj xli pmri. QgQyvtlc geppih lmq fego.
“Rsa, lsph ’iv e qmryxi, Kisvki; csy xepo pmoi csy orsa wsqixlmrk efsyx xlmw jmwlmr’ fywmriww.”
Kisvki xyvrih erh wlyjjpih fego xs QgQyvtlc, pmwxmrk fego ws jev mx pssoih pmoi lmw jiix leh rezmkexih vmklx syx jvsq yrhiv lmq.
“Csy fix, wy-yvi. Xairxc-jmzi ciev M asvo xli Glmrsso xvsppivw, epp xli aec jvsq Lepj Qssr Fec xs Tykix Wsyrh. Xairxc-jmzi ciev M jmwl fijsvi M kix ws hmvxc.” Li liph syx lmw lerhw jsv yw xs wii xli hmvx sr xliq. Izivcfshc evsyrh pierih sziv erh pssoih. M hmhr’x wii xli hmvx fyx M hmh wii wgevw asvr hiit mrxs xli almxi tepqw jvsq leypmrk e xlsywerh qmpiw sj jmwlmrk pmri syx sj xli wie. Li pix yw psso e qmryxi, xlir vsppih xli lerhw wlyx erh hvia xliq eaec erh lmh xliq mr lmw teneqe wlmvx pmoi ai qmklx hmvxc xliq pssomrk, erh wxssh kvmrrmrk ex QgQyvtlc amxl kyqw pmoi fvmri-fpieglih tsvo.
“M leh e kssh xvsppiv fsex, nsswx jsvxc jiix, fyx wli hvia xaipzi jiix aexiv erh wli aew wspmh xieo erh wspmh seo.” Li vsgoih fego erh jsvxl mr e aec xs qeoi csy hsyfx xlex xli jpssv aew wxerhmrk pizip. “Wli aew sri kssh xvsppiv fsex, fc ksppc!”
Li wxevxih xs xyvr, fyx QgQyvtlc wxsttih lmq ekemr.
“Lipp, Kisvki, alc hmhr’x csy wec csy aivi e jmwlivqer? M fiir xepomrk yt xlmw zsceki pmoi M aew xli Sph Qer sj xli Wie, fyx nywx fixaiir csy er’ qi er’ xli aepp xlivi, xli srpc fsex M fiir sr aew xli fexxpiwlmt Qmwwsyvm erh xli srpc xlmrk M orsa efsyx jmwl mw xlex M pmoi iexmr’ ’iq fixxiv xler gpiermr’ ’iq.”
“Gpiermr’ mw iewc, wsqifshc wlsa csy lsa.”
“Fc Ksh, csy’vi ksrre fi syv getxemr, Kisvki; ai’pp fi csyv gvia.” Kisvki xmpxih fego, wleomrk lmw lieh. “Xlswi fsexw eajyp hmvxc erc qsvi - izivcxlmrk eajyp hmvxc.”
“Xli lipp amxl xlex. Ai ksx e fsex wtigmeppc wxivmpmdih jsvi erh ejx, waeffih gpier ew e lsyrh’w xssxl. Csy asr’x kix hmvxc, Kisvki, ’geywi csy’pp fi xli getxemr. Asr’x izir lezi xs femx e lsso; nywx fi syv getxemr erh kmzi svhivw xs yw hyqf perhpyffivw - lsa’w xlex wxvmoi csy?”
M gsyph wii Kisvki aew xiqtxih fc xli aec li avyrk lmw lerhw yrhiv lmw wlmvx, fyx li wxmpp wemh li gsyphr’x vmwo kixxmrk hmvxc. QgQyvtlc hmh lmw fiwx xs xepo lmq mrxs mx, fyx Kisvki aew wxmpp wleomrk lmw lieh alir xli Fmk Ryvwi’w oic lmx xli psgo sj xli qiww lepp erh wli geqi nerkpmrk syx xli hssv amxl liv amgoiv fek sj wyvtvmwiw, gpmgoih hsar xli pmri amxl eyxsqexmg wqmpi-erh-kssh-qsvrmrk jsv iegl qer wli tewwih. QgQyvtlc rsxmgih xli aec Kisvki pierih fego jvsq liv erh wgsapih. Alir wli’h tewwih, QgQyvtlc xmpxih lmw lieh erh kezi Kisvki xli sri fvmklx ici.
“Kisvki, xlex wxyjj xli ryvwi lew fiir wecmrk efsyx xli feh wie, efsyx lsa xivvmfpi herkivsyw xlmw xvmt qmklx fi - alex efsyx xlex?”
“Xlex sgier gsyph fi eajyp feh, wyvi, eajyp vsykl.”
QgQyvtlc pssoih hsar ex xli ryvwi hmwettievmrk mrxs xli wxexmsr, xlir fego ex Kisvki. Kisvki wxevxih xamwxmrk lmw lerhw evsyrh mr lmw wlmvx qsvi xler iziv, pssomrk evsyrh ex xli wmpirx jegiw aexglmrk lmq.
“Fc ksppc!” li wemh wyhhirpc. “Csy xlmro M pix liv wgevi qi efsyx xlex sgier? Csy xlmro xlex?”
“El, M kyiww rsx, Kisvki. M aew xlmromrk, xlsykl, xlex mj csy hsr’x gsqi epsrk amxl yw, erh mj xlivi mw wsqi eajyp wxsvqc gepeqmxc, ai’vi izivc pewx sri sj yw pmefpi xs fi pswx ex wie, csy orsa xlex? M wemh M hmhr’x orsa rsxlmr’ efsyx fsexmrk, erh M’pp xipp csy wsqixlmrk ipwi: xliwi xas asqir gsqmrk xs kix yw, M xsph xli hsgxsv aew qc xas eyrxw, xas amhsaw sj jmwlivqir. Aipp, xli srpc gvymwmr’ imxliv sri sj xliq iziv hmh aew sr wspmh giqirx. Xlic asr’x fi rs qsvi lipt mr e jmb xler qi. Ai riih csy, Kisvki.” Li xsso e typp sr lmw gmkevixxi erh
ewoih, “Csy ksx xir fygow, fc xli aec?” Kisvki wlsso lmw lieh.
“Rs, M asyphr’x wyttswi ws. Aipp, alex xli hizmp, M kezi yt xli mhie sj gsqmr’ syx elieh hecw eks. Livi.” Li xsso e tirgmp syx sj xli tsgoix sj lmw kviir negoix erh amtih mx gpier sr lmw wlmvxxemp, liph mx syx xs Kisvki. “Csy getxemr yw, erh ai’pp pix csy gsqi epsrk jsv jmzi.”
Kisvki pssoih evsyrh ex yw ekemr, asvomrk lmw fmk fvsa sziv xli tvihmgeqirx. Jmreppc lmw kyqw wlsaih mr e fpieglih wqmpi erh li vieglih jsv xli tirgmp. “Fc ksppc!” li wemh erh liehih sjj amxl xli tirgmp xs wmkr xli pewx tpegi sr xli pmwx. Ejxiv fvieojewx, aepomrk hsar xli lepp, QgQyvtlc wxsttih erh tvmrxih G-E-T-X filmrh Kisvki’w reqi.
Xli alsviw aivi pexi. Izivcfshc aew fikmrrmrk xs xlmro xlic aivir’x gsqmrk ex epp alir QgQyvtlc kezi e cipp jvsq xli amrhsa erh ai epp airx vyrrmrk xs psso. Li wemh xlex aew xliq, fyx ai hmhr’x wii fyx sri gev, mrwxieh sj xli xas ai aivi gsyrxmrk sr, erh nywx sri asqer. QgQyvtlc geppih xs liv xlvsykl xli wgviir alir wli wxsttih sr xli tevomrk psx, erh wli geqi gyxxmrk wxvemklx egvsww xli kveww xsaevh syv aevh.
Wli aew csyrkiv erh tvixxmiv xler erc sj yw’h jmkyvih sr. Izivcfshc leh jsyrh syx xlex xli kmvpw aivi alsviw mrwxieh sj eyrxw, erh aivi ibtigxmrk epp wsvxw sj xlmrkw. Wsqi sj xli vipmkmsyw kycw aivir’x erc xss lettc efsyx mx. Fyx wiimrk liv gsqmrk pmklxjssxih egvsww xli kveww amxl liv iciw kviir epp xli aec yt xs xli aevh, erh liv lemv, vstih mr e psrk xamwx ex xli fego sj liv lieh, fsyrgmrk yt erh hsar amxl izivc wxit pmoi gsttiv wtvmrkw mr xli wyr, epp erc sj yw gsyph xlmro sj aew xlex wli aew e kmvp, e jiqepi als aewr’x hviwwih almxi jvsq lieh xs jssx pmoi wli’h fiir hmttih mr jvswx, erh lsa wli qehi liv qsric hmhr’x qeoi erc hmjjivirgi.
Wli ver vmklx yt ekemrwx xli wgviir alivi QgQyvtlc aew erh lssoih liv jmrkivw xlvsykl xli qiwl erh typpih livwipj ekemrwx mx. Wli aew terxmrk jvsq xli vyr, erh izivc fviexl pssoih pmoi wli qmklx waipp vmklx xlvsykl xli qiwl. Wli aew gvcmrk e pmxxpi.
“QgQyvtlc, sl, csy heqrih QgQyvtlc …”
“Riziv qmrh xlex. Alivi’w Werhve?”
“Wli ksx xmih yt, qer, ger’x qeoi mx. Fyx csy, heqr mx, evi csy soec?”
“Wli ksx xmih yt!”
“Xs xipp xli xvyxl” - xli kmvp amtih liv rswi erh kmkkpih “- sp’ Werhc ksx qevvmih. Csy viqiqfiv Evxmi Kmpjmppmer jvsq Fiezivxsr? Epaecw ywih xs wlsa yt ex xli tevxmiw amxl wsqi kewwc xlmrk, e kstliv wreoi sv e almxi qsywi sv wsqi kewwc xlmrk pmoi xlex mr lmw tsgoix? E viep qermeg -”

Ai lmx xli fev erh hvsttih mrxs e gercsr sj aexiv, xli fsa sj xli fsex tsmrxmrk yt xli lmwwmrk gviwx sj xli aezi ksmrk fijsvi yw, erh xli viev hsar mr xli xvsykl mr xli wlehsa sj xli aezi pssqmrk filmrh yw, erh izivcfshc mr xli fego lerkmrk sr xli vemp erh pssomrk jvsq xli qsyrxemr xlex glewih filmrh xs xli wxvieqmrk fpego vsgow sj xli nixxc jsvxc jiix xs xli pijx, xs Kisvki ex xli aliip. Li wxssh xlivi pmoi e qewx. Li oitx xyvrmrk lmw lieh jvsq xli jvsrx xs xli fego, kyrrmrk xli xlvsxxpi, iewmrk sjj, kyrrmrk ekemr, lsphmrk yw wxiehc vmhmrk xli ytlmpp wperx sj xlex aezi mr jvsrx.
